śiva māyayā ca sakalam śūnyam yat tat mahā mune brahma rūpam jalam abhūt sparśanāt pāpa nāśanam tadā śrāntaḥ ca puruṣaḥ viṣṇuḥ tasmin jale svayam prītaḥ bahukālam vimohitaḥ nārāyaṇa iti nām api tasya parīkṣāvaḥ agni sambhavam adhas gamiṣyāmi anala stambhasya anupamasya ca parīkṣā artham prajānāthaiḥ tasya vai vāyu vegāt tadā prayatnena gaṃtum arhasi satvaram uvāca evam vyāhṛtya viśvātmā sva rūpam hi abruvan vacanam śubham ūcuḥ nityam sevā tu kasya eva bhagavant kāryā duḥkha apahāriṇī iti etat vacanam śrutvā bhagavant bhakta vatsalaḥ sa amarasya mama prītyā kṛpayā vākyam abravīt śrī bhagavant uvāca brahman śṛṇu suraiḥ samyak śrutam ca bhavatā purā tathā api kathyate tubhyam devebhyaḥ ca tathā punar dṛṣṭam ca dṛśyate adya eva kim punar prastutam ca eva dṛṣṭam vaḥ sarvam dṛṣṭāntam adbhutam tyājyam tat acanam na eva kadāpi sukham īpsubhiḥ saṃtyajya devadeveśam liṅga mūrti maheśvaram eva ete naṣṭāḥ te api sa bāndhavāḥ mayā ca mohitāḥ te vai māyayā dūratas kṛtāḥ sarve vinaṣṭāḥ pradhvastāḥ śivena rahitāḥ yadā tasmāt sadā pūjanīyaḥ liṅga mūrti dharaḥ haraḥ sevanīyaḥ viśeṣeṇa śraddhayā deva sattamaḥ śarva liṅga arcanāt eva devāḥ daityāḥ ca sattamāḥ aham tvam ca sṛ0 khaṃ0 te duḥkhasya bhājanāḥ bhavanāni manojñāni manojña ābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ dhanam ca tuṣṭi paryantam putra pautra ādi saṃtatiḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ śarīram ca pratiṣṭhām ca api alaukikām ye vāṃchanti mahābhāgāḥ sukham vā tridaśālayam ante mukti phalam ca eva bhakti vā parameśituḥ uvāca iti uktāḥ ca tadā devāḥ praṇipatya harim svayam liṅgāni prārthayāmāsuḥ sarva kāma āptaye nṛṇām tat śrutvā ca tadā abravīt ca tat eva kathayāmi adya śrūyatām ṛṣi sattamaiḥ padmarāga mayam śakaḥ hem viśravasaḥ sutaḥ pītam maṇi mayam dharma om varuṇaḥ śyāmalam śivam nīla mayam viṣṇuḥ brahmā hema mayam tathā viśvedevāḥ tathā raupyam vasavaḥ ca tathā eva ca ārakūṭa mayam vā api pārthivam hi aśvinaḥ mune ca tat tat tat tat tathā tathā eva ca mayaḥ nāgāḥ pravāla mayam ādarāt navanīta mayam devī yogī bhasma mayam tathā yakṣā dadhi mayam liṅgam chāyā piṣṭa mayam tathā hi śiva liṅgam ca brahmāṇī ratnam pūjayati dhruvam pāradam pārthivam bāṇaḥ samarcati pare api vā evaṃvidhāni liṅgāni dattāni viśvakarmaṇā pūjayanti sarve vai devāḥ ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tathā viṣṇuḥ dattvā ca liṅgāni devebhyaḥ hita kāmyayā pūjā vidhi samācaṣṭa brahmaṇe me pinākinaḥ tat śrutvā vacanam tasya brahmā aham deva sattamaiḥ āgaccham ca svakam dhām harṣa nirbhara mānasaḥ tatra āgatya ṛṣīn sarvān devaḥ ca aham tathā sune pūjā vidhim samyak anuvam sakala iṣṭa dam mānuṣam janma saṃprāpya durlabham sarva jantuṣu tatra api sat kule devāḥ duṣprāpyam ca muni īśvarāḥ atri aṅgam ca eva vipreṣu sa ācāreṣu su puṇyaiḥ yatas sama rasam sva iṣṭam yogī dhyānena paśyati dhyāna yajña ratasya asya sadā saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ na asti vijñāninām kiṃcid prāyaścitta ādi śodhaiḥ viśuddhāḥ vidyayā ye ca brahman brahma vidaḥ janāḥ na asti kriyā ca teṣām vai sukham duḥkham vicārāt dhyāna vidhiḥ tathā sarvadā nirvikārāḥ te vidyayā ca tayā amarāḥ para ānanda karam liṅgam viśuddham śivam akṣaram niṣkalam sarva gam jñeyam yoginām sthūla liṅga arcane ratāḥ asatām bhāvanā arthāya sūkṣmeṇa sthūla vigrahāḥ ādhyātmikam tu yat ḍiṅgam pratyakṣam yasya no bhavet sa tad ḍiṅge tathā sthūle kalpayet ca naḥ ca anyathā na asti hi sarvasmin tathā na asti vihita avihite tathā na asti vihita avihite tathā yathā jaleṣu kamalam salilaiḥ na avalipyate tathā jñānī gṛhe tiṣṭhan karmaṇā na avabadhyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ jala ādhārāḥ divastubhiḥ dṛśyate śrūyate loke yat yat sat asat ātmakam tat tat sarvam surāḥ vitta param brahma śiva ātmakam yad asmin pratibhāve vicārāt evam āhuḥ tathā ca anye sarve veda artha tattva gāḥ hṛdi saṃsāriṇaḥ sākṣāt sakalaḥ parameśvaraḥ yuktasya kim tasya pratimā ādibhiḥ iti vijñāna hīnasya pratimā kalpanā śubhā padam uccais samāroḍhum puṃsaḥ hi ālambanam smṛtam vinā tasya padam uccais su duṣkaram nirguṇa prāptaye nṛṇām pratimā ālambanam smṛtam smṛtam sa guṇāt nirguṇa prāptiḥ bhavati iti su niścitam devānām pratimā pratyaya āvahā devānām pratimā pratyaya āvahā deva śva ayam mahīyāḥ vai tasya arthe pūjanam tu idam gandha candana puṣpa ādi kimartham pratimām vinā pratimā pūjyā yāvat vijñāna sambhavaḥ jñāna abhāve na pūjyeta patanam tasya niścitam etasmāt kāraṇāt viprāḥ śrūyatām paramārthāt manas sarvaḥ raṅgaḥ prasajjate tathā ca nirmale dehe devānām samyak arcayā jñāna raṅgaḥ prajāyeta tadā vijñāna sambhavaḥ ca sat mūlam bhaktiḥ avyabhicāriṇī jñānasya api ca sat mūlam bhaktiḥ eva abhidhīyate bhaktyāḥ mūlam tu sat karma sva iṣṭa deva ādi pūjanam tad mūlam sat guruḥ śi0pu0 proktaḥ tad mūlam saṃgatiḥ satām jāyate ca tadā nivartate dvaṃdva duḥkha vihīnaḥ tu śiva rūpaḥ bhavati asau dvaṃdva aprāptau na jāyetām sukha duḥkhe vijānataḥ vihita avihite tasya na syātām mahā ca sura ṛṣayaḥ loke gṛha āśrama vivarjitaḥ yadi loke bhavati asmin darśanāt pāpa hārakaḥ tīrthāni ślāghayanti iha tādṛśam jñāna vittamam devāḥ ca munayaḥ sarve para brahma ātmakam śivam tādṛśāṇi na tīrthāni na devāḥ mṛd śilā mayāḥ te punaṃti uru yālena vijñānī darśanāt api kālena vijñānī darśanāt api yāvat vaha āśrame tiṣṭhet tāvat ākāra pūjanam kuryāt śreṣṭasya su prītyā sureṣu khalu pañcasu pūjyaḥ mūlam ekam viśiṣyate male sikke tathā śākhāḥ tṛptāḥ santi akhilāḥ surāḥ śākhāsu ca su tṛptāsu mūlam tṛptam na karhicit tṛpteṣu sureṣu muni sattamāḥ tṛpteṣu sureṣu muni sattamāḥ sarvathā śiva tṛptiḥ na om vijñeyā sukṣma buddhibhiḥ śive ca pūjite devāḥ pūjitāḥ sarve eva hi tasmāt ca pūjaye devam śaṃkaram loka śaṃkaram sarva kāma phala avāptaye sarva bhūta hite rataḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām prathama khaṇḍe bhū ākhyāne pūjā vidhi varṇane sārāsāravicāravarṇanaḥ nāma dvadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ brāhme muhūrte ca utthāya saṃsmaret sa ambakam śivam brāhme muhūrte ca utthāya saṃsmaret sa ambakam śivam kuryāt tad prārthanām bhaktyā sa añjaliḥ nata mastakaḥ hṛdayeśaya deveśaḥ uttiṣṭha hṛdayeśaya uttiṣṭha tvam umāsvāmin brahmāṇḍe maṅgalam kuru jānāmi dharmaiḥ na ca mama pravṛttiḥ jānāmi adharme na ca mama nivṛttiḥ mahādevaiḥ hṛdi sthitena yathā niyuktaḥ asmi tathā karomi iti uktvā vacanam bhaktyā smṛtvā ca guru pāduke bahis gacchet dakṣiṇa āśām tyāga artham malaiḥ mūtrayoḥ tatas kṛtvā saḥ mṛd jala viśodhanaiḥ ca prakṣālya dantadhāvanam ācaret divānāthe tu anudite kṛtvā vai danta dhāvanam ācaret mukham ṣoḍaśa vāram tu prakṣālya añjalibhiḥ tathā mukham ṣoḍaśa vāram tu prakṣālya añjalibhiḥ tathā ṣaṣṭyāt yamāḥ ca tithayaḥ navamī arka dine tathā varjyāḥ sura ṛṣayaḥ yatnāt bhaktena mahādāne tathā tīrthe lapavāsa dine tathā aśauce ipi athavā prāpte na snāyāt uṣṇa vāriṇā yathā sa abhimukham snāyāt tīrtha ādau bhaktimān naraḥ taila abhyaṅgam ca kurvīta vārān dṛṣṭvā krameṇa ca nityam abhyaṅgake ca eva vāsitam vā na dūṣitam śrāddhe ca grahaṇe ca eva upavāse pratipad dine sārṣapam tailam na duṣye grahaṇam vinā deśam kālam vicāyya evam snānam kuryāt yathāvidhi uttara abhimukhaḥ ca eva prāc mukhaḥ api athavā punar snānam tathā kārye kṣālitam ca parityajet tarpaṇam ca tatas kāryam deva ṛṣi pitṛ tṛpti dam dhīta vastram tatas dhāryam punar ācamanam caret tatas gatvā gomaya ādi upamārjite āsanam ca śubham tatra racanīyam dvijottamāḥ śuddha kāṣṭha samutpannam staritam eva vā dānam tripuṇḍrān saphalam bhavet āsthāya vai punar tad anujñām avāpya ca saṃkalpam vidhivat kṛtvā kāmanām ca niyujya vai pūjayet parayā bhaktvā śivam sa parivārakam mudrām ekām pradarśay mā enam tadā devaiḥ bhrātrā ca eva samanvitam pūjayet parayā bhaktyā namaskuryāt punar punar dvārapālam sadā dvāri ca mahodaram pūjayitvā tatas paścāt pūjaye girijām satīm candanaiḥ kuṅkumaiḥ ca eva dhūpaiḥ dīpaiḥ anekaśas naivedyaiḥ virvidhaiḥ ca eva pūjayitvā tatas śivam namaskṛtya punar tatra gacchet ca śiva saṃnidhau yadi gehe pārthivām vā haimām vā rājatām tathā dhātu janyām tathā eva anyām pāradām vā prakalpay tat punar tām ca pūjayet bhakti tatparaḥ namaskṛtya punar tām ca pūjayet bhakti tatparaḥ tasyām tu pūjitāyām vai sarvam syuḥ pūjitāḥ tadā sthāpayet ca mṛdā liṅgam vidhāya vidhi bhū tatra sthā sthā sthā mūlamantra abhiyogāt śivālaye gṛhe śivaḥ sadā pūjyaḥ mūlamantra abhiyogāt tatra tu dvārapālānām niyamaḥ na asti sarvathā gṛhe liṅgam ca yat pūjyam tasmin sarve pratiṣṭhitam pūjā kāle ca sa aṅgam vai parivāreṇa saṃyutam āvāhya pūjayet devam niyamaḥ atra na vidyate śi0pu0 parikalpayet caret caret prakṣālya hastau paścāt vai prāṇāyāmam prakalpayet tatra eva daśa āvartam nayet naraḥ pañcamudrāḥ prakartavyāḥ pūjā vaśyam kara īpsitāḥ tatas ca vāruṇam snānam karaṇīyam śivāya vai sugandham candanam dadyāt anya lepāni yatnatas sa sugandha jalena eva jala dhārām prakalpayet veda mantraiḥ ṣaḍaṅgaiḥ vā nāmbhiḥ rudra saṃkhyayā yathāvakāśam tām da tvā vastreṇa mārjayet tatas paścāt ācamanam dadyāt tatas vastram samarpayet tilāḥ ca eva javāḥ vā api godhūmāḥ mudga māṣakāḥ arpaṇīyāḥ śivāya evam mantraiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ api tatas puṣpāṇi deyāni pañcāsyāya mahātmane ca tatas ācamanam prītyā kārayet vā vilambataḥ tatas ācamanam prītyā kārayet vā vilambataḥ tatas śivāya tāmbūlam sa aṅga upāṅgam vidhāya ca pādayoḥ ca catur vāram dvis kṛtvas nābhi maṇḍale eka kṛtve sukhe sapta kṛtvas sarva aṅge eva hi tatas vyānam yathoktam vai kṛtvā mantram udīrayet yathājñānam kuryāt mantra vidhin naraḥ guru upadiṣṭa mārgeṇa kṛtvā mantra japam sudhīḥ guru upadiṣṭa mārgeṇa kṛtvā mantra japam sudhīḥ stotraiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ prītyā stuvīta vṛṣabhadhvajam tatas pradakṣiṇām kuryāt śivasya ca śanais śanais mayā sṛḍa iti vijñāya gaurīśaiḥ bhūtanāthaiḥ prasīda mama bhūmau skhalita pādānām bhūmiḥ eva avalambanam tvayi jāta aparādhānām tvam eva śaraṇam prabho ityādi bahu vijñaptim kṛtvā samyak vidhānāt puṣpa añjali samapya eva punar kuryāt na ti muhur sva sthānam gaccha deveśaiḥ parivāra yutaḥ prabho pūjā kāle punar nāthaiḥ tvayā gantavyam ādarāt iti ūcuḥ vyāsa śiṣyaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ kathaya tvam pramāṇāt kaiḥ puṣpaiḥ pūjitaḥ śaṃsuḥ kim kim yacchati vai phalam śaunaka ādyāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ śṛṇuta ādarāt akhilam kathayāmi adya su prītyā puṣpa arpaṇa vinirṇayam eṣaḥ eva vidhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ nāradena mahā ṛṣiṇā provāca lakṣa saṃkhyākaiḥ pūjitaḥ ced bhavet śivaḥ pāpa hāniḥ tathā vipraiḥ lakṣmī syāt na atra saṃśayaḥ viṃśatiḥ kamalānām tu prastham ekam mudā bilvaḥ dala sahasreṇa prastha ardha paribhāṣitam bilvaḥ dala sahasreṇa prastha ardha paribhāṣitam śata pattra sahasreṇa prastha ardha paribhāṣitam palaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ prasthaḥ palam smṛtaḥ tu mānena tulām āropayet yadā sarvān kāmān avāpnoti niṣkāmaḥ ced śivaḥ bhavet rājyasya kāmukaḥ yaḥ vai pārthivānām ca pūjayā toṣayet śaṃkaram devam daśa koṭyā muni īśvarāḥ liṅgam śivam tathā puṣpam akhaṇḍam taṇḍulam tathā candanena eva jala dhārām tathā punar mantram bilvī dalam anuttamam athavā śatapattram ca kamalam vā tathā punar śaṅkha puṣpaiḥ tathā proktam viśeṣeṇa purātanaiḥ sarva kāma phalam divyam paratra iha api sarvathā dhūpam dīpam ca naivedya marṣam ca ārārtikam tathā pradakṣiṇām namaskāram kṣamāpana visarjane kṛtvā sa aṅga tathā bhojyam kṛtam yena bhave māraṇe vai tu mohane tu tad ardhāt sāmantānām jaye ca eva koṭi pūjā praśasyate rājñām ayuta saṃkhyam ca vaśīkaraṇa karmaṇi yaśase ca tathā saṃkhyā vāhana ādyaiḥ sahasrikā mukti kāma urcayet śambhum pañca koṭyā su bhaktyāḥ jñāna arthī pūjayet koṭayā śaṃkaram loka śaṃkaram śiva darśana kāmaḥ vai tad ardhena prapūjayet tathā mṛtyuṃjayaiḥ jāpyaḥ kāmanā phala rūpāt pañca lakṣāḥ japāḥ pratyakṣam tu bhavet śivaḥ tṛtīye kāmanā lābhaḥ caturthe tam prapaśyati ca yadā lakṣam phalam yacchati asaṃśayam eva tu bhavet yukti kāmaḥ bhavet yaḥ vai darbhaiḥ ca pūjanam caret lakṣa saṃkhyā tu sarvatra jñātavyā ṛṣi sattam āyuḥ kāmaḥ bhavet yaḥ vai dūrvābhiḥ pūjanam caret tulasyā pūjayet yadi arka puṣpaiḥ pratāpaḥ ca kubja kalhārakaiḥ tathā japā kusuma pūjā tu śatrūṇām mṛtyu dā smṛtā bandhukaiḥ bhūṣaṇa avāptiḥ jātyā vāhāt na saṃśayaḥ atasī puṣpakaiḥ devam viṣṇu vallabha tām iyāt śamī pattraiḥ tathā muktiḥ prāpyate puruṣeṇa ca mallikā kusumaiḥ dattaiḥ striyam śubhatarām śivaḥ yūthikā kusumaiḥ śasyaiḥ gṛha na eva vimucyate tathā vastra sampattiḥ jāyate nṝṇām nirguṇḍī kusumaiḥ loṇe nirmala tām vrajet bilva pattraiḥ tathā lakṣaiḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt bhṛṅgāra hāra puṣpaiḥ tu vardhate sukha saṃpadā ṛtu jātāni puṣpāṇi mukti dāni na saṃśayaḥ rājikā kusumāni iha śatrūṇām mṛtyu dāni ca param ca dhānyānām pūjane śaṃkarasya ca pramāṇam ca phalam sarvam prītyā śṛṇu ca sattamaiḥ taṇḍula āropaṇa nṛṇām lakṣmī vṛddhiḥ prajan bhavet bhavet ca hi āditya saṃkhyayā tatra brāhmaṇān bhojayet tatas lakṣa pūjā tathā jātā sa aṅgam ca mantra pūrvakam śatam aṣṭa uttaram tatra mantre vidhiḥ udāhṛtaḥ nāśanam ca palam lakṣam mahāpātaka nāśanam ekādaśa palaiḥ eva lakṣa mānam udāhṛtam pūrvavat pūjanam tatra kartavyam hita kāmyayā bhojyāḥ vai brāhmaṇāḥ mahāpātaka jam duḥkham tasmāt atra kāryā nareṇa hi mahāpātaka jam duḥkham tad kṣaṇāt naśyati dhruvam yava pūjā tathā proktā lakṣaṇa paramā śive prasthānām aṣṭakam ca eva tathā prastha ardhakam punar pala dvaya yutam tatra mānam etat purātanam yava pūjā ca munibhiḥ svarga saukhya vivardhinī brāhmaṇānām bhavyam ca phala īpsubhiḥ godhūma annaiḥ tathā pūjā praśastā śaṃkarasya vai saṃtatiḥ vardhate tasya yadi lakṣa avadhiḥ kṛtā brāhmaṇāḥ ca tathā bhojyāḥ rudra saṃkhyā pramāṇāt priyaṅgu pūjanāt eva dharma adhyakṣe parātmani dharma artha kāmāḥ vardhante pūjā sarva sukha āvahā prastha ekena ca tasya uktam lakṣam ekam purātanaiḥ brahmabhojam tathā proktam arka saṃkhyā pramāṇāt rājikā pūjanam śambhoḥ śatroḥ mṛtyu karam smṛtam sārṣapāṇām tathā lakṣam palaiḥ viṃśati saṃkhyayā teṣām ca pūjanāt eva śatroḥ mṛtyuḥ udāhṛtaḥ āḍhakīnām dalaiḥ ca eva śobhayitvā ācayet śivam ca pradātavyā tathā eva ca sukha karā hi eṣā pūjā sarva phala pradā prasthānām ca tathā ca ekam śaṅkhapuṣpa samudbhavam proktam vyāsena lakṣam hi sūkṣma māna pradarśiṇā prasthaiḥ ekādaśaiḥ jāti lakṣa mānam prakīrtitam tathā mānam rājikāyāḥ tad ardhakam prasthaiḥ viṃśatikaiḥ ca eva mallikā mānam uttamam tila puṣpaiḥ tathā mānam prasthāt nyūnam tathā eva ca tatas ca dviguṇam mānam karavīra bhave smṛtam nirguṇḍī kusume mānam tathā eva kathitam budhaiḥ karṇikāre tathā mānam śirīṣa kusume punar tathā mānam prasthānam daśakena ca ityādyaiḥ vividhaiḥ mānam dṛṣṭvā kuryāt śiva arcanam sarva kāma samṛdhi artham mukti arthaiḥ kāmanā ujjhitaḥ tam param pravakṣyāmi dhārā pūjā phalam mahat yasya śravaṇa mātreṇa kalyāṇam jāyate nṛṇām vidhāna pūrvakam pūjām kṛtvā bhaktyā śivasya vai jala dhārā hi kartavyā bhakti tatparaiḥ jala dhārā hi kartavyā bhakti tatparaiḥ jvara pralāpa śānti arthaiḥ jala dhārā śubha āvahā śatarudriya mantreṇa rudrasya ekādaśena tu rudra jāpyena vā tatra sūktena pauruṣeṇa vā ṣaḍaṅgena atha vā tatra mahā mṛtyuṃjayena ca gāyatryā vā namaḥ oṃ taiḥ śva nāmabhiḥ praṇava ādibhiḥ mantraiḥ vā atha āgama uktaiḥ jala dhārā ādikam tathā dhārā ādikam tathā sukha saṃtāna vṛdhi arthe dhārā pūjanam uttamam nānā dravyaiḥ śubheḥ divyaiḥ prītyā sat bhasma dhāriṇā ghṛta dhārā śive kāryā yāvat mantra sahasrakam tadā vaṃśasya vistāraḥ jāyate na atra saṃśayaḥ evam mad ukta mantreṇa kārya vai śiva pūjanam brahma bhojyam tathā proktam prājāpatyam saṃjāyate xchā jīva sadṛśā buddhiḥ uttamā yāvat mantra ayutam na syāt tāvat dhārā prapūjanam yadā ca uñcāṭanam dehe jāyate kāraṇam vinā kutra api vā prem duḥkham ca pari vardhitam sva gṛhe kalahaḥ nityam yadā ca eva prajāyate tad dhārāyām kṛtāyām vai sarva vilīyate dhārā ca ikṣu rasasya api sarva ānanda karā śive dhārā ca ikṣu rasasya api sarva ānanda karā śive dhārā gaṅgā jalasya eva bhukti mukti phala pradā etāḥ sarvāḥ ca yāḥ proktāḥ mṛtyuṃjaya samudbhavāḥ tatra ayuta pramāṇam hi kartavyam tad vidhānāt kartavyam brāhmaṇānām ca bhojyam vai rudra saṃkhyayā etat te sarvam ākhyātam yat pṛṣṭaḥ aham munī tatas bhukta akhilam saukhyam putra pautra ādibhiḥ śubham tatas yāti maheśasya lokam sarva sukha āvaham sūrya koṭi pratīkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ sarvakā hari kanyā samākīrṇa iyavādya samanvitaiḥ rudra kanyā samākīrṇa iyavādya samanvitaiḥ krīḍate śiva bhūtaḥ ca yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam tatas mokṣam avāpnoti vijñānam prāpya tat ca avyayam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe prathama khaṇḍe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām sṛṣṭayupākhyāne śivapūjāvidhānavarṇanaḥ nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ dhanyaḥ tvam sura sattamaiḥ śrāvitā adya adbhutā śaiva kathā parama pāvanā utpattiḥ śrutā śubhā śrutvā yasyāḥ prabhāvam ca duḥkha nāśaḥ bhavet iha anantaram ca yat jātam māhātmyam caritam tathā sṛṭyāḥ ca eva prakāram ca kathaya uvāca samyaka pṛṣṭam ca bhavatā yat jātam tat anantaram kathayiṣyāmi saṃkṣepāt yathā pūrvam śrutam mayā antarhite tadā deve mama viṣṇuḥ ca vipra indra adhikam sukham āptavan mayā ca viṣṇunā rūpam haṃsa vārāhayoḥ tadā yaḥ rūpam yuvābhyām ca dhṛtam katham anyat rūpam vihāya eva kim atra vada kāraṇam sūtaḥ uvāca iti etat vacanam śrutvā nāradasya mahātmanaḥ vivecayati vivecayati na eva labdhaḥ ca yatas mayā haṃsa rūpiṇā gamane adhas varāhasya gatiḥ bhavati niścalā dhṛtam vārāha rūpam hi viṣṇunā vana cāriṇām athavā bhava kalpa artham tat rūpam hi prakalpitam viṣṇunā ca varāhasya bhuvana avana kāriṇā yat dinam hi samārabhya tad rūpam dhṛtavan hariḥ tad dinam prati kalpaḥ asau kalpaḥ vārā tad icchā vā yadā jātā ca ābhyām rūpam hi dhāraṇe tad dinam pratikalpaḥ asau kalpaḥ vārāha saṃjñakaḥ iti praśna uttaram dattam prastutam nāradaiḥ smṛtvā śivapada abhojam vakṣye sṛṣṭi vidhim mune antarhite mahādeve tu aham lokapitāmahaḥ tadīyam vacanam kartum adhyāyan dhyāna tatparaḥ namaskṛtya tadā śambhum jñānam prāpya hareḥ tadā ānandam paramam gatvā sṛṣṭim kartum manaḥ dadhe viṣṇuḥ ca api tadā tatra praṇipatyam sadāśi upadiśya ca mām tātaiḥ hi antardhānam upāgataḥ brahmāṇḍāt ca bahis gatvā prāpya śambhoḥ anugraham vaikuṇṭha nagaram gatvā tatra uvāsa hariḥ sadā aham smṛtvā śivam tatra viṣṇum vai sṛṣṭi kāmyayā pūrva sṛṣṭam jalam yat ca tatra añjalim udākṣipam atas aṇḍam abhavat tatra caturviṃśati saṃkhyā mahā rūpam abhūt vipraiḥ jala rūpam apaśyataḥ tatas saṃśayam āpannaḥ tapaḥ tepe su dāruṇam dvādaśa abdam aham tatra viṣṇu dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ mām uvāca mahā prītyā mad aṅgam saṃspṛśan mudā mām uvāca mahā prītyā mad aṅgam saṃspṛśan mudā mama adya dehi viṣṇo namaḥ astu te virā rūpam idam jhaṇḍam caturviṃśati para sādhakaḥ ca brahmanaḥ parikīrtitāḥ tatra ādyaḥ mahantaḥ sargaḥ om dvitīyaḥ sūkṣmabhautikaḥ vaikārikaḥ tṛtīyaḥ ca iti ete prākṛtāḥ trayaḥ evam ca aṣṭavidhāḥ sargāḥ prākṛteḥ vaikṛtaiḥ saha kaumāraḥ navamaḥ proktaḥ prākṛtaḥ vaikṛtaḥ ca saḥ eṣām avāntaraḥ bhedaḥ mayā vaktum na śakyate alpa tvāt upayogasya vacmi dvija ātmakam kaumāraḥ sanaka ādīnām yatra mahān abhūt sanaka ādyāḥ sutāḥ mama hi tvayā ca śaśimaulinaḥ adbhutā kathitā līlā tvayā ca śaśimaulinaḥ gṛhīta dāre madane hṛṣṭe hi sva gṛham gate dakṣe ca sva gṛham yāte tathā hi tvayi karttri mānaseṣu ca putreṣu gateṣu sva sva dhāmsu saṃdhyā kutra gatā sā ca brahmaputrī pitṛprasūḥ kim cakāra ca kena eva puruṣeṇa vivāhitā yad viśeṣeṇa saṃdhyāyāḥ caritam vada dhīmataḥ saṃsmṛtya śaṃkaram bhaktyā brahmā provāca saṃ0 ca saṃdhyā sutā me hi manas jātā purā abhavat tapaḥ taptvā tanum tyaktvā sā eva jātā tu arundhatī medhātitheḥ sutā bhūtvā suni śreṣṭhasya dhīmatī brahma viṣṇu maheśāna vacanāt carita vratā vatre patim mahātmānam vasiṣṭham śaṃsita vratam pativratā ca mukhyā abhūt vandyā pūjyā tu abhīṣaṇā uvāca tayā tapaḥ taptam kimartham kutra saṃdhyayā katham śarīram sā tyaktvā abhavan medhātitheḥ sutāḥ katham vā vihitam devaiḥ brahma viṣṇu śivaiḥ patim mahātmānam śaṃsita vratam brūhi saṃdhyām dṛṣṭvā pūrvam atha ātmanaḥ kāmāya āśu manaḥ akārṣe tyaktā śiva bhayāt ca sā saṃruddha mānasānām mahātmanām bhargasya vacanam śrutvā sa upahāsam ca mām prati ātmanaḥ calita tvam vai hi amaryādam ṛṣīn prati kāmasya tādṛśam bhāvam muni moha karam su duḥ dṛṣṭvā saṃdhyā svayam tatra upayamāya ati duḥkhitā tatas tu brahmanā śapte madane ca mayā mune mayi hi śive gate ca api nija āspade manasvinī idam saṃdhyā tasmin kāle yathocitam uvāca utpanna mātrām mām dṛṣṭvā yuvatīm madana īritaḥ akārṣīt sa anurāgaḥ yam abhilāṣam pitā mama paśyatām mānasānām ca munīnām bhāvitātmanām dṛṣṭvā eva mām amaryādam sa kāmam abhavat manaḥ mama api mathitam cittam madanena durātmanā yena dṛṣṭvā munīn sarvān calitam mad manaḥ bhṛśam phalam etasya pāpasya madanaḥ svayam āptavan tam maśāpa kupitaḥ śambhoḥ pitāmahaḥ śaśāpa kupitaḥ śambhoḥ a pitāmahaḥ prāpnuyām phalam etasya pāpasya svagha kāriṇī tad śodhana phalam aham āśu ca icchāmi sādhanam mām mama api kāma bhāvaḥ bhūt amaryādam samīkṣya tān patyāḥ iva svake tāte sarveṣu sahajeṣu api kariṣyāmi asya pāpasya prāyaścittam aham svayam ātmānam agnau hoṣyāmi veda mārga anusārāt aham tu ekām sthāpayiṣyāmi maryādām iha bhū tale utpanna mātrāḥ na yathā sa kāmāḥ syuḥ śarīriṇaḥ etad artham aham kṛtvā tapaḥ paramaiḥ maryādām sthāpayiṣyāmi paścāt tyakṣāmi jīvitam yasmin śarīre pitrā mama hi abhilāṣaḥ svayam kṛtaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ tena kāyena kiṃcid na asti prayojanam mayā yena śarīreṇa tāteṣu saha ijeṣu ca udbhāvitaḥ kāma bhāvaḥ na tat sukṛta sādhanam śi0pu0 manasā saṃdhyā śaila varam tatas jagāma candrabhāga ākhyam candra bhāga āpagā yatas atha tatra gatām jñātvā saṃdhyām giri varam prati niyata ātmānam brahma avocam aham sutam vasiṣṭham saṃyata ātmānam sarvajñam jñāna yoginam samīpe sve samāsīnam veda vedāṅga pāragam uvāca vasiṣṭha putraiḥ gaccha tvam saṃdhyām jātām manasvinīm tapase dhṛta kāmām ca dīkṣasva enām yathāvidhi purā dṛṣṭā eva kāmukān vaḥ mām ca tathā ātmānam sa kāmām muni sattamaiḥ anukta mūrta tat karma pūrva mṛtyum vimṛśya sā vaḥ ātmanaḥ ca api prāṇān saṃtyatum icchati samaya deṣu maryādām tapasā sthāpayiṣyati tapaḥ kartum gatā sādhvī candrabhāga ākhya bhūdhare na bhāvam tapasaḥ tātaiḥ tasmāt sā anujānāti kaṃcana tasmāt yathā upadeśāt sā prāpnotu iṣṭam tathā kuru idam rūpam parityajya nijam rūpa antaram mune parigṛhya antika tasyāḥ tapa mahā aśvaryā nidarśayan idam sva rūpam bhavataḥ dṛṣṭvā pūrvaiḥ yathā atra vām na āpnuyāt sā atha kiṃcid vai tatas rūpa antaram kuru mama samājñaptaḥ dayāvatā yathā stu iti ca mām procya yayau saṃdhyā antikam muniḥ saṃdhyām tad tīra gām api saṃdhyām tad tīra gām api tīra sthayā tayā reje tat saraḥ kamala ujvalam udyat indu su nakṣatram pradoṣe gaganam yathā muniḥ dṛṣṭvā atha tām tatra susaṃbhāvām sa kautukī vīkṣāṃcakre saraḥ tatra bṛhalohita saṃjñakam candrabhāgā nadī tasmāt prākārāt dakṣiṇa ambudhim yānt sā ca eva dadṛśe tena bhāgebṛhat hohita tīra gām saṃdhyām dṛṣṭvā atha papraccha vasiṣṭhaḥ sa ādaram tadā uvāca kimartham āgatā bhadre nirjanam tvam mahīdharam vā tanayā kim vā bhavatyā api cikīrṣitam icchāmi śrotum vada guhyam na ced bhavet vadanam pūrṇa candra ābham niśceṣṭam vā katham te vāca tat śrutvā vacanam tasya vasiṣṭhasya mahātmānaḥ dṛṣṭvā ca tam mahātmānam jvalantam iva pāvakam setsyati vāti bho tapaḥ cartum aham brahma nirjanam śailam āgatā brahmanā ūham sutā jātā nānā saṃdhyā iti viśrutā yadi te sam mām samupadeśaya etat cikīrṣitam guhyam na anyaiḥ kim ca na vidyate a jñātvā tapasaḥ bhāvam tapas vanam upāśritā cintayā pariśuṣya iham vepate hi manaḥ mama uvāca ākarṇya tasyāḥ vacanam vasiṣṭhaḥ brahma vittamaḥ svayam ca sarva kṛtya jñaḥ na anyat kiṃcana pṛṣṭa uvāca tapasā iti dhṛta udyamām atha tām niyata ātmānam tapasā iti dhṛta udyamām provāca manasā smṛtvā śaṃkaram bhakta vatsalam paramam yaḥ mahat tejaḥ paramam yaḥ mahat tapaḥ paramaḥ parama ārādhyaḥ śambhuḥ manasi dhāryatām dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām yaḥ ekaḥ tu ādikāraṇam tam ekam jagantām ādyam bhajasva puruṣottamam mantreṇa anena deveśam śambhum bhaja śubha ānane tena te sakala avāpti mauna tapasya a prārambham bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ bhavet maunena hara pūjanam bhavet bhavet tam tvad uddiśya kāmam ciṃtaya śaṃkaram saḥ te praśannaḥ iṣṭa artham acirāt eva dāsyati upaviśya vasiṣṭhaḥ utha saṃdhyāyai tapasaḥ kriyām tām ābhāṣya yathānyāyam tatra eva antardadhe muniḥ mahā varṇanaḥ nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śru saṃdhyā tapaḥ mahat tapas bhāvam vasiṣṭhe sva gṛham gate saṃdhyā api tapasaḥ bhāvam jñātvā modam avāpa ha tatas sa ānanda manasaḥ veṣam kṛtvā tu yā āha mahat hohita tīra gā tapaḥ cartum samārebhe bṛhaddhohita tīra gā yathoktam tu vasiṣṭhena mantram tapasi sādhanam mantreṇa tena saṃgattyā pūjayāmāsa śaṃkaram tathā ākāśe darśayitvā nijam vapuḥ darśayitvā nijam vapuḥ yat rūpam citayatī sā tena pratyakṣatām gataḥ atha sā puratas dṛṣṭvā manasā cititam prabhum vadanam mumoda atīva śaṃkaram sa sādhvasam aham vakṣye kim katham staumi vā haram iti cintā parā bhūtvā nyamīlayata cakṣuṣī akṣyā haraḥ divyam jñānam dadau tasyai vācam divye ca cakṣuṣī divya jñānam divya cakṣuḥ divyām vācam avāpā pratyakṣam vīkṣya durgeśam tuṣṭāva jagantām patim na api sūkṣmam na ca uccam antar cityam yogibhiḥ tasya rūpam tasmai te loka kartre namaḥ astu jñāna agamyam sva prakāśe avikāram kha adhva prakhyam dhvānta mārgāt parastāt rūpam yasya tvām namāmi prasannam ekam śuddham dīpyamānam vinājām cidānanda sahajam ca avikāri nitya ānanda satya bhūti prasannam yasya śrī dam rūpam asmai namaḥ te vidyā kāra udbhāvanīyam prabhinnam sattva chanda dhyeyaiḥ sāram pāram pāvanānām pavitram tasmai rūpam yasya ca evam namaḥ te yat tu ākāram śuddha rūpam manojñam ratna ākalpam svaccha karpūra gauram bhūta abhītī śūla muṇḍa dadhānam hastaiḥ namaḥ yoga yuktāya te gaganam bhū diśaḥ ca eva salilam jyotiḥ eva ca punar kālaḥ ca rūpāṇi yasya te namaḥ astu te mad kurute sthitim saṃhariṣyati yaḥ rudraḥ tasmai te namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ kāraṇa kāraṇāya divya amṛta jñāna vibhūti dāya samasta loka antara bhūti dāya prakāśa rūpāya parātparāya yasya aparam naḥ jagant ucyate padāta kṣitiḥ diśaḥ sūryaḥ induḥ manojaḥ barhi mukhāḥ nābhitas ca antarikṣam tasmai te śambhave mama astu tvam paraḥ paramātmā ca tvam vidyā vividhā haraḥ sa ca param brahma vicāraṇa parāyaṇaḥ yasya na ādiḥ na madhyam ca na antam asti yatas katham stoṣyāmi tam devam vāc manas gocaram haram yasya brahma ādayaḥ sunayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ na rūpāṇi varṇanīyaḥ mama katham sa me striyāḥ mayā te kim jñeyāḥ nirguṇasya guṇāḥ prabho na eva jānanti yad rūpam sa indrāḥ api sura asurāḥ namaḥ te maheśānaiḥ taraḥ ca abhūt śaṃkaraḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ atha tasyāḥ śarīram tu valkala añjina saṃyutam jaṭā vātaiḥ pavitre mūrdhani rājitaiḥ tarjitām bhoja sadṛśam vadanam tadā nirīkṣya kṛpayā āviṣṭaḥ haraḥ provāca tām idam uvāca prītaḥ asmi tapasā bhadre bhavatyāḥ para yadi devaḥ varaḥ prītyā vara yogyā asmi aham yadi yadi śuddhā asmi aham jātā tasmāt pāpāt maheśvaraiḥ yadi na eva sa kāmāḥ saṃbhavantu vaiṃ yadi lokeṣu triṣu api prathitā yathā aviṣyāmi tathā na anyā varaḥ ekaḥ vṛtaḥ mayā sa kāmā mama saṃ0 tadā saḥ ca kkībaḥ bhaviṣyati uvāca iti śrutvā vacaḥ tasyāḥ śaṃkaraḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca su prasanna ātmā niṣpāpāyāḥ tayā īrite uvāca śṛṇu devi ca saṃdhye tvam tvad pāpam bhasma tām gatam tvayi tyaktaḥ mayā krodhaḥ śuddhā jātā tapas karāt yat yat vṛtam tvayā bhadre tat akhilam mayā dattam tat akhilam mayā su prasannena tapasā te saṃdhye vareṇa hi prathamam śaiśavaḥ bhāvaḥ kaumāra ākhyaḥ dvitīyakaḥ tṛtīyaḥ yauvanaḥ bhāvaḥ catuthaḥ ūm vārddha tṛtīye tu atha saṃprāpte vayas bhāge śarīriṇaḥ sa kāmāḥ syuḥ dvitīya antaḥ bhaviṣyati kvacid kvacid mayā utpanna mātrāḥ na yathā sa kāmāḥ syuḥ śarīriṇaḥ tvam ca loke satī bhāvam tādṛśam samavāpnuhi triṣu lokeṣu na anyasyāḥ yādṛśam yaḥ paśyati sa kāmaḥ tvām pāṇigrāham ṛte tava saḥ sadyas kkība tām prāpya durbala tvam gamiṣyati tapas rūpa samanvitaḥ sapta kalpa anta jīvī ca bhaviṣyati saha tvayā iti te ye varāḥ mattaḥ prārthitāḥ te kṛtāḥ mayā anyat ca te vadiṣyāmi pūrva hi janmani saṃsthitam agnau śarīra tyāgaḥ te pūrvam eva pratiśrutaḥ tad upāyam vadāmi tvā tat kuruṣva na saṃśayaḥ sa ca medhātithiḥ yajñe mune bhāga dvādaśa vārṣike kṛtsna prajvalite vahnau acirāt kriyatām tvayā etad śaila upatyakāyām candrabhāgā nadī taṭe medhātithiḥ mahā yajñam kurute āśrame tatra gatvā svayam chaṃṃ muniḥ bhinna upalakṣitā mad prasādāt vahni jātā tasya putrī bhaviṣyati yaḥ te varaḥ vāñchanīyaḥ tu kṛte yuge vyatīte tu kṛte yuge tretāyāḥ prathame bhāge jātāḥ dakṣasya kanyakāḥ vāc pāś śīla samāpannāḥ yathāyogyam vivāhitāḥ sa dadau kanyāḥ vidhave saptaviṃśati candraḥ anyāḥ saṃparityajya rohiṇyām prītimān abhūt tad hetoḥ hai yadā candraḥ śaptaḥ dakṣeṇa kopinā tadā bhavatyāḥ nikaṭe sarve devāḥ samāgatāḥ na dṛṣṭāḥ ca tvayā saṃdhye te devāḥ brahmaṇā saha mayi vinyasta manasā kham ca dṛṣṭvā labhet punar candrasya śāpa mokṣa artham jātā candranadī tadā sṛṣṭā dhātrā tat eva atra medhātithiḥ upasthitaḥ tapasā tad samoḥ na asti na bhūtaḥ na bhaviṣyati iti śrī varṇā bhūtvā ruṣā mune upadiṣṭā tapaḥ cartu vacanāt parameṣṭhinaḥ tam eva kṛtvā manasā tapa mahā īścarya upadeśakam pati tvena tadā saṃdhyā brāhmaṇam brahmacāriṇam samidh henau mahā yajñe dṛṣṭā śambhu prasādena sā viveśa vidhe tasyāḥ puroḍāśa mayam śarīram tad kṣaṇāt tatas dagdham puroḍāśa gandham tastāra yat alakṣitam maṇḍalam śuddham praveśayāmāsa śambhoḥ eva ājñayā punar sūryaḥ vyartham vibhajya atha tat śarīram tadā rathe sva keśam sthāpayāmāsa prītaye pitṛ devayoḥ tad ūrdhva bhāgaḥ tasyāḥ tu śarīrasya muni īśvaraiḥ prātar saṃdhyā bhavat sā tu ahar rātra ādi madhya gā tad śeṣa bhāgaḥ tasyāḥ tu ahar rātra anta madhya tad sāyam abhavat saṃdhyā pitṛ prīti pradā sadā sā sāyam abhavat saṃdhyā pitṛ prīti pradā sadā sūrya udayāt tu prathamam yadā syāt aruṇa udayaḥ prātassaṃdhyā tadā udi devānām prīti kārin tam gate tatas sūyye śoṇi padma nibhe sadā udeti sāyaṃsaṃdhyā api pitṝṇām moda kāriṇī tasyāḥ prāṇāḥ tu manasā śambhunā atha dayālu muneḥ yajña avasāne tu śarīreṇa cakrire hi śarīriṇaḥ muneḥ yajña avasāne tu saṃprāpte muninā tu sā prāptā putrī vahni madhye tapta kāñcana su prabhā tām jagrāha tadā putrīm muniḥ āmoda saṃyutaḥ yajña artham tām tu saṃkhāpya nija koḍe mune atha sā vavṛdhe devī tasmin muni vara āśrame candrabhāgā nadī tīre tāpasāraṇya saṃjñake candrabhāgā nadī tīre tāpasāraṇya saṃjñake mahoḍham api sā pavitram akarot satī vivāham kārayāmāsuḥ tasyāḥ brahma sutena vai vasiṣṭhena hi arundhatyā brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ tad vivāhe mahoḥ babhūva sukha vardhanaḥ sarve surāḥ ca munayaḥ sukham āpuḥ param mune brahma viṣṇu maheśānām kara nissṛta toyāt śakti ādayaḥ śubhāḥ vasiṣṭham prāpya tam kāntam saṃreje muni sattamaiḥ evam saṃdhyā caritram te kathitam muni sattamaiḥ pavitram pāvanam divyam sarva kāma phalaiḥ avāpnoti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvi satīkhaṇḍe saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya brahmanaḥ hi prajāpateḥ prasanna mānasaḥ bhūtvā tam provāca nāradaḥ divyā śiva bhakti vivardhinī arundhatyāḥ tathā tasyāḥ svarūpāyāḥ pare bhave idānīm brūhi dharma jña pavitram caritam param śivasya para pāpa ghnam maṅga ca mad ṛṣa bhāvitātmanaḥ suprasannataraḥ bhūtvā brahmā vacanam abravīt bhaktyā dhanyaḥ tvam śiva sevakaḥ aham vimohitaḥ tātaiḥ yadā eva tarhitaḥ purā aciṃtayam sadā aham tad śambhu vākya viṣa arditaḥ citte śiva māyā vimohitaḥ citte śiva māyā vimohitaḥ śive ca īrṣyām akārṣa hi tat śṛṇuṣva vadāmi te atha aham agamam tatra yatra dakṣa ādayaḥ sthitāḥ sāratim madanam dṛṣṭvā sama as kiṃcana doham hi kiṃcana dakṣam ābhāṣya su prītyā parān putrān ca nāradaiḥ avocam vacanam saḥ aham śiva māyā vimohitaḥ marīci ādyāḥ sutāḥ śṛṇuta mad vacaḥ śrutvā upāyam vidheyam hi mama kaṣṭa apanuttaye kāntā abhilāṣa mātram mama dṛṣṭvā aśambhuḥ agarhayat mām ca yuṣmān mahā yogī dhikkāram kṛtavan bahu tena duḥkha abhitapta ūhum labhe ham śarma na kvacid yathā gṛhṇātu kāntām saḥ saḥ yatnaḥ kāryaḥ eva hi tu kāntām sa sukhī syām duḥkha varjitaḥ durlabhaḥ satum kāmaḥ mama param manye vicārāt kāntā abhilāṣa mātram mama dṛṣṭvā śambhuḥ agarhayat puratas yasmāt sa kāntām saṃgṛhīṣyati kasmāt saḥ kāntām saṃgṛhīṣyati kā vā nārī triloke idam yā bhavet tad manāḥ sthitā yoga mārgam avajñāpya tasya moham kariṣyati manmathaḥ api samarthaḥ no bhaviṣyati asya mohane nitānta yogī rāmāṇām nām api sahate na saḥ agṛhīteṣu nā ca eva hareṇa kathaya ādinā ca bhavet sṛṣṭiḥ tad vācā na anya vāritā bhuvi kecid bhaviṣyāntaiḥ māyā vadhvā mahā asurāḥ vadhvā kecid hareḥ nūnam kecid śambhoḥ upāyāt vimukhe śambhau tathā ekānta virāgiṇi asmāt ṛte na karma anyat kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ iti uktvā tanayaḥ ca aham su nirīkṣya ca madanam tatra sa ānandam agadam tatas anayā sahacārinyā rājase tvam manobhavaiḥ eṣā ca bhavatā patyā yuktā saṃśobhate bhṛśam yathā striyā hṛṣīkeśaḥ hariṇā sā yathā icchayā mayā tyaktā bhaviṣyati manaḥ avocam ca iti vinamrakaḥ śṛṇu nāthaiḥ maheśānaiḥ mārgitā yādṛśā tvayā nivedayāmi su prītyām tām striyam tādṛśām prabho sā bhinna rūpeṇa saṃjātā kārya sādhinī sarasvatī tathā lakṣmī dvidhā rūpā purā prabho padmā kāntā abhavat viṣṇoḥ tathā mama sarasvatī sā sā tapasya deveśa tvat atha hi dṛḍha vratā tvām patim prāptu kāmā vai mahā tejovatī satī dātum gaccha varam tasyai kṛpām kuru maheśvaraiḥ vivāhaya paramam bhūyāt ripu lokeṣu sukha āvaham sarva jvaraḥ vinaśyet vai sarveṣām na atra saṃśayaḥ athavā mad vacaḥ śeṣa iva datam madhusūdanaḥ upari kṛpām kṛtvā mama upari kuru sa dṛṣṭayā trilokam su vivāhya tām iti uktvā bhagavant viṣṇuḥ tūṣṇīm āsa muneṃ tathā stutim vihasya āha saḥ prabhuḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ tathā stutim vihasya āha saḥ prabhuḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ tatas tu āvām ca saṃprāpya ca ājñām saḥ munibhiḥ suraiḥ agacchau asva iṣṭa deśam para harṣitau iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīye satīkhaṇḍe viṣṇubrahmakṛta śivaprārthanāvarṇanam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śi0pu0 uvāca iti uktā sarva deva aiśva kṛtā śambhoḥ tutiḥ sā varam prāptā śṛṇuhi ādarāt mune upoṣitā āśvine māsi sarva īśam pūjayāmāsa bhaktyāḥ iti nandāvate pūrṇe navamyām dina bhāga maṅgnāyāḥ pratyakṣam abhavat haraḥ sarva aṅga sundara om gauraḥ pañcavaktraḥ trilocanaḥ candrabhālaḥ prasanna ātmā śitikaṇṭhaḥ caturbhujaḥ bhāsvaraḥ svardhunyā vilasat śīrṣaḥ sakala aṅga manoharaḥ prāha varaya saṃdāsye yatra vā abhimatam bhavet uvāca jānan api iha tad bhāvam mahādevaḥ jagatpatiḥ jagau varam vṛṇīṣva iti tad vākya śravaṇa icchayā sā api trapā vaśā yuktā vaktum naḥ hṛdi yat sthitam punar tat jñātvā su prasannaḥ bhūt śaṃkaraḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ varam brūhi varam brūhi prāha iti saḥ punar dutam satī bhakti vaśaḥ śambhuḥ antaryāmī atha trapām yadā prāha haram satī yadā prāha haram satī yatheṣṭam dehi vara da varam iti anivārakam tadā vākyasya avasānam an avekṣya vṛṣadhvajaḥ bhava tvam mama prāha tām bhakta vatsalaḥ etat śrutvā vacaḥ tasya sa abhīṣṭa phala bhāvanam tūṣṇīm tasthau pramuditā varam prāpya manogatam sthitā sā cāru hāsinī sthitā sā cāru hāsinī akarot nija bhāvān ca hāvān kāma vivardhanān tatobhāvān samādāya śṛgāra ākhyaḥ rasaḥ tadā āśu reje satī haram prāpya snigdha bhinna jana prabhā candra abhyāse āmra lekhā iva sphaṭika ujvala varṣmaṇaḥ atha sā tam uvāca idam haram dākṣāyaṇī muhur evam satī vacaḥ śrutvā maheśaḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ tathā astu iti vacaḥ prāha nirīkṣya tām haraḥ prāpta ājñā mātuḥ abhyāsam aāsāt moha mudā anvitā haraḥ api himavatprastham praviśya ca nija āśramam dākṣāyaṇī viyogāt vai kṛcchra dhyāna paraḥ abhavat samādhāya manaḥ śambhu laukikām gatim āśritaḥ ciṃtayāmāsa deva ṛṣe manasā mām vṛṣadhvajaḥ tatra eva samupasthitaḥ sarasvatī yutam mām ca deva ṛṣe vīkṣya saḥ prabhuḥ utsukaḥ satyā śambhuḥ uvāca ha mām sā satī dākṣāyaṇī tu iti gocarīkṛtya mām gṛhāṇa jagatpate gocarīkṛtya mām gṛhāṇa jagatpate tat api aṅgīkṛtam brahman mayā tad bhakti tuṣṭitas sā gatā bhavanam mātuḥ aham atra āgataḥ vidhe tasmāt tvam gaccha bhavanam dakṣasya mama śāsanāt tām dakṣaḥ api yathā kanyām dadyāt mama aram tathā vada yathā mama tvam tathā kuru samāśvāsayam tam dakṣam sarva vidyā viśāradaḥ iti udīrya mahādevaḥ sakāśe mama prajāpateḥ sarasvatīm vilokyāsu viyoga vaśagaḥ bhavat tena aham api ca ājñaptaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ mudā anvitaḥ prāvocam ca iti jagantām nātham tam bhakta vatsalam sutām svām ca svayam eva pradāsyati aham ca api vadiṣyāmi tvad vākyam tad samakṣāt prabhum agamam dakṣa nilayam syandanena ati veginām tatas mātre pitreya tad praṇāmam akarot tadā mātre pitreyaiḥ tad sakhyam samācakhyau maheśvarāt vara prāptiḥ sva saṃkhyā vai satyā stuṣṭā astu bhaktyāḥ mātā pitā ca vṛttām tam sarvam śrutvā sakhī mukhāt ānandam paramam lebhe cakre ca parama utsavam dravyam dadau dvijātibhyaḥ yathā abhīṣṭa su dāra dhīḥ mūrkhī ca mahāmanāḥ vīriṇī tām samāliṃgya sva sutām prīti vardhinīm mūrkhī upāghrāya muditā praśaṃsa muhur muhur dakṣaḥ suta arthe añ ā gamiṣyatiḥ mām dṛṣṭvā pitaram dakṣaḥ praṇamya avanataḥ sthitaḥ āsanam ca dadau me sva bhavāya yathocitam tatas mām sarva loka īśam tatra āgamana kāraṇam dakṣaḥ papraccha saḥ kṣipram citā āviṣṭaḥ api harṣitaḥ putra snehāt kārya vaśāt atha vā loka kārakaiḥ mama āśramam samāyātaḥ ruṣṭasya te darśanāt na śarma labhate iṃjasā na śarma labhate iṃjasā alabdha chidra madanaḥ jiṃgāya giriśam na yam sarvaiḥ puṣpa mayaiḥ bāṇaiḥ yatnam kṛtvā api bhūriśas parityajya ātma cintanam satīm vicitayan āste vyākulaḥ prākṛtaḥ yathā vismṛtya praśrutām vāṇīm gaṇa agre viprayogāt kka satī iti eva mayā pūrvam tvayā ca madanena ca marīca ādyaiḥ muni varaiḥ tat siddham adhunā suta tasmāt tu dakṣa tanayām śambhu artham parikalpitām tasmāt tu dakṣa tanayām śambhu artham parikalpitām tasmai deha avilambena kṛtā te kṛtakṛtya tā aham tam ānayiṣyāmi nāradaiḥ tat tat tat samāptam nāradaiḥ dakṣaḥ api sa dāra tanayaḥ hi api abhavat pūrṇa kāmaḥ tu pīyūṣaiḥ iva pūritaḥ iti śrī śaive mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitā tāyām dvitīye satīkhaṇḍe satīvaralābhaḥ nāma saṃptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca rudra pārśve tvayi gate kim abhūt caritam tatas kā vārttā hi abhavat tātaiḥ kim cakāra haraḥ svayam uvāca mām vīkṣya hi mahādevam himavat giri saṃsthitam mām vīkṣya vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ prītyā haraḥ loke gatim āśritya līlayā satyā bhaktyā ca mām kṣipram uvāca prākṛtaḥ yathā tām prāṇa dhāriṇīm satī iti satatam brahman vada kārya karomi aham abhedāt mama sā prāpyā tadvidhe kriyatām tathā mad abhīṣṭam idam kāryam tvad vākyāt adhikam punar mad putrī ārādhitaḥ śambhuḥ etad artham svayam punar saḥ api anviṣyati mām yasmāt tadā deyā mayā hare marīca ādīn sva putrān ca mānasān api saṃsmara taiḥ sārdham dakṣa nilayam gamiṣye sa gaṇaḥ vidhe tāḥ sarve mānasāḥ tanayāḥ tvayā mama smaraṇa mātreṇa hṛṣṭāḥ te drutam ādarāt viṣṇuḥ samāgataḥ tūrṇam smṛtaḥ rudreṇa śaivarāj sa sva sainyaḥ tathā hara gaṇānām ca prāṇanda manasām ati gaja go vyātra sarpāḥ ca jaṭā candra kalā tathā jagmuḥ sarve bhūṣaṇa tvam yathāyogyam śiva iccha tatas kṣaṇena balinā valīvardena veginā saḥ viṣṇu pramukhaḥ prītyā prāpa dakṣa ālayam haraḥ tatas dakṣaḥ vinīta ātmā tanūruhaḥ prayayau sat mukham tasya saṃyuktaḥ sakalaiḥ nijaiḥ sarve sura gaṇāḥ tatra svayam dakṣaṇaiḥ satkṛtāḥ pārśve śreṣṭham ca munibhiḥ upaviṣṭā yathākramam haram vidhānena da tvā āsanam anuttamam tatas viṣṇum ca mām viprān surān sarvān gaṇān tathā pūjayāmāsa sat bhaktyā yatho śi0pu0 bhūtvā yathocitām pūjām teṣām pūjya ādibhiḥ tathā cakāra saṃvidam dakṣaḥ munibhiḥ mānasaiḥ punar tatas mām pitaram prāha dakṣaḥ prītyā hi mad sutaḥ praṇipatya tvayā karma kārya vaivāhikam vibho vāḍham iti aham api uktvā prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā samutthāya tatas akārṣe tat kāryam akhilam tathā tat kāryam akhilam tathā tatas śubhe muhūrte hi lagne gṛha bala anvite satīm nija sutām dakṣaḥ dadau harṣeṇa śambhave udvāha vidhinā saḥ api pāṇim jagrāha harṣitaḥ dākṣāyaṇyāḥ vara tanvaḥ tadānīm vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ aham hariḥ tvad ādyāḥ vai sunayaḥ ca surāḥ gaṇāḥ nemuḥ sarve saṃstutibhiḥ toṣayā īśvaram samutsavaḥ mahān āsīt nṛtya gāna puraḥsaraḥ ānandam paramam jagmuḥ sarve muni gaṇāḥ surāḥ kanyām datvā kṛtārthaḥ bhūt tadā dakṣaḥ hi mad sutaḥ śiva aśivau prasannau ca nikhilam maṅgala ālayam iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīye satīkhaṇḍe uvāca kanyādānavarṇanaḥ nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca kṛtvā dakṣa smutā dānam yautakam vividham dadau harāya su prasannaḥ ca dvijebhyaḥ bhavat vividham dhanam atha śambhum upāgatya samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ sārdham kamalayā ca idam uvāca garuḍadhvajaḥ mahādeva karuṇā sāgara prabho tvam pitā jagantām tāta satī mātā akhilasya ca tvam līlāvatārau vai satām kṣemāya sarvadā mad arthāya śrutiḥ eṣā sanātanā snigdha nīlāñjana śyāma śobhayā śobhase haraiḥ dākṣāyaṇyā yathā ca aham pratilomena padmayā nṝṇām rakṣām kuru satyā anayā satām saṃsāra sāriṇām śambho maṅgalam sarvadā tathā yaḥ enām sa abhilāṣaḥ vai dṛṣṭvā śrutvā athavā bhavet madhusūdanam samāgatya gṛhye ukta vidhinā akhilam agni kāryam yathoddiṣṭam akārṣe ca su vistaram tatas śivā śivaḥ ca eva yathāvidhi prahṛṣṭa vat agneḥ tadā mad ācārya dvija ājñayā tadā mad ācārya dvija ājñayā tadā mahā utsavaḥ tatra adbhutaḥ bhū dvijasattamaiḥ sarveṣām sukha dam vādya aṃgīta nṛtya puraḥsaram tatra caritam samabhūt ati su vismaya karam tāta tat śṛṇu tvam vadāmi te durjñeyā śāmbhavī māyā tayā saṃmohitam jagant yaḥ sura mānuṣam yaḥ haiṃ śambhum mohayitum purā iccham kapaṭena ha mām ca tam śaṃkaraḥ tātaiḥ mohayāmāsa līlayā madana āviṣṭa cetāḥ ca bhūtvā aṅgāni vyalokayam aham satyā dvijaśreṣṭha śiva māyā vimohitaḥ yathā yathā aham ramyāṇi vyaikṣam aṅgāni hi tathā tathā satyā babhūva saṃhṛṣṭaḥ hi tathā tathā aham evam tathā dṛṣṭvā dakṣajām ca pativratām smara āviṣṭa manāḥ vakram draṣṭu kāmaḥ bhavam mune na śambhoḥ lajjayā vakram pratyakṣam ca vilokitam na ca sā lajjayā āviṣṭā karoti pragaṭam mukham tatas tad darśana arthāya sat upāyam bhūrīṇi kṣiptvā tatra vibhāvasau tathā prādurbhūtaḥ tatas dhūmaḥ bhūyāḥ tatra samaṃtataḥ tādṛś yena tamaḥ bhūtam vedi bhūmi vinirmitam tatas dhūma ākule netre maheśaḥ parame hastābhyām chādayāmāsa bahu līlā karaḥ prabhuḥ hastābhyām chādayāmāsa bahu līlā karaḥ prabhuḥ tatas vastram samutkṣipya satī vakram aham avekṣam kila kāma ārtaḥ prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā mama kāntāyāḥ vakram dṛṣṭam na rāgāt vivāhe mama kāntāyāḥ vakram dṛṣṭam na rāgāt tvam votsi śaṃkareṇa etat karma jñātam na kiṃcana trailokye api na mama ajñātam gūḍham tasmāt katham vidhe yat kiṃcid triṣu lokeṣu jaṅgamam sthāvaram tathā tasmāt aham madhya gaḥ mūḍhaiḥ tailam yadvat tila antigam uvāca iti uktā tadā viṣṇu vacaḥ smaran iyeṣa hetum brahmānam śūlam udyamya śaṃkaraḥ ca hetum dvijottamaiḥ marīci pramukhāḥ te vai hāhākāram ca cakrire tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve munayaḥ ca akhilāḥ tathā tuṣṭuvuḥ śaṃkaram tatra prajvalantam tvam bhaya āturāḥ ūcuḥ devaiḥ devaiḥ mahādevaiḥ śaraṇa āgata vatsalaiḥ brahmānam rakṣa rakṣa īśaiḥ kṛpām kuru maheśvaraiḥ jagatpitā maheśaiḥ tvam ha tvad bhaktim īśvaraiḥ uvāca ittham bahutaram dīnāḥ nirjarāḥ munayaḥ ca te tuṣṭuvuḥ devadeveśam krodha āviṣṭam maheśvaram dakṣaḥ mā evam mā eva tat iti pāṇim udyamya śaṃkitaḥ vārayāmāsa bhūteśam kṣipram etya purogataḥ atha agreśam gatam vīkṣya tadā dakṣam maheśvaraḥ saṃsmaran prārthanām hareḥ satīm yaḥ sa abhilāṣaḥ san vīkṣeta vadha tam prabho iti viṣṇu vacaḥ satyam vidhim hatvā karomi aham sa abhilāpaḥ katham brahmā satīm mānuṣāḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt audāsīnyam ca sarvaśas abhūvam vikalaḥ atīva tadā aham tad vimohakaḥ tam evam vādinam rudram tuṣṭāva praṇataḥ sudhīḥ tam evam vādinam rudram tuṣṭāva praṇataḥ sudhīḥ stutvā ca vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ śaṃkaram bhakta vatsalam idam ūce vārayan tam kṣipram bhūtvā bhaktaḥ bhakta rājaḥ iti īritaḥ vijñaptim hṛdi mama matvā kṛpām kuru mama upari traṣṭum kṛpām kṛtvā mama upari trayaḥ devāḥ kariṣyāmaḥ punar punar trayaḥ devāḥ vayam nāthaiḥ śiva rūpaiḥ tvad ājñayā uvāca iti ākarṇya maheśaḥ tu vijñaptim viṣṇunā kṛtām pratyuvāca akhilān tān ca śrāvayan ca dṛḍha vrataḥ deva deva rama īśāna viṣṇo mad prāṇa vallabhaiḥ na nivāraya mām tātaiḥ vadhāt asya khalaḥ tu ayam pūrayiṣyāmi vijñaptim pūrva antagīkṛtām mayā mahā pāpa karam duṣṭam hanmi enam caturānanam aham eva prajāḥ trakṣye sarvāḥ sthira carāḥ api anyam srakṣye sṛṣṭi karam athavā aham sva tejasā hatvā enam vidhim eva aham sva paṇam pūrayan kṛtam sraṣṭāram ekam sakṣyāmi na nivāraya mā īśaiḥ mām mahā bhakta priyasya saḥ śambhuḥ ūce punar tam vai khyāpayan ātmanaḥ gatim yaḥ vidhiḥ mama lakṣyate bhinnaḥ eva ayam pratyakṣeṇa agratas thitaḥ tvad ājñayā vadāmi īśaiḥ śṛṇvantu nikhilāḥ surāḥ manaḥ saṃdhārya svam manaḥ ca kaḥ tvam kaḥ ham ca kaḥ brahmā te eva paramātmanaḥ aṃśa trayam idam bhinnam sṛṣṭi sthiti anta kāraṇam ciṃtayasva ātmanā ātmānam sva līlā dhṛta vigrahaḥ mayaḥ tvam brahma saguṇaḥ hi aṃśa bhūtāḥ vayam trayaḥ śiras grīvā ādi bhedena yathā ekasya eva varṣmaṇaḥ aṅgāni te tathā īśasya tasya bhāga trayam haraiḥ tirabhram sva puram purāṇam kūṭastham avyaktam aneta rūpam nityam ca dīrgha ādi viśeṣaṇa ādi ahīnam śivaḥ tvam tatas eva sarvam tasya mahādevaḥ muni īśvaraiḥ su prasannaḥ ca na jaghāna saḥ mām tatas nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ nāma caritam śambhoḥ adbhutam maṅgalāyanam tatas kim abhavat tātaiḥ kathyatām śaśimaulinaḥ satyāḥ ca caritam divyam sarva agha ogha vināśanam tatas tuṣṭa manāḥ śambhuḥ bahu līlā karaḥ prabhuḥ mune mām samuvāca idam sarveṣām śṛṇvatām tadā uvāca brahman tātaiḥ nirbhayaḥ tvam bhava adhunā sva śīrṣa spṛśa hastena mad ājñām kuru asaṃśayam iti ākarṇya vacaḥ śambhoḥ bahu līlā kṛtaḥ prabhoḥ spṛśan svam kam tathā bhūtvā prāṇamam vṛṣabhadhvajam yāvat evam aham svam kam spṛśāmi nija pāṇinā tāvat tatra sthitam sadyas tad rūpa vṛṣa vāhanam tatas lajjā parītām thitaḥ ca aham adhomukhaḥ indra ādyaiḥ amaraiḥ sarvaiḥ su dṛṣṭaḥ sarvatas sthitaiḥ atha aham lajjayā āviṣṭaḥ praṇipatya maheśvaram prāvocam saṃstutim kṛtvā kṣamyatām kṣamyatām iti asya pāpasya śudhi artham prāyaścittam vada prabho nigraham ca tathā anyāyam yena pāpam prayātu mama iti uktaḥ tu mayā na ātmā mad ārādhana tatparaḥ khyātim yāsyasi sarvatra nāmnā rudraśiraḥ kṣitau sādhakaḥ sarva kṛtyānām tejas bhājām dvijanmanām idam kṛtyam yasmāt tvayā adhunā tasmāt tvam mānuṣaḥ bhūtvā vicariṣyasi bhū tale yaḥ tvām ca anena rūpeṇa dṛṣṭvā kaḥ vicariṣyati kim etat brahmaṇaḥ mūrdhni vadan iti pura antakaḥ tatas te ceṣṭitam sarvam kautukāt śroṣyati iti yaḥ para dāra kṛtāt tyāgāt muktim sadyas sa yāsyati muni śreṣṭhaiḥ layaṃkarāḥ dine vyoniḥ su garjadbhiḥ ca śaṃkaraḥ dine vyoniḥ su garjadbhiḥ ca śaṃkaraḥ dākṣāyaṇī devī bhṛśam śāntaḥ abhavat dutam atha ca aham vīta bhayaḥ śaṃkarasya ājñayā tadā mune śeṣam vaivāhikam karma samāptim anayam mune papāta puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ ca śiva aśiva śiraskayoḥ sarvatra ca muni śreṣṭhaiḥ mudā deva gaṇa ujjhitā vādyamāneṣu vādyeṣu gāyamāneṣu teṣu ca paṭhatsum vipra vargeṣu vādān bhaktyā anviteṣu ca rambhā ādiṣu puraṃdhrīṣu nṛtyamānāsu sādaram mahān āsīt deva patnīṣu nāradam atha karma avitāna īśaḥ prasannaḥ parameśvaraḥ prāha mām prāñjalim prītyā laukikām gatim āśritaḥ mahā īśvaraḥ uvāca he brahman su kṛtam karma vaivāhikam ca yat prasannaḥ asmi tvam ācārya om dadyām te dakṣiṇām ca kām syāt su durlabhā brūhi śīghram mahābhāgaiḥ na ādeyam vidyate mama uvāca yena eva tu rūpeṇa vedau asyām maheśvaraiḥ tvayā stheyam sadā eva atra nṝṇām pāpa viśuddhaye yena asya saṃnidhau kṛtvā sva āśramam śaśiśekharaiḥ tapaḥ kuryām vināśāya sva pāpasya asya śaṃkaraiḥ caitra śukka trayodaśyām nakṣatre bhaga daivate sūryavāre ca yaḥ bhaktyā vīkṣeta bhuvi mānavaḥ tadā eva tasya pāpāni hara saṃkṣayam vardhate vipulam puṇyam rogāḥ naśyantu sarvaśas yā nārī durbhagā vandhyā kāṇā rūpa vivarjitā api hitāya sarva lokasya vedyām tasyām vvavasthitaḥ sthāsyāmi sahitaḥ patnyā satyā tvad vacanāt vidhe uvāca iti uktvā bhagavant tatra sa bhāryaḥ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ uvāca vedi madhya sthaḥ mūrti kṛtvā aṃśa rūpiṇīm tatas dakṣam samāmam mahā bhāgavata śaṃkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ patnyā satyā gaṃtu manāḥ abhūt sva jana vatsalaḥ etasmin antare dakṣaḥ vinaya avanataḥ sudhīḥ sa añjaliḥ natakaḥ vṛṣabhadhvajam viṣṇu ādayaḥ surāḥ sarve munayaḥ ca gaṇāḥ tadā natvā saṃstūya vividham cakruḥ jaya ravam mudā mudā āropya vṛṣabhe śambhuḥ satī dakṣa ājñayā mudā jagāma himavatprastham vṛṣabha sthaḥ svayam prabhuḥ mohinī cāru hāsinī vireje vṛṣabha sthā vai candra ante kālikā yathā viṣṇu ādayaḥ surāḥ sarve marīci ādyāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ madhyamā gadi sṛṣṭaḥ hi dakṣaḥ prītyā atha śambhunā sva dhām prāpa sa gaṇaḥ śambhuḥ prema samākulaḥ visṛṣṭāḥ api viṣṇu ādyāḥ śambhunā punar eva te tatra gatvā akhilān devān sunīn api parāḥ tathā mudā visarjayāmāsa bahu sat mānya sa ādaram śambhum ābhāṣya te sarve viṣṇu ādyā suditā tatas saḥ śaṃkaraḥ satyā sa gaṇaḥ sūtikṛt mune prāpa svam dhām saṃhṛṣṭaḥ kailāsam parvata uttamam etat vaḥ sarvam ākhyātam yathā tasya anvitā sādhvī syāt putriṇī prītyā śrutvā ākhyānam idam śubham iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīye satīkhaṇḍe nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ mad caritam śivayoḥ śubham caritam śivayoḥ śubham vivāhaḥ ca śrutaḥ samyak sarva moha apahārakaḥ parama jñāna saṃpannaḥ maṅgala ālayaḥ uttamaḥ bhūyas eva vivitsā mama caritam mad śivayoḥ śubham tat varṇaya mahā prājñaiḥ kṛpām kṛtvā atula amaram tassaumyaiḥ śiva līlā anuvarṇane sva gaṇaḥ sva sthānam prāpya modanam deva ṛṣe tatra vṛṣabhāt avātarat ati priyāt yathāyogyam nija sthānam praviśya sa satī sakhaḥ mumudeti iva rudra saṃ0 deva ṛṣe bhava ācāra karaḥ śivaḥ tatas virūpākṣaḥ imām prāpya dākṣayaṇī gaṇān svīyān niyīpayāmāsa nandi ādīn giri kandarāt uvāca ca etān tān sarva ānandi ādīn ati sūnṛtam laukikām rītim āśritya karuṇā sāgaraḥ prabhuḥ yadā aham ca smarāmi atra smaraṇa ādara mānasāḥ samāgamiṣyatha tadā mad pārśva mama gaṇāḥ drutam iti ukte vāmadevena nandi ādyāḥ sva gaṇāḥ ca te mahā vegāḥ mahā vīrāḥ nānā sthāneṣu saṃyayuḥ īśvaraḥ api tayā sārdham teṣu yāteṣu vibhramī dākṣāyaṇyā samam reme rahasye muditaḥ bhṛśam kadācid vanya puṣpāṇi samāhṛtya manoharām mālām vidhāya satyāḥ tu hāra sthāne saḥ yojayat kadācid darpaṇe ca eva vīkṣatīm ātmanaḥ bahu tat karṇe kathayati tyasyāḥ haraḥ draṣṭum tad ānanam na dūram api gantā asau samāgatya prayatnāt anubadhnāti nāma akṣī tām pṛṣṭhadeśenya mānasām antarhitaḥ tu tatra eva māyayā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ tām āliliṃga bhītyā svam cakitā vyākulām abhavat sva kara sparśanam muhur aṅgadān valayān ūrmān viśleṣya ca punar punar tad sthānāt punar eva asau tad sthāne pratyayojayat yāti savarṇā te sakhī tu imām yāti savarṇā te sakhī tu imām yāsyatu asyāḥ tathā as as as as as as as as as as as as saṃkāśāḥ palāśāḥ ca virejire kāma astra vat sumanasaḥ pramodāt pādapa acaraḥ babhuḥ paṅkaja puṣpāṇi saraḥsu sakala añjanān vāyudevatā nāgakeśara vṛkṣāḥ ca svarṇa varṇaiḥ prasūnakaiḥ babhruḥ madana ketu āmnā manojñāḥ śaṃkara rātike lavaṃgavallī mohayāmāsa cetāṃsi bhṛśam kāmi jane purā cetāṃsi bhṛśam kāmi jane purā cāru pāvaka carcitsu susvara aśvata śālinaḥ babhuḥ madana bāṇa oghaiḥ paryaka madana āvṛtāḥ tuṣārāḥ sūrya raśmīṇām saṃgamāt agaman bahis bahis tadā prasannāḥ saha candreṇa vibhāvaryaḥ priyeṇa evam kāminyaḥ su manoharāḥ tasmin kāle mahādevaḥ saha satyā dharā uttame reme saḥ su ciram chandam nikuñjeṣu nadīṣu ca tathā tena samam reje tadā dākṣāyaṇī haraḥ kṣaṇam api śāntim āpa tayā vinā sambhoga viṣaye devī satī tasya manas priyā viśati iva harasya aṅge pāyayan iva tad vasam mālābhiḥ bhūṣayan sakalām tanum sva hasta racitābhiḥ tu nava śarma akarot ca saḥ ālāpaiḥ vīkṣitaiḥ āsyaiḥ tathā sambhāṣaṇaiḥ haraḥ tad vakra ambuja vāsena tu bhuja parimāṇaiḥ krīḍataḥ tasya jātāḥ daśa daśa ca sura ṛṣe vatsarāḥ pañca ca anye satī khaṇḍe satīśivakriḍāvarṇanam nāma ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ prāha prastha stham vṛṣabhadhvajam dhautāḥ pāthaḥ vindu vikarṣaṇāḥ na sūryaḥ dṛśyate na api megha channaḥ niśāpatiḥ divā api rātri vat bhāti virahi vyasana ākaraḥ meghāḥ na ekatra tiṣṭhataḥ dhvanantaḥ pavane śaṃkaraiḥ patantaḥ iva lokānām dṛśyaṃte mūrdhani śaṃkaraiḥ vāta āhatāḥ mahā vṛkṣāḥ nartataḥ iva ca ambare dṛśyaṃte haraiḥ bhīrūṇām trāsa dāḥ yad kāmuka īpsitāḥ snigdha nīla añjanasya āśu sa divaughasya pṛṣṭhatas balāka rājīva ati uccais yamunā pṛṣṭha phena vat valayam dṛśyate kā śi0pu0 ham tyajya sat kiṃśukān uccāvacān kalau lakṣmī yantrā saṃtyajya sat janān mandāra stana pilūnām śabdena hṛṣitā su duḥ kekāyante prativane satatam megha utsukānām madhura śvātakānām manoharaḥ dhārā sāra śaraiḥ tāpam petuḥ pratipatha udgatam meghānām paśya mad dehe durnayam kara ye chādayanti anugate mayūrān cātakān tathā ye chādayanti anugate mayūrān cātakān tathā śikhi sāraṅgayoḥ dṛṣṭvā mitrāt api parābhavam harṣaiḥ gacchanti giriśam vidūram api mānasam nīḍam kāka aśva korakāḥ nīḍam kāka aśva korakāḥ tvām vinā gehān katham śāntim avāpsyasi mahatī tvam vṛṣabhadhvajaiḥ mahātmā satīm devīm smita bhinna oṣṭha puṭaḥ mahātmā sarva tattva jñaḥ toṣayan parameśvaraḥ uvāca meghāḥ tatra na gaṃtāraḥ kadācid api mad priye mahībhṛtaḥ sadā prāleya sānoḥ tu varṣāsu api manohare mūlam samāsādya puṣkarāvartaka ādayaḥ iti ukteṣu giri indreṣu yasya upari bhavet hite manoruciḥ nivāsāya tam ācakṣva drutam hi mama kanyā giri kanyakāḥ ca yāḥ nāga kanyāḥ ca turaṃga mukhyāḥ sarvāḥ tu tāḥ te satatam sahāya tām samācariṣyanti anumoda vibhramaiḥ rūpam tat evam tulam vadanam su cāru dṛṣṭvā aṅganā nija vapuḥ nija kānti sahyam helā nije vapuṣi rūpa gaṇeṣu nityam kartāraḥ iti animiṣa īkṣaṇa cāru rūpāḥ mama parvatarāja jāyā rūpaiḥ guṇaiḥ khyātavatī triloke sā ca api te tatra manas numodam nityam kariṣyati anunāthana ādyaiḥ puram hi vagaiḥ girirāja vandyaiḥ prītim vicinvadbhiḥ udāra rūpā śikṣā sadā te khalu śocitā api kāyaḥ anvaham prīti yuta aguṇa ādyaiḥ vicitraiḥ kokila ālāpa modaiḥ kuñja gaṇā sadā vasantaiḥ prabhavam gantum icchasi kim priye nānā bahu jala āpūrṇa saras śīta samāvṛtam padminī śataśas yuktam acala indram himālayam sarva kāma pradaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ śādvalaiḥ kalpa saṃjñakaiḥ sakṣaṇam paśya kusumāni atha aśva kari gotra je sakṣaṇam paśya kusumāni atha aśva kari gotra je praśānta śvāpada gaṇam su nibhiḥ yatibhiḥ vṛtam mahā nānā mṛga gaṇaiḥ yutam rājataiḥ ca virājitam rājataiḥ ca virājitam paṅkajaiḥ mukulaiḥ vṛtam śiśumāraiḥ tathā asaṃkhyaiḥ kacchapaiḥ makaraiḥ karaiḥ niṣevitam mañjulaiḥ ca tathā nīlotpala ādibhiḥ tasmāt muktaḥ ca kuṅkumaiḥ kuṅkumaiḥ lasat gandha jalaiḥ śubhraiḥ āpūrṇaiḥ su accha kāntibhiḥ śādvalaiḥ taruṇaiḥ tugaiḥ tīra sthaiḥ upaśobhitam madhura ārāvibhiḥ modakāri tri bhramara ādibhiḥ śabdāyamānam ca muda meroḥ uccais surālayam rambhā śacī menakā bhoru gaṇa sevitam kim tvam icchasi sarveṣām parvatānām hi bhūbhṛtām sāra bhūte mahā ramye saṃvihartum tatra devī sakhī yutā sa apsaras gaṇa maṇḍitā tatra devī sakhī yutā sa apsaras gaṇa maṇḍitā nityam kariṣyati śacī te yogyam sahāya tām athavā mama kailāsa parva nānā mṛga gaṇaiḥ yukte padma ākara śata āvṛte sarvaiḥ guṇaiḥ sat vastu sumeroḥ api sundari sthāneṣu eteṣu yatra api te antaḥkaraṇe spṛhā tam drutam me samācakṣva vāsa kartāsmi tatra te tad vākyam ākarṇya haraḥ parama mohitaḥ himādri śikharam tuṅgam dākṣāyaṇyā samam yayau siddha aṅganā gaṇa yutam agamyam ca eva yakṣibhiḥ agamat śikharam ramyam sarasi vana rājitam maphulaiḥ ca nīlotpala cayaiḥ tathā śobhitam cakravāka ādyaiḥ pramatta sārasaiḥ śabditaiḥ sadā na yajñe sa divārātrau na brahmāni tapaḥ samam satyām hi manasā śambhuḥ prītim eva cakāra ha evam mahādeva mukham satī apaśyat sma sarvadā sarvatra sadā adrākṣīt satī mukham evam anyonya saṃsargāt anurāga mahīruham vardhayāmāsatuḥ kālī śivau bhāva ambu secanaiḥ brahmā uvāca evam kṛtvā vihāram vai hariṇā ca sā satī saṃtuṣṭā sā bhavat ca ati virāgā samajāyata ekasmin divase devī satī rahasi saṃgatā śivam praṇamya sat bhaktyā nyasya uccais su kṛta añjaliḥ su prasannam prabhum na tvā sā dakṣa tanayā satī uvāca sa añjaliḥ bhaktyā vinaya avanatā tatas mahā yogin prabho dīna uddhara mahā yogin kṛpām kuru mama upari tvam puras puruṣaḥ svāmī rajaḥ sattva tamaḥ paraḥ nirguṇa sa guṇaḥ sākṣī nirvikārī mahā prabhuḥ maheśānaiḥ nivṛttam te manaḥ tatas jñātum icchāmi deveśaiḥ param tattvam sukha āvaham yam na saṃsāra duḥkhāt vai taret jīva ojasā haraiḥ yat kṛtvā viṣayī jīvaḥ saḥ labhet paramam padam saṃsārī na bhavet nāthaiḥ vada kṛpām kuru brahmā uvāca iti apṛcchat sma sat bhaktyā śaṃkaram sā satī mune maheśānī jīva uddhārāya kevalam ādiśaktiḥ maheśānī jīva uddhārāya kevalam ākarṇya tat śivaḥ svāmī sva icchayā upapātta vigrahaḥ avocat parama prītaḥ satīm yoga virakta dhīḥ maheśvari yatas vijānīhi mahā vijñānam parameśvari dvitīyam smaraṇam yatra na aham brahma iti śuddha dhīḥ tat durlabham triloke idam tad jñātā viralaḥ priye tad kartuḥ sarvadā asukham vijñānam na bhavati eva sati bhakti virodhinaḥ vijñānam na bhavati eva sati bhakti virodhinaḥ bhaktyā ahīnaḥ sadā aham vai tad prabhāvāt gṛheṣu api nīcānām yāti hīnānām gāmi devi na saṃśayaḥ bhedāt vividhe dvividhe hi te bhedāt vividhe dvividhe hi te ṣaḍvidhā naiṣṭhikā jñeyā dvitīyā ekavidhā smṛtā vihita avihita abhedāt tām anekam viduḥ budhāḥ tayoḥ bahuvidha tvāt ca tattvam tu anyatra varṇitam te nava aṅge ubhe jñeye varṇite munibhiḥ priye varṇayāmi nava aṅgāni premṇaḥ śṛṇu dakṣa je śravaṇam kīrtanam ca eva smaraṇam tathā dāsyam tathā ca enam devi vandanam mama sarvadā sakhyam ātma arpaṇam ca iti nava aṅgāni viduḥ budhāḥ upāṅgāni śive tasyāḥ bahūni vai vai śṛṇu devi nava aṅgānām lakṣaṇāni pṛthak pṛthak mama bhaktyāḥ manaḥ da tvā bhukti mukti pradāni hi kathā ādeḥ nitya sanmānam kurva mudā sthira āsanena tat pānam yat tat śravaṇam ucyate hṛd ākāśena saṃpaśyan janma karmāṇi vai mama prītyā ucca uccāraṇam teṣām etat kīrtana su nirbhaya tvam sadā loke smaraṇam tat udāhṛtam sadā sevya ānukūlyena sevanam tat hi go gaṇaiḥ hṛdaya amṛta bhogena priyaṃdāsyam udāhṛtam parātmane bhūti ānukūlyena vidhinā mama parātmane arpaṇa ṣoḍaśānām vai pādya ādīnām tat acanam mantra uccāraṇa dhyānābhyām manasā vacasā kramāt aṣṭāṅgena bhūsparśaiḥ tat vai vadanam ucyate maṅgala amaṅgalam yat yat karoti iti īśvaraḥ hi mama sarvam tat maṅgalāya iti viśvāsaḥ sakhya lakṣaṇam priyāṇi ca atīva jñāna utpatti karāṇi ca upāṅgāni ca mad bhakte bahūni kathitāni vai bilva ādi sevana ādīni samūhyāni vicārāt sā sthitā nityam sarvadā mad priyaḥ trailokye bhakti sadṛśaḥ pathī na asti sukha āvahaḥ catur yugeṣu deveśi kalau tu su viśeṣataḥ bhāvāt aham nityam tad vaśī na atra saṃśayaḥ yaḥ bhaktimān sadā aham tad sahāya kṛt vighna hartā ripuḥ tasya daḍyaḥ na atra ca saṃśayaḥ mad śūlam gṛhītvā anvajayam purā bhakta hetoḥ aham devi rāvaṇam sa gaṇam krudhā tyajati sma kṛtaḥ na eva pakṣapātaḥ hi tasya vai śi0pu0 graham vyāsam hi kumati graham kāśyā nyasārayata krodhāt daṇḍayitvā ca nandinā kim bahu uktena deveśi bhakta adhīnaḥ sadā hi aham tad kartuḥ puruṣa sya ati vaśagaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ punar papraccha sat bhaktyā tad kāṇḍa viṣayam sune śāstram sukha karam loke jīva uddhāra parāyaṇam sa yantra mantra śāstram ca tad māhātmyam viśeṣataḥ anyāni dharma vastūni jīva uddhāra karāṇi hi tatra śāstram sa yantram hi sa pañcāṅgam maheśvaraḥ babhāṣe mahimānam ca tat tat deva varasya vai sa itihāsa katham teṣām bhakta māhātmyam eva ca īśvara śrama dharmāḥ ca muni īśvara suta strī dharma māhātmyam varṇa āśramam anaśvaram vaidya śāstram tathā jyotiḥśāstram jīva sukha āvaham param śāstram anyat śāstrāṇi bhūriśas kṛpām kṛtvā maheśānaḥ tattvāt dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīye satakhaṇḍe bhaktiprabhāvavarṇanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca prajānātha mahā prājña śrāvitam śaṃkara yaśaḥ satī śaṃkarayoḥ śubham idānīm brūhi sat prītyā param tat yaśaḥ uttamam tatas caritam dampatī śivau ca śṛṇu mama premṇaḥ mune laukikām gatim āśritya cikrīḍāte sadā anvaham mad bhoḥ an adatta deham tatyāja saṃgatā punar himālaye śaivā āvirbhūtā pārvatī iti śivam prāpa taptvā bhūri vi tat vacaḥ vāhataḥ tatas kim abhavat tatra kim akārṣīt maheśvaraḥ tat sarva me samācakṣva śraddhā yukta tad śrutau aham mune paramātmā para brahma saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ paramātmā para brahma saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ yam sadā bhajate śrīśaḥ ham ca api sakalāḥ surāḥ munayaḥ ca mahā ātmānaḥ siddhāḥ ca sanaka ādayaḥ śeṣaḥ sadā yaśaḥ yasya mudā gāyati nityaśas pāram na labhate tāta saḥ prabhuḥ śaṃkaraḥ śivaḥ bhavaḥ bhavaḥ vṛṣam āruhya līlā viśāradaḥ āgatya daṇḍaka araṇyam paryaṭan sāgarāmbarām ca tad prāptim pracchantam tad gatim hṛdā naṣṭa dhiyam atrapam śoka vihvalam sūrya vaṃśa udbhavam vīram bhūpam daśaratha ātmajam bharata ayajam ānanda rahitam vigata prabham pūrṇa kāmaḥ vara adhīnam mahā bhakta vatsalaḥ iti īdṛśām satīm dṛṣṭvā śiva līlām vimohanām su vismitā śivam prāha śiva māyā vimohitā uvāca yatnena nirvikārī para prabhuḥ kau imau puruṣau nāthaiḥ viraha vyākula ākṛtī vicarantau vane kiṣṭau dīnau vīrau dhanurdharau yajja śyāmam dṛṣṭvā vai kena hetunā su prasanna ātmā abhavaḥ bhaktaḥ iva adhunā māyā vaṃśī bhūtvā papraccha ittham śivam prabhum tat ākarṇya vacaḥ satyāḥ śaṃkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ tadā vihasya saḥ prāha satī līlā viśāradaḥ uvāca śṛṇu devi sati prītyā vacmi na chalam vara dāna prabhāvāt tu praṇāmam ca evam ādarāt rāma lakṣmaṇa nāmnau bhrātarau vīra saṃmatau sūrya vaṃśa udbhava devi prājñau daśaratha ātman naḥ iti uktvā virarāma asau śambhu smṛti karaḥ prabhuḥ śrutvā api ittham vacaḥ śambhoḥ na viśaśvāsa tad manaḥ tad vākya mohinī jñātvā uvāca śiva ājñayā satī tatra gatvā acintayat īśvarā kuryāt parīkṣām ca katham rāmasya vana cāriṇaḥ rūpam aham dhṛtvā gaccheyam rāma saṃnidhau yadi rāmaḥ hariḥ sarvam vijñāsyati na ca anyathā ittham vicārya sītā sā bhūtvā rāma samīpatas īrīkṣā arthī satī moha parāyaṇā sītā rūpam satīm dṛṣṭvā japan nām śiva iti ca vihasya tat pravijñāya natvā avocat raghūdvahaḥ uvāca tvam tyaktvā sva rūpam kasmāt te dhṛta rūpam idam satī brūhi tat kā devi kṛpām kṛtvā mama upari rāmam vijñāya viṣṇum tam sva rūpam saṃvidhāya ca smṛtvā śiva padam citte sati uvāca prasanna dhīḥ śivaḥ mayā gaṇaiḥ ca eva paryaṭan vasudhām prabhuḥ parameśvaraḥ iha agacchat ca vipine svatantraḥ parameśvaraḥ apaśyat atra saḥ tvām hi sītā anveṣaṇa tatparam sa lakṣmaṇam virahinam sītayā kliṣṭa mānasam mūle vaṭasya sthitaḥ evam hi śaṃsan mahimānam te vaiṣṇavam paramam yathā idam rūpam amalam paśyan ānandam āptavan tat śrutvā vacanam śambho mama ānīya cetasi tad ājñayā parīkṣā te kṛtavatī asmi rāghavaiḥ jñātam mama rāmaiḥ viṣṇuḥ tvam dṛṣṭā te prabhu tā akhilā niḥsaśaṃyā tadā api tat śṛṇu tvam ca mahāmate katham praṇamyaḥ tvam tasya satyam brūhi mama agratas tvam mām śamalam prāpnuhi drutam uvāca vacaḥ tasyāḥ phulla locanaḥ matyā vinā ājñayā śambhu samīpam na agaman sune saṃvarṇya mahimānam ca prāvocat rāghavaḥ tīm rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīye satī khaṇḍe rāmaparīkṣāvarṇanam nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca ekadā hi purā devi śambhuḥ parama siṃhāsanam varam tatra chattram mahā divyam sarvadā adbhutam uttamam kārayāmāsa vinā artham śaṃkaraḥ viśvakarmaṇā śakra ādīnām juhāva āśu samastān devatā gaṇān siddha gandharva nāga ādīn upadeśān ca kṛtsraśas devān sarvān āgamān ca vidhim putraiḥ munīn api devīḥ sarvāḥ apsarobhiḥ nānāve devānām ca tathā ṛṣīṇām siddhānām phaṇinām api ānayat maṅgala karāḥ kanyāḥ ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśa kārayāmāsa vādayitvā su gāyanaiḥ pratyakṣa tīrtha pāthobhiḥ pañca kumbhān ca pūritān tathā anyāḥ saṃvidhāḥ divyāḥ ānayat sva gaṇaiḥ tadā brahmaghoṣam mahā rāvam kārayāmāsa śaṃkaraḥ tad bhaktyā pūrṇayā devi modati sma maheśvaraḥ su muhūrte mahādevaḥ tatra siṃhāsane vare upaveśya harim prītyā bhūṣayāmāsa sarvaśas ca na ejam na anya gāmi yat na ejam na anya gāmi tatas tuṣṭāva tam śambhuḥ svatantraiḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ brahmānam lokakartāram avocat vacanam tu idam vara adhīnam svatantram bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca atas prabhṛti lokeśaiḥ mad nideśāt ayam hariḥ mama vaṃdyaḥ svayam viṣṇuḥ jātaḥ sarva śṛṇoti hi tatas maheśaḥ tadā tatas maheśaḥ tadā su prasannaḥ dhṛtavan bhakta vatsalaḥ bhartā hartā mad ājñayā bhartā hartā mad ājñayā dātā dharma artha kāmānām śāstā durṇaya kāriṇām jagadīśaḥ jagat pūjyaḥ mahā bala parākramaḥ ajeyaḥ tvam raṇe kvāpi mama api hi bhaviṣyasi śakti trayam gṛhāṇa tvam icchā ādi prāpitam mayā nānā līlā prabhāva tvam svatantra tvam bhavat traye veṣṭāraḥ hare mayā śāsyāḥ prayatnāt tvad bhaktānām mayā viṣṇo deyam nirvāṇam uttamam māyām ca api gṛhaṇa imām duṣpraṇodyām sura ādibhiḥ mama bāhuḥ madīyaḥ tvam dakṣiṇā usau vidhire asya api hi vidheḥ pātā jane bhaviṣyasi na śi0pu0 tān apya nijāt varāt tadā prabhṛti lakṣmīśaḥ gopa veṣaḥ bhavat tathā ayāsīt tatra su prītyā gopa gopī gavām patiḥ saḥ api viṣṇuḥ prasanna ātmā jugopa nikhilam jagant nānā avatāraḥ saṃghartā vana kartā śiva ājñayā idānīm sa caturddhātrau atarat śaṃkara ājñayā rāmaḥ uham tatra bharataḥ lakṣmaṇaḥ śatru hā iti ca atha pitṛ ājñayā devi sa sītā lakṣmaṇaḥ sati āgataḥ ham vane duḥkhitaḥ daivataḥ abhavam anveṣyāmi priyām ca atra virahī bandhunā vane mahat bhāgyam mama adya eva kṛpām yuvam sa karuṇau syātām sa dhanyaḥ puruṣaḥ varaḥ ittham ābhāṣya bahudhā su praṇamya satīm śivām tad ājñayā vane tasmin vicacāra raghūdvahaḥ atha ākarṇya satī vākyam rāmasya prayata ātmanaḥ hṛṣṭā abhūt sā praśaṃsantam śiva bhakti ratam hṛdi mad rāma prati kudhīḥ tadā kim uttaram aham dāsye gatvā śaṃkara saṃnidhau iti saṃcintya bahudhā paścāt tapaḥ bhavat tadā gatvā śambhu samīpam ca praṇanāma śivam hṛdā viṣaṇṇa vadanā śoka vyākulā vigata prabhā atha tām duḥkhitām dṛṣṭvā papraccha kuśalam haraḥ provāca vacanam prītyā tad parīkṣā kṛtā katham mahat kim api praṇata ānanā satī śoka viṣaṇṇā sā tasthau tatra samīpatas hṛdā dakṣa jāyā mahā yogī nānā līlā viśāradaḥ sasmāra sva paṇam pūrvam yat kṛtam hari kopāt tad prārthitā utha rudraḥ asau maryādā prati mahān hi sneham pūrvam yathā mahān naśyet paṇaḥ śuddhaḥ loka līlā anusāriṇaḥ mad paṇam na nāśayāmāsa veda dharma prapālakaḥ hi tam vyomavāṇī uvāca maheśvaram tam vyomavāṇī uvāca maheśvaram sarvān śrāvayan tatra dakṣajām ca viśeṣataḥ viprabhā kam kṛtavan nāthaiḥ brūhi mama parameśvaraiḥ iti pṛṣṭaḥ api giriśaḥ satyā hita karaḥ prabhuḥ na udvāham svam paṇam tasyai kaharyaye akarot purā tadā satī śivam dhyātvā sva patim prāṇa vallabham sarvam buvodha hetum tam priya tyāga mayam sune tatas atīva śuśoca āśu budhvā sā ātmanaḥ śambhunā dakṣa jāyā tvāt niśvasatī muhur muhur śivaḥ tasyāḥ samājñāya guptam cakre manobhavam satyai paṇam svakīyam hi kathāḥ bahīḥ vai prabhuḥ satyā prāp sa kailāsam kathayan vividhāḥ kathāḥ vare sthitvā nijam rūpam yogī samādhi bhṛt ā mad śivam devī hṛdayena vidūyatā āsanam dattavan śambhuḥ sva sammukhaḥ udāra dhīḥ kathayāmāsa su prītyā kathāḥ bahīḥ manā ramāḥ kṛta sadyas līlām kṛtvā ca tādṛśām pūrvavat sā mukham lebhe tatyāja sva paṇam namaḥ na iti āścarye śive tātaiḥ maṃtavyam parameśvare śivā muni śiva kathām vadanti munayaḥ om mune kila kecid avidvasaḥ viyogaḥ ca katham tayoḥ kila kecid avidvasaḥ viyogaḥ ca katham tayoḥ śiva aśiva caritram kaḥ jānāti paramārthāt icchayā bhāgavate mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīye satīkhaṇḍe saṃtīviyogaḥ nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca purā bhavat ca sarveṣām adhvaraḥ vidhinā mahān prayāge samavetānām munīnām ca mahātmanām tatra siddhāḥ samākhyātāḥ sanaka ādyāḥ sura ṛṣayaḥ sa prajāpatayaḥ devāḥ jñāninaḥ brahma darśiṇaḥ tatra nānā śāstra samudbhavaḥ tasmin avasare rudraḥ sa bhavānī gaṇaḥ prabhuḥ triloka hita kṛt svāmī tatra agāt sūkti kṛt mune dṛṣṭvā śivam surā sarve siddhāḥ ca munayaḥ tathā anamastam prabhum bhaktyā tuṣṭuvuḥ ca tathā hi aham tasthuḥ śiva ājñayā sarve yathāsthānam mudā anvitāḥ prabhu darśana saṃtuṣṭāḥ brahmāṇḍa adhipatiḥ mānyaḥ mānī tatra mad ājñayā brahmāṇḍa adhipatiḥ mānyaḥ mānī tattva bahirmukhaḥ stutibhiḥ praṇipātaiḥ ca dakṣaḥ sarvaiḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ pūjitaḥ vara tejasvī tau karau badhvā vinamrakaiḥ nānā vihāra kṛt nāthaḥ svatantraḥ parama ūti kṛt nānamat tam tadā dakṣam sva āsana sthaḥ maheśvaraḥ dṛṣṭvā ānatam haram tatra saḥ mama putraḥ aprasanna dhīḥ akupat sahasā rudre tadā dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ krūra dṛṣṭyā mahāgavaiḥ dṛṣṭvā rudram mahā prabhum sarvān saṃśrāvayan uccais avocat jñā yaḥ tu abhūt tu yaḥ bhūta piśāca saṃvṛtaḥ mākhaṇḍinaḥ durjana pāpa śīlāḥ dṛṣṭvā dvijam proddhata nindakāḥ ca badhvam sadā āsakta rati pravīṇaḥ tasmāt ayum pravṛttaḥ bahiṣkṛtaḥ mama varṇeṣu atītaḥ yaiḥ vivarṇa rūpaḥ devaiḥ na bhāgam labhatām saha eva śmaśāna vāsī kula janma hīnaḥ pa mad akṣa ūti ruṣā anvitaḥ abravīt tvaritam dakṣam śāpam dātu manāḥ gaṇaḥ nandīśvaraḥ uvāca re re śaṭhaiḥ mahā mūḍhaiḥ dakṣaiḥ duṣṭa mate tvayā mama svāmī maheśaḥ hi kṛtaḥ katham brahma cāpalyāt śata uyam dakṣaiḥ durmate vṛthak upahasitaḥ ca eva aduṣṭaḥ rudraḥ mahā prabhuḥ yena idam pālyate viśvaiḥ sṛṣṭam ante vināśitam śaptaḥ yam sa katham rudraḥ adhamaiḥ hi ca śaśāpa atha dakṣaḥ roṣa samanvitaḥ uvāca bhavantu bhasma asthi dhāriṇaḥ pratyuvāca drutam dakṣam garvitam tam mahā khalam śilāda tanayaḥ nandī tejasvī śiva vallabhaḥ uvāca re dakṣa śaṭha durbuddhe vṛthak eva karāḥ śaptāḥ te brahma cāpalyāt śiva tattvam a jānatā bhṛgu ādyaiḥ duṣṭa cittaiḥ ca mūḍhaiḥ saḥ upahāsitaḥ mahā prabhu maheśānaḥ brāhmaṇa tvāt ahaṃmate atra dadāmi puraskṛtya brāhmaṇāḥ śūdra yājinaḥ daridrāḥ vai bhaviṣyati pratigraha ratāḥ sadā ca eva sarve niraya gāminaḥ bhaviṣyanti sadā dakṣa hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt śaptaḥ dakṣeṇa ca īśvaraḥ tat ākarṇya aham atyantam anindam tam muhu muhur bhṛgu ādīn api viprān ca veda sṛj śiva tattva vid īśvaraḥ api vacaḥ śrutvā nandinaḥ prahasan iva uvāca madhuram vākyam bodhayan tam sadāśivaḥ uvāca śṛṇu nandin mahā prājñaiḥ na kartum krodham arhasi vṛthak śaptaḥ brahma kulaḥ matvā śatam ca mām bhramāt ramaya sākṣāt sūkta mayaḥ bhṛśam sūkte pratiṣṭhitaḥ hi ātmā sarveṣām api dehinām tasmāt ātma vidaḥ nityam tvam mā śapa ruṣā anvitaḥ śapyāḥ na vedāḥ yajña aṅgāni ca sarvaśas yajña ātmā yajña nirataḥ yajña vāhyaḥ ūham eva vai kaḥ iyam kaḥ tvā eme ke hi sarvaḥ ūham api tattvāt iti buddhayā hi vimṛśa evam prabodhitaḥ tena śambhunā nandikeśvaraḥ viveka paramaḥ bhūtvā śāntaḥ abhūt krodha varjitaḥ śivaḥ api tam prabodhya āśu sva gaṇam prāṇa vallabham sa gaṇaḥ sa yayau tasmāt sva sthānam pramudā anvitaḥ dakṣaḥ api saḥ ruṣā āviṣṭaḥ taiḥ dvijaiḥ parivāritaḥ sva sthānam ca yayau citte śiva droha parāyaṇaḥ rudram tadānīm pariśapyamānam saṃsmṛtya dakṣaḥ parayā rūpa anvitaḥ śraddhām vihāya eva saḥ mūḍha buddhiḥ dakṣa durbuddhiḥ śambhunā paramātmanā tasya śṛṇu tātaiḥ vadāmi aham khaṇḍe satyupākhyāne śivena dakṣavirodhaḥ nāma ṣaḍaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tāḥ tadā sarve dīkṣitena sura ṛṣayaḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ akhilān tatra nirjarāḥ ca samāgatāḥ yad yajña karaṇa artham hi śiva māyā vimohitaḥ kaśya vāmadevaḥ tathā bhṛguḥ dadhīciḥ bhagavān vyāsaḥ bhāradvājaḥ atha gautamaḥ pailaḥ parāśaraḥ gargaḥ bhārgavaḥ kakupaḥ sitaḥ mahodayāḥ sarve stropakāra bala anvitāḥ sarve stropakāra bala anvitāḥ satya lokāt samānītaḥ viśva kārakaḥ yutaḥ vaikuṃṭhāt ca tathā viṣṇuḥ saṃprārthyam vividha ādarāt sa pārṣada parīvāraḥ samānī makham prati evam anye samāyātāḥ dakṣa yajñam vimohitāḥ satkṛtāḥ tena dakṣeṇa sarve te hi durātmanā bhavanāni suprabhāni ca tvaṣṭrā kṛtāni divyāni tebhyaḥ dattāni tena vai teṣu sarveṣu dhiṣṇyeṣu yathāyogyam ca saṃsthitāḥ sat mānitāḥ arājan te sakalāḥ viṣṇunā mayā kṛtāḥ tena sagva ādyāḥ ca tapodhanāḥ dikpālāḥ dvārapālāḥ ca rakṣakāḥ sa āyudhāḥ sa parīvārāḥ kutūhala karāḥ sadā tad śreṣṭhāḥ svayam veda dharāḥ abhavan tanūnapāt api nijam cakre rūpam sahasraśas haviṣām grahaṇāya āśu tasmin yajñe mahā utsave maha astrāṇi juhvati saha ṛtvijaḥ udgātāraḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi sura ṛṣayaḥ udgātāraḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi sura ṛṣayaḥ adhvaryavaḥ tha hotāraḥ tāvantaḥ nārada ādayaḥ saptarṣayaḥ samāḥ gāthāḥ kuvaiti dvijarṣi rājarṣi surarṣi saṃdhāḥ nṛpāḥ sa mitrāḥ sacivāḥ sa sainyāḥ vasu pramukhyāḥ gaṇadevatāḥ ca sarve vṛtāḥ tena makha upavetrāḥ tasmin yajñe vṛtaḥ śambho na dakṣeṇa durātmanā tasya yajña arha tā na hi eti api ca na āhūtā yajña viṣaye dakṣeṇa a guṇa darśiṇā dakṣa yajñe mahā utsave sva kārya lagnāḥ tatra āsan sarve te adhvara saṃmatāḥ etasmin antare tatra dṛṣṭvā vai śaṃkaram prabhum progri mānasaḥ śaivaḥ abravīt śru mad vākyam deva ṛṣi pramukhāḥ mudā kasmāt na eva āgataḥ yajñe mahā utsave sureśā sunayaḥ mahattarāḥ sa lokapālāḥ ca samāgatāḥ hi tathā api na śobhate bhṛśam pinākinā tena mahātmanā vinā maṅgalāni bhavati śaṃsanti mahā vipaścitaḥ saḥ asau na dṛṣṭaḥ utra pumān purāṇaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ nīlagalaḥ para īśaḥ amaṅgalāni eva ca maṅgalāni bhavanti yena adhigatāni dakṣaḥ tripañcakena api atha maṅgalāni bhavati sadyas paratas purāṇi yatra devaḥ maheśvaraḥ dākṣāyiṇyā samam śambhum ānayadhvam tvarā anvitāḥ tena sarva pavitram syāt śambhunā paramātmanā tasmāt sarva prayatnena śaṃkare uvāca tvaritam mūḍhaḥ prahasan iva duṣṭa dhīḥ mūlam viṣṇuḥ devatānām yatra dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ samānītaḥ mayā samyak yajña karmaṇi yajñāḥ ca karmāṇi vividhāni ca pratiṣṭhitāni sarvāṇi saḥ asau viṣṇuḥ iha āgataḥ satya lokāt samāyātaḥ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ tathā sura gaṇaiḥ sa upaniṣadbhiḥ ca vividhaiḥ āgamaiḥ saha tathā sura gaṇaiḥ sa gataḥ surarāj svayam tathā yūyam samāyātāḥ ṛṣayaḥ vīta almaṣāḥ mahā jña ucitāḥ śāntāḥ pātra bhūtāḥ samāgatāḥ veda veda artha tattva jñāḥ sarve yūyam dṛḍha vratāḥ atra eva ca kim naḥ rudreṇa api prayojanam mayā vipraiḥ brahmaṇā na uditena hi hi haras akulīnaḥ asau vipraiḥ pitṛ mātṛ vivarjitaḥ bhūta preta piśācānām patiḥ ekaḥ duratyayaḥ mūḍha stambdhaḥ maunī sa matsaraḥ karmaṇi asmin na yogyaḥ asau na ānītaḥ hi mayā adhunā tasmāt tvam īdṛśam vākyam punar vācyam na hi kvacid sarvaiḥ bhavadbhiḥ kartavyaḥ yajñaḥ mama saphalaḥ mahān saṃyutam muktvā dadhīcaḥ usau ekaḥ eva vinirgataḥ yajña vāṭāt ca dakṣasya tvaritaḥ sva āśramam yayaiau mān sadyas śāpam dattvā tathā eva ca sunau vinirgate tasmin makhāt anyeṣu duṣṭa dhīḥ śiva drohī munīn dakṣaḥ prahasan idam abravīt uvāca gataḥ śivapriyaḥ vipraḥ dadhīcaḥ nāma nāmnaḥ anye tathāvidhāḥ ye ca gatāḥ te mama ca adhvarāt etat śubhataram jātaiḥ saṃmatam sarvathā satyam bravīmi deveśaiḥ surāḥ ca munayaḥ tathā vinaṣṭa cittāḥ mandāḥ ca mithyā vāda ratāḥ khalāḥ veda bāhyāḥ durācārāḥ tyājyāḥ te makhaiḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ procyate śṛṇu sādaram śi0pu0 parivāritā dākṣāyaṇī mahā krīḍāḥ cakāra vividhāḥ tī krīḍā saktā tadā devī dadarśa atha mudā satī prayātam ca sa tvaram tvaram tam atha ākarṇya sva yātrām pūrvam ādarāt bhasmasātkuru satvaram tatra astu viṣṇuḥ brahmā vā śacīśaḥ vā yadi astu viṣṇu astu viṣṇu astu viṣṇu astu v iti uktaḥ roṣa tāmra akṣaḥ veda maryādā pālakaḥ virarāma mahā vīram kālāriḥ sakala īśvaraḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīye satīkhaṇḍe vīrabhadrotpattiśivopadeśavarṇanam nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāca iti uktam śrī maheśasya śrutvā vacanam ādarāt vīrabhadra ūti saṃtuṣṭaḥ praṇanāma maheśvaram śāsanam śirasā dhṛtvā devadevasya śūlinaḥ bhadraḥ makham prati pracacāla tatas śīghram vīrabhadraḥ makham prati śivā utha preṣayāmāsa śobhā artham koṭiśas gaṇān tena sārdham mahā vīrān pralaya anala saṃnibhān atha te vīrabhadrasya puratas prabalāḥ gaṇāḥ paścāt api yayu varāḥ kutūhala karāḥ gaṇāḥ vīrabhadra sametāḥ ye gaṇāḥ śata sahasraśas pārṣadāḥ kāla kālasya yayau dakṣa vināśāya sarva bhūta gaṇaiḥ saha ḍākinī śākinī ca eva bhūtapramathaiḥ guhyakāḥ kūṣmāṇḍāḥ parpaṭāḥ ca eva caṭakāḥ brahmarākṣasāḥ bhairavāḥ kṣetrapālāḥ ca dakṣa yajña vināśakāḥ niryayuḥ tvaritam vīrāḥ śiva ājñā pratipā tathā eva yoginī cakram catuḥṣaṣṭi gaṇa anvitam niryayau sahasā kruddham dakṣa yajñam vināśitum teṣām gaṇānām sarveṣām saṃkhyānam nārad mahā balavatām saṃghaḥ mukhyānām dhairya śālinām abhyayāt śaṅkukarṇaḥ ca daśa koṭyā gaṇeśvaraḥ kekarām mahā akṣaḥ ca vikṛta uṣṭābhiḥ eva ca viśākhaḥ ca navabhiḥ pāriyātrikaḥ vīraḥ tathā evam vikṛta ānanaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ koṭibhiḥ gaṇa puṃgavaḥ saptabhiḥ samadat jīmān dudrabha uṣṭābhiḥ eva ca pañcabhiḥ ca kapālī īśaḥ ṣaṭvis saṃdārakaḥ gaṇaḥ ca koṭi koṭibhiḥ eva iha koṭikuṇḍaḥ tathā eva ca viṣṭabhoṣṭa aṣṭabhiḥ vīraiḥ koṭibhiḥ gaṇa saptamaḥ sahasra koṭibhiḥ tātaiḥ śaṃnādaḥ pippalaḥ tathā āveśanaḥ tathā aṣṭābhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ candratāpanaḥ mahāveśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭyāḥ gaṇapaḥ vṛtaḥ kuṇḍī dvādaśa koṭibhiḥ tathā parvatakaḥ mune vināśitum dakṣa yajñam niryayau gaṇa sattamaḥ kālaḥ ca kālakaḥ ca eva mahākālaḥ tathā eva ca koṭīnām śatakena eva dakṣa yajñam yayau prati mūrdhā kṛt śata koṭyā ca koṭyā agnimukhaḥ eva ca vṛṣabhaḥ tathā sumantrakaḥ gaṇādhīśaḥ tathā tātaiḥ suniryayau kākapādodaraḥ ṣaṣṭi koṭibhiḥ gaṇa sattamaḥ tathā saṃtānakaḥ ṣaṣṭi koṭibhiḥ geṇa puṃgavaḥ mahābalaḥ ca navabhiḥ koṭibhiḥ puṃgavaḥ tathā madhupiṅgaḥ tathā tātaiḥ gaṇādhīśaḥ hi niryayau nīsaḥ navatyā koṭīnām pūrṇabhadraḥ tathā eva ca niryayau śata koṭībhiḥ caturvakaḥ gaṇādhipaḥ hāgūḍhaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā sukeśaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ tathā virūpākṣaḥ ca koṭīnām catuḥṣaṣṭyā gaṇeśvaraḥ gaṇādhipaḥ saṃvartakaḥ tathā ca eva kulīśaḥ ca svayam prabhuḥ loka antakaḥ ca dīpta ātmā tathā daitya antakaḥ mune gaṇaḥ bhṛṅgīriṭiḥ devadeva priyaḥ tathā hi abhyayāt vīraḥ vīrabhadraḥ śiva ājñayā bhūta koṭi sahasraiḥ tu prayayau kauṭibhiḥ tribhiḥ roma jaiḥ śva gaṇaiḥ ca eva tathā vīraḥ yayau drutam mukhāḥ ca eva śṛṅgāṇi vividhāni ca te tāni vitatāni eva bandhanāni sukhāni ca vāditrāṇi vineduḥ ca vividhāni mahā utsave dvitīye satī khaṇḍe vīrabhadrayātrāvarṇanam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ brahmā uvāca evam pracalite ca asmin vīrabhadre gaṇa anvite dakṣeṇa dṛṣṭāni vibudhaiḥ api dakṣeṇa dṛṣṭāni vibudhaiḥ api utpātāḥ vividha āśvāsana vīrabhadre gaṇa anvite trividhāḥ api deva ṛṣe yajña vidhvaṃsa sūcakāḥ bāhu ūru vispandaḥ samajāyata nānā kaṣṭa pradaḥ tātaiḥ sarvathā aśubha sūcakaḥ samabhūt tatra dakṣa yāga sthale tadā madhyāhne nakṣatrāṇi adbhutāni ca diśaḥ ca asan su malināḥ karburaḥ bhūt divākaraḥ pariveṣa sahasreṇa saṃkrāntaḥ ca bhayaṃkaraḥ patanti mahā vidyut agni prabhāni ca nakṣatrāṇām abhūt hakā tadā maṇḍapaḥ vavāśire yāga bhūmau kroṣṭāraḥ netrakaḥ tadā ulkā vṛṣṭiḥ abhūt tatra śveta vṛścika sambhavā kharāḥ vātāḥ vavuḥ tatra pāṃśu vṛṣṭi samanvitāḥ samudbhūtāḥ vivarta anila kampitāḥ rītaiḥ ca pavanaiḥ ūrdhva saḥ dakṣa adhvara maṇḍapaḥ deva anvitena dakṣeṇa yaḥ kṛtaḥ nūtana udbhutaḥ hakṣa ādayaḥ sarve tadā aśoṇitam adbhutam vemuḥ ca māṃsa khaṇḍāni sa śalyāni muhur muhur sa kampāḥ ca babhūvuḥ te dīpāḥ vāta hatāḥ iva sarve śastra dhārā āhatāḥ iva tadā nināda jātāni vāṣpa varṣāṇi tad kṣaṇe prātar tuṣāra varṣāṇi padmāni iva vana antare dakṣa ādi akṣīṇi jātāni tasmāt viśadāni api niśāyām kamalāḥ ca eva kumudāni iva saṃgave asṛj vavarṣa timireṇa āvṛtāḥ diśaḥ digdāhaḥ bhūt viśeṣeṇa trāsayan sakala añjanān evaṃvidhāni ariṣṭāni dadṛśuḥ vibudha ādayaḥ bhayam āpedire atyantam mune viṣṇu ādikāḥ tadā bhuvi te mūrchitāḥ petuḥ hām hatāḥ sma īrayan taravaḥ tīra saṃjātāḥ nadī vega hatāḥ iva patitvā te sthitāḥ bhūmau krūrāḥ sarpāḥ sva sva upakaṇṭham ākaṇṭham luluṭhuḥ kamaṭhāḥ iva etasmin antare tatra saṃjātā ca aśarīra vāc śrāvayati akhilān devān dakṣam ca eva viśeṣataḥ pāpa vāṇī uvāca janma te dakṣaiḥ adya pāpa dhīḥ bhaviṣyati mahā duḥkham a nivārya hara udbhavam mūḍhāḥ tava deva ādayaḥ sthitāḥ teṣām api mahā duḥkham bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ca dakṣaḥ prāpat bhayam ca ati pare deva ādayaḥ api ha vepamānaḥ tadā dakṣaḥ cetasi agacchat śaraṇam viṣṇoḥ sva prabhoḥ indirā pateḥ su praṇamya bhaya āviṣṭaḥ saṃstūyam ca vicetanaḥ avocat devadevam tam viṣṇum sva jana vatsalam iti śrī śiva mahāpurī dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām dvitīyesatīkhaṇḍe duśśakunadarśanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ mama rakṣā vidhātavyā bhaktā sādhvarasya ca mama rakṣā vidhātavyā bhaktā sa adhvarasya ca rakṣakaḥ tvam makhasya eva makha karmā makha ātmakaḥ vidhe yā yajñasya bhaṅgaḥ bhavatu na prabho kṛ kṛtvā vijñaptim ādarāt papāta pādayoḥ tasya bhaya vyākula mānasaḥ utthāpya tam tatas viṣṇuḥ dakṣam vikinna mānasam śrutvā ca tasya tat vākyam kumateḥ asmarat śivam smṛtvā śivam maheśānam sva prabhum parame harim avadat śiva tattva jñaḥ dakṣam saṃbodhayan hariḥ uvāca hi kṛtā dakṣaiḥ tvayā tattvam a jānatā avajñā hi kṛtā dakṣaiḥ tvayā tattvam tadā śivaḥ kevalam jñānam āśritya nirīśvara pare narāḥ nirayam te ca gacchanti kalpa koṭi śatāni ca saṃbhūtaḥ samāyāta udhvara aṅgaṇe mām idam sarvān dhruvam eva mahā prabhuḥ tatas praśānta hṛdayaḥ asmi aham kāla traye api mām cakram īdṛśam a saṃhatya eva sahasā kṛpayā eva sthiram param samākulam vīrabhadraḥ pūjitaḥ api śīghram asmābhiḥ ādarāt mahā krodha samākrāṃtaḥ na asmān saṃrakṣayiṣyati api yama yātanāḥ śakyate soḍhum bahu duḥkha pradāyinīḥ śiva drohinam ālokya dṛṣṭa dantaḥ yamaḥ svayam tapta tela kaṭāheṣu pāntayatu eva na anyathā gantum eva aham udyuktam sarvathā śapatha uttaram tathā api na gantar śīcam duṣṭa saṃsarga pāpāt kriyate smābhiḥ palāyanam itas tadā kriyate smābhiḥ palāyanam itas tadā karṣakaḥ śastraiḥ asmān ākarṣayiṣyati svarge vā bhuvi pātāle yatra kutra api vā yatas manam na hi durlabham ravaḥ kāśau nakha agreṇa eva līlayā purā śiraḥ ciccheda pañcamam brahmanaḥ dhruvam etat uktvā sthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ atitrasta mukha ambujaḥ saṃprāpa tadā eva adhvara maṇḍapam eva svāni svāni pratāpinaḥ teṣām udyogam ālokya dakṣaḥ ca amṛṅmukhaḥ tathā tad antikam samāgatya sa kalatraḥ abhyabhāṣata tvad balena eva mayā yajñaḥ prāraṃbhitaḥ mahān sat karma siddhaye yūyam sarvathā nirvikārayā tad anugrahāt nūnam jñātavyaḥ hi sadāśivaḥ param tu saṃvadiṣyāmi kārya akārya vivakṣitau sidhi aṃśam sa ca sureśāna tam śṛṇu tvam hitāya vai tvam indra bāliśaḥ bhūtvā lokapālaiḥ saha adya vai āgataḥ dakṣa yajñam hi kim kariṣyasi vikramam ete rudra sahāyāḥ ca gaṇāḥ parama kopanāḥ āgatāḥ yajña vighna artham tam kariṣyam asaṃśayam sarvathā na hi upāyaḥ utra keṣāṃcid api tattvāt indra ādīn lokapālān tān smṛtvā manasi śaṃkaram uvāca prayacchāmi āgacchata mamatikam he śakra he śuce bhāno he śaśin he dhanādhipa he pāśa pāṇe he vāyo nirṛte yamaiḥ śeṣaiḥ he he sura asura saṃghāḥ ca ca vicakṣaṇāḥ avadānāni dāsyāmi ātṛptyā adya asatām varām anvitaḥ nikhilān tān surān sadyas vīrabhadraḥ gaṇa agraṇī taiḥ vāṇaiḥ nihatāḥ sarve vāsava ādyāḥ sura īśvarāḥ palāyana pare bhūtvā jagmuḥ te ca diśaḥ daśa gateṣu lokapāleṣu vidruteṣu sureṣu ca hi hi vīrabhadra ugamat guṇaiḥ tadā te ṛṣayaḥ sarve subhītāḥ hi maheśvaraiḥ m śīghram ūcuḥ natāḥ bhṛśam devadeva ramānātha sarveśvara mahā prabho hite rataḥ tatas provāca sādaram śiva bhaktaḥ ati śuddha ātmā nirvikāraḥ prasanna dhīḥ saḥ phalam prāptavan adya sva rājyam hi karotu saḥ mātuḥ ājñā vaśāt rahman kṛtam etat mayā akhilam na mama bhoga
