jvalam pāpīyāḥ iti śeṣaḥ śakra viṣṇū iti bhāvaḥ yāvat triśūleṇa tadā haṃtu kāmaḥ mahā balaḥ vīrabhadraḥ asuram yāvat kumāreṇa nivāritaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām caturthe kumāra khaṇḍe tārakavākyaśakaviṣṇuvīrabhadrayuddhavarṇanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca nivārya vīrabhadram tam kumāraḥ para vīra hā samaicchat tārakavadham smṛtvā saṃstutaḥ vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ tadā eva ca sura ṛṣibhiḥ tārakasya kumārasya saṃgrāmaḥ atīva dussaṃhaḥ jātaḥ tadā mahā ghoraḥ sarva bhūta bhayaṃkaraḥ siṃhau iva mahā balau samāśritya tathā matam ca samāśritya śaktyā śaktim vijannatuḥ madbhutam anyonyam sādhakau bhūtvā mahā bala parākramau mahā balam paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ viśāradau vāṇī jagau devān ca sāṃtvayan asuram tārakam ca atra kumāraḥ ayam haniṣyati mā śocyatām suraiḥ sava sukhena sthīyatām iti hi putra rūpeṇa saṃsthitaḥ śrutvā tadā tām gagane samīritām vācam śubhām sa pramathaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ nihaṃtu kāmaḥ sukhitaḥ kumārakaḥ daitya adhipam tārakaiḥ māśu abhūt tadā śaktyā tayā mahā bāddurājaghāna stanāṃtare kumāraḥ sma ruṣā āviṣṭaḥ tāraka asuram ojasā tam prahāram an āhṛtya tārako hanta daitya puṃgavaḥ kumāram ca api saṃkruddhaḥ sva śaktyā saṃjaghāna saḥ tena śakti prahāreṇa śāṃkariḥ mūcchitaḥ abhavat a muhūrtāt cetanām prāpa stūyamānaḥ maha yathā siṃhaḥ mada unmattaḥ hantu kāmaḥ tathā asuram kumāraḥ tārakam śaktyā saḥ jaghāna pratāpavān evam parasparam tau hi kumāraiḥ mad api tārakaḥ yuyudhāte atisaṃdhau śakti yuddha viśāradau abhyāsa paramau āstām anyonyam vijigīṣayā padātinaḥ citra rūpau etasmin antare tatra himālaya mukhāḥ gharāḥ sneha arditāḥ tadā jagmuḥ kumāram ca parīpsavaḥ tatas saḥ dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān bhaya bhītān ca śāṃkariḥ pu0 paribodhayan parvatān girijā putraḥ babhāṣe paribodhayan uvāca mā khidyatām mahābhāgāḥ mā ciṃtām kurvatām nagāḥ ghātayāmi adya pāpiṣṭham sarveṣām prapaśyatām evam samāśvāsya tadā parvatān nirjarān gaṇān praṇamya girijām śambhum ādade śaktim utprabhām tam tārakam haṃtu manāḥ tejasā āḍhyaḥ śaṃkarasya tam tam papāta sadyas sahasā viśīrṇa aṅgaḥ asuraḥ kṣitau tāraka ākhyaḥ mahā vīraḥ sarva asura gaṇa adhipaḥ kumāreṇa hataḥ sotivīraḥ sa tārakaḥ layam yayau ca tatra eva sarveṣām paśyatām mune tathā tam patitam dṛṣṭvā tārakam balavattaram na punar varaḥ saḥ gatvā vyasum āhave hate tasmin mahā daitye tāraka ākhye mahā bale kṣayam praṇītāḥ bahavaḥ asurāḥ deva gaṇaiḥ tadā hatāḥ daityāḥ sa añjalayaḥ tadā hatāḥ tatra kiyantaḥ ca palāyitāḥ palāyamānāḥ vyathitāḥ tāḍitāḥ nirjaraiḥ gaṇaiḥ saha sraśas praviṣṭāḥ te pātāle ca jijīṣavaḥ palāyamānāḥ te sarve bhagna āśāḥ dainyam āgatāḥ evam daitya sainyam bhraṣṭam jātam muni īśvaraiḥ mad kacid tatra saṃtasthuḥ guṇa deva bhayāt tadā āsīt niṣkaṇṭakam sarve hate tasmin durātmani te devāḥ sukham āpannāḥ sarve śakra ādayaḥ tadā evam vijayam āpannam kumāram nikhilāḥ surāḥ babhūvuḥ yugapad hṛṣṭāḥ tri lokāḥ ca mahā sukhāḥ tadā śivaḥ api tam jñātvā vijayam kārtti tatra ājagāma saḥ mudā sa gaṇaḥ priyayā saha sva ātmajam sva aṅkam āropya kumāram sūrya varcasam lālayāmāsa su prītyā śivā ca saṃkulā himālayaḥ tadā āgatya sva putraiḥ parivāritaḥ sa bandhuḥ sa anugaḥ śambhum tuṣṭāva ca śivām guham tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve munayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ śāṃkarim śambhum girijām tuṣitām bhṛśam puṣpa vṛṣṭim su mahatīm cakruḥ ca upasurāḥ tadā jaguḥ gandharva patayaḥ nanṛtuḥ śva apsaras gaṇāḥ hari neduḥ tadānīm ca viśeṣataḥ jaya śabdaḥ namaḥ śabdaḥ babhūva uccais muhur muhur tatas mayā acyutaḥ ca api saṃtuṣṭaḥ bhūt viśeṣataḥ hi śivam śivām kumāram ca saṃtuṣṭāva samādarāt kumāram agratas kṛtvā hari kendra mukhāḥ surāḥ cakruḥ nīrājanam prītyā munayaḥ ca apare tathā mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām caturthe kumārakhaṇḍe tārakāsuravadhadevotsavavarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatra tatra ājagāma kumārasya śaraṇam bāṇa pīḍitaḥ palāyamānaḥ yaḥ yuddhāt asoḍhā tejaḥ aiśvaram tutoda atīva saḥ kau pratipatya kumārasya saḥ bhaktyā caraṇa ambujam pratipatya kumārasya saḥ bhaktyā caraṇa ambujam prema nirbharayā vācā tuṣṭāva guham ādarāt māra skanda deveśa tāraka asura nāśaka pāhi mām śaraṇa āpannam bāṇa asura nipīḍitam saṃgarāte mahā sena samucchinnaḥ palāyitaḥ nyapīḍayat ca māgadhaiḥ hā nātha karuṇākara hā nātha karuṇākara tad pīḍitaḥ te śaraṇam āgataḥ aham su duḥkhitaḥ palāyamānaḥ deveśaiḥ śara janman dayām kuru daityam tam nāśaya vibho bāṇa āhvam mām sukhīkuru daitya naḥ tvam viśeṣeṇa devāvana karaḥ svarāj mahā śaktim atulām svām sasmāra śivaḥ dhyā cikṣepa tām samuddiśya saḥ bāṇam śaṃkara ātmajaḥ mahā śabdaḥ vabhūva atha jajvaluḥ ca diśaḥ nabhaḥ sabalam bhasmasātkṛtvā asuram tam kṣaṇa mātrāt guhā upakaṇṭham śaktiḥ sā ājagāma paramā sune tatas kumāraḥ provāca krauñcam giri varam prabhuḥ tatas skandaḥ maheśasya mudā sthāpitavan sune trīṇi liṅgāni tatra eva pāpa ghnāni vidhānāt trīṇi liṅgāni tatra eva pāpa ghnāni vidhānāt pratijñeśvara nāma ādau kapāleśvaram ādarāt eva mudā liṅgam sthāpitavantaḥ te devadevasya śūlinaḥ sarveṣām mahimā abhūt tadā adbhutaḥ sarva kāma pradaḥ ca api mukti daḥ bhakti kāriṇām tatas sarve surāḥ viṣṇu pramukhāḥ prīta mānasāḥ aichat giri varam gantum puraskṛtya gurum mudā tasmin avasare śeṣa putraḥ kumuda nāmakaḥ kumārī śaraṇam daitya pīḍitaḥ pralamba ākhyaḥ asuraḥ yaḥ hi raṇāt asmāt palāyitaḥ saḥ tatra upadravam cakre prabalaḥ tārakāṃnugaḥ saḥ atha śeṣasya tanayaḥ kumudaḥ ahi yateḥ mahān kumāra śaraṇam prāptaḥ tuṣṭāva girija ātmajam uvāca ārṣaḥ pu0 hi aham pralambeṇa tvā aham śaraṇam āgataḥ pāhi mām śaraṇa āṃpannam pralamba asura pīḍitam kumāraiḥ skandaiḥ deveśaiḥ tārakāre mahā prabho dīnaiḥ bandhuḥ karuṇā sindhurā nata vatsalaḥ khala nigraha kartā hi śaraṇyaḥ ca satām gatiḥ kumudena stutaḥ ca ittham vijñaptaḥ tad vadhāya hi mahā śabdaḥ jagrāha smṛtvā śiva pada ambujau cikṣepa tām samuddiśya pralambam girijā sutaḥ mahā śabdaḥ babhūva atha jajvaluḥ ca diśaḥ namaḥ mahā bhasmasāt kṛtvā ca bhasmasāt sahasā ājagāma akliṣṭa kāriṇī tatas kumāraḥ provāca kumudam nāga bālakam bhukti mukti pradam satām ye kīrtayanti su yaśaḥ amita bhāgya yutāḥ narāḥ kumāra caritam divyam śiva lokam prayānti te ye ca tad kīrti bhaktyā śraddhā anvitāḥ janāḥ mukti prāpsyanti te divyām iha bhuktvā param sukham bāṇapralaṃvavadha kumāravijayavarṇanam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ānanāḥ karim bhaktyā sarve anye mudita ānanāḥ uccuḥ namaḥ kalyāṇa rūpāya namaḥ te viśvamaṅgalaiḥ viśvabandho namaḥ te astu namaḥ te viśvabhāvanaiḥ namaḥ astu te dānava varyatre bāṇa asura prāṇa harāya deva pralamba nāśāya pavitra rūpiṇe namaḥ namaḥ śaṃkara tātaiḥ te tvam eva kartā jagantām ca bhartā tvam eva hartā bhūtvā provāca pradadan varān uvāca yūyam sarve parvatāḥ hi pūjanīyāḥ tapasvibhiḥ karmibhiḥ jñānibhiḥ ca eva sevyamānāḥ bhaviṣyatha ca eva hi bhaviṣyatha na saṃdehaḥ parvatāḥ vacanāt mama ayam abhāva ku0 khaṃ0 tapasvinām mahābhāgaḥ phala daḥ hi bhaviṣyati ūcuḥ evam da tvā varān hatvā tārakam ca asura adhipam tvayā kṛtāḥ ca sukhinaḥ vayam sarve brahmā uvāca iti uktvā nikhilā devāḥ viṣṇu ādyāḥ prāpta śāsanāḥ kṛtvā mahā utsavam bhūri sa kumārāḥ yayuḥ girim kumāre gacchati vibhau kailāsam śaṃkara ālayam jagmuḥ ca pramudāḥ tadā jagmuḥ ca pramudāḥ tadā śambhoḥ jayam prabhāṣataḥ prāpuḥ te śambhuparvatam sa ānandāḥ viviśuḥ tatra uccaritaḥ maṅgala dhvaniḥ dṛṣṭvā śivam śivām ca eva sarve viṣṇu ādayaḥ drutam praṇamyam śaṃkaram bhaktyā karau baddha vinamrakāḥ kumāraḥ api vinīta ātmā vimānāt avatīrya ca praṇanāma mudā śambhum śivām siṃhāsana sthitām atha dṛṣṭvā kumāram tam tanayam prāṇa vallabham tau dampatī śivau devau mumudāte ati nāradaiḥ mahā snehāt tārakāreḥ mahā prabhoḥ api samutthāpya saṃnyaveśayat kṛttvā mahā snehāt tad mukha abjam cucumba hi tayoḥ tadā mahā āmodaḥ vavṛdhe iti iva nāradaiḥ dampatiyoḥ śivayoḥ tātaiḥ bhava ācāram prakurvatoḥ śivālaye na a vidhiḥ śivālaye jaya śabdaḥ namas śabdaḥ vabhūva atīva sarvatas tatas turaṃgaṇāḥ sarve viṣṇu ādyāḥ munayaḥ tathā suṃpraṇamya mudā śambhum tuṣṭuvuḥ saḥ pūjā sukha pradā sarveṣām śaṃkaraiḥ satām dīna bandho mahā prabho evam mūḍha dhiyaḥ śva ajñāḥ pūjāyām te sanātanam āvāhanam na jānīmaḥ gatim na eva prabho adbhutām gaṅgā salila dhārāya hi ādhārāya guṇa ātmane namaḥ te tridaśa īśāya śaṃkarāya namaḥ namaḥ maheśāya śāśvate visaṅgāya pareśāya śivāya paramātmane niṣprapañcāya śuddhāya paramāya avyayāya ca daṇḍa hastāya kālāya pāśa hastāya te maṃtra pradhānāya śatajihvāya te namaḥ veda maṃtra pradhānāya śatajihvāya te namaḥ bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyat ca sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca yat te dehāt samutpannam sarvathā parameśvaraiḥ pāhi pu0 nissarvadā svāmin prasīda bhagavant prabho vayam te śaraṇa āpannāḥ sarvathā parameśvaraiḥ vayam te śaraṇa āpannāḥ sarvathā parameśvaraiḥ śitikaṇṭhāya rudrāya svāhākārāya te namaḥ sarūpa viśvarūpāya te namaḥ śivāya nīlakaṇṭhāya citā bhasma aṅga dhāriṇe nityam nīlaśikhaṇḍāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namaḥ namaḥ saṃyama praṇatāya ca mahādevāya śarvāya sarva arcita padāya ca tvam brahmā sarva devānām rudrāṇām nīlalohitaḥ ātmā ca sarva bhūtānām sāṃkhyaiḥ puruṣa mayaḥ sarva vedānām trātā maheśvara tvam ca loka hita arthāya bhūtāni pariṣiṃcasi maheśvara mahābhāga śubha aśubha nirīkṣaka āpaya asmān hi deveśa kartan vai devāḥ viṣṇu ādyāḥ pramukha sthitāḥ muhur muhur su praṇamya skandam kṛtvā puraḥsaram deva stutim samākarṇya śivaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ svarāj babhūva atha vijahāsa dayā paraḥ uvāca su prasanna ātmā viṣṇu ādīn sura sattamān śaṃkaraḥ parameśānaḥ dīna bandhuḥ satām gatiḥ devāḥ vākyam mama śṛṇuta ādarāt devāḥ vākyam mama śṛṇuta ādarāt sarvathā aham satām trātā devānām vaḥ kṛpā nidhiḥ duṣṭa hantā triloka īśaḥ śaṃkaraḥ tad bhakta vatsalaḥ kartā bhartā ca hartā ca sarveṣām nirvikāravān yūyam vai bhajantu sukha hetave mudā bhavantaḥ yaśaḥ ramyam śivayoḥ śāṃkareḥ ca tat ānandam paramam prāpya sva dhāmāni yayuḥ mune śivaḥ api śivayā sārdham sa gaṇaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām caturthe kumārakhaṇḍe svāmikārtikacaritagarbhitaśivāśivacaritavarṇanam nāma uvāca devadevaiḥ prajānāthaiḥ śiva jñāna nidhe mayā śrutam kārttika sadṛttam amṛtāt api ca uttamam adhunā śrotum icchāmi gāṇeśam vṛttam uttamam na leka iti niṣedhāt karmaṇi na ṣaṣṭhī tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tatra hi hi sṛjyate pālyate tathā ha vai vicāre tat purā bhavata ca prathamāḥ te hi asaṃkhyātāḥ asmadīyaḥ na kaścana dvāri tiṣṭhanti te sarve śaṃkara ājñā parāyaṇāḥ te sarve api asmadīyāḥ ca tathā api na ekaḥ ca eva asmadīyaḥ hi racanīyaḥ tvayā anave tat ca kartum sma api adhyavasyati tat ca kartum sma api adhyavasyati tatas kadācid majjatyām pārvatyām vai sadāśivaḥ nandinam hi ājagāma gṛha antaram āyatam śaṃkaram dṛṣṭvā yat sukha āvaham āvaham evam jāte tadā kāle kadācid pārvatī śivā vicitya manasā ca iti paramāyā para īśvarā mad ājñayā param na anyat rekhā mātram calet iha mad ājñayā param na anyat rekhā mātram calet iha vicāyati ca sā devī vapuṣaḥ mala sambhavam puruṣam nirmamau sā tu sarva lakṣaṇa saṃbhavam yutam sarva avayava nirdoṣam sarva avayava sundaram viśālam sarva śobhā āḍhyam mahā vala parākramam vastrāṇi ca tadā tasmai da tvā sā vividhāni hi nānā alaṃkaraṇam ca eva bahu āśiṣam anuttamām mad putraḥ tvam madīyaḥ asi na anyaḥ kaścid iha asti mama evam uktaḥ ta puruṣaḥ namaskṛtya śivām jagau yat kāryam vidyate te idya karavāṇi te uditam iti uktā sā tadā tena pratyuvāca sutam śivā uvāca mad vākyam dvārapālaḥ bhava adya mama mad putraḥ tvam madīyaḥ asi na anyathā kaścid asti mama vinā mad ājñām sat putra na eva ayāt mad guha antaram api yat kvāpi haṭhāt tāta satyam etat mayā uditam su prītyā āliṃgya tam kṛpayā sutam sva dvāri sthāpayāmāsa yaṣṭi pāṇi gaṇādhipam atha devī sutaḥ tātaiḥ gṛha dvāri phu yutā yutā yutā etasmin eva kāle tu śivaḥ dvāri samāgataḥ kautukī muniḥ śādūlaiḥ nānā līlā viśāradaḥ uvāca ca śiveśam tam a vijñāya agrahīt tam dṛṣṭvā tu śivaḥ prāha kam niṣedhasi mūḍha dhīḥ mām na jānāsi asamuddhe śivaḥ ham iti na anyathā tāḍitaḥ tena yaṣṭyā tvam na jānāsi śivaḥ uham girijāpatiḥ yāmire bālaiḥ niṣedhasi katham hi mām iti uktvā praviśatam tam maheśam gaṇanāyakaḥ krodham kṛtvā tatas vipraiḥ daṇḍena atāḍayat punar tatas śivaḥ ca saṃkruddhaḥ gaṇān ājñāpayat nijāna kaḥ vā ayam vartate kim ca kriyate paśyatām gaṇāḥ iti uktvā tu śivaḥ tatra sthitaḥ kruddhaḥ bhava ācāra rataḥ svāmī bahu ahuta su līlakaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām caturthe kumārakhaṇḍe gaṇeśa utpatti varṇanam mahā bhāga nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ brahmā uvāca tadīyam tat vacaḥ śrutvā girijā tanayaḥ saḥ vai nirbhayaḥ daṇḍapāṇiḥ ca dvārapān abravīt idam īme yāta dūram kimartham vai sthitāḥ atra virodhinaḥ mahā vīrāḥ gata smayāḥ parasparam iti procya sarve te śiva pārṣadāḥ dvārapālam gaṇeśam tam pratyūcuḥ kruddha mānasāḥ dvārapālāḥ hi vayam śiva gaṇāḥ varāḥ tvām nivārayitum prāptāḥ śaṃkarasya ājñayā vibhoḥ tvām api iha gaṇam matvā na hanyāmaḥ anyathā itas tiṣṭha dūre svatas tvam ca kim artham mṛtyum īhase te sarve api gaṇāḥ śevāḥ tatratyāḥ vacanam tadā te sarve api gaṇāḥ śevāḥ tatratyāḥ vacanam tadā śrutvā tatra śivam gatvā tad vṛttāntam atha abruvan tatas ca tad vacaḥ śrutvā adbhuta līlaḥ mahe sva mṛtyum vāṃchati dhruvam dūratas kriyatām hi eṣa dvārapālaḥ navīnakaḥ iva sthitāḥ tasya vṛttam vadatha mama katham tvad iti śeṣaḥ sarve iti arthaḥ ku0 khaṃ0 ca ca kutas na eva asmān gāṇayasi evam katham jīvitum icchasi dvārapālāḥ vayam sarve sthitāḥ kim paribhāṣase siṃhāsana gṛhītaḥ ca śṛgālaḥ śivam īhate tāvat garjāsi mūrkhaiḥ tvam yāvat guṇa parākramaḥ na anubhūtaḥ tvayā atra iva hi anubhūtaḥ patiṣyāse iti uktaḥ taiḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ hastābhyām yaṣṭikām gaṇeśvaraḥ punar maryādā rakṣyate asmābhiḥ anyathā kim bravīti ca uvāca tatas śambhu gaṇāḥ sarve śivam dūre vyavasthitam krośa mātram tu kailāsā drutvā te ca tathā bruvan śivaḥ vihasya tān sarvān triśūla karaḥ ugra dhīḥ uvāca parameśaḥ hi sva gaṇān vīra saṃmatān uvāca mad agre na vīrāḥ vīra māninaḥ mad agre na uditum yogyāḥ bhatsitaḥ kim punar vadet gamyatām tāḍhyatām ca eṣa yaḥ kaścid prabhavet iha uvāca śrutvā yat vacaḥ teṣām śiva ājñā kāriṇām dhruvam śivā sutaḥ tadā abhūt saḥ kim karomi iti duḥkhitaḥ etasmin antare devī teṣām tasya ca vai punar paśya iti sā bravīt samāgatya sakhīm tatra vṛttatim samabudhyata kṣaṇa sāṃpratam yadi tasmāt tvam pūjanīyaḥ asi sindūreṇa sadā naraiḥ puṣpaiḥ vā candanaiḥ vā api gandhena eva śubhena ca sakalā siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ vinā ani aneka rūpāṇi kṣayam yāsyati asaṃśayam brahmā uvāca iti uktvā ca tadā devī sva putram pu0 maheśvarī nānā vastuṣu utkṛṣṭam punar api arcayat tathā tatas svāsthyam ca devānām gaṇānām ca viśeṣataḥ girijā kṛpayā vipraiḥ jāta tad kṣaṇa mātrāt maheśam paścāt utsaṅge san nyaveśayan bālakam tam maheśānyā atri jagat sukha hetave bālakam tam maheśānyā atri jagat sukha hetave śivaḥ api tasya śirasi da tvā sva kara paṅkajam uvāca nārada ādyān ṛṣīn sarvān sa tu āsthāya puras abravīt saṃtavyaḥ ca aparādhaḥ mama mānaḥ ca eva īdṛśaḥ nṛṇām aham ca śaṃkaraḥ ca eva viṣṇuḥ ca ete trayaḥ surāḥ vayam ca prākṛtāḥ ca ayam prākṛtaḥ pūjyaḥ eva ca gaṇeśaḥ vighna hartā ahi sarva kāma phala pradaḥ etad pūjām purā kṛtvā paścāt pūjyāḥ vayam naraiḥ vayam ca pūjitāḥ sarve na ayam ca apūjitaḥ yadā uvāca iti uktvā saḥ gaṇeśānaḥ nānā vastuṣu ādarāt śivena pūjitaḥ pūrva viṣṇunā tu prapūjitaḥ brahmanā ca mayā tatra pārvatyā ca prapūjitaḥ sarvaiḥ deva gaṇaiḥ ca eva pūjitaḥ parayā mudā savaiḥ militvā tatra eva brahma viṣṇu hara ādibhiḥ sa gaṇeśaḥ śivā tuṣṭaye sarva adhyakṣaḥ niveditaḥ punar ca eva śivena asmai su prasannena cetasā sarvadā sukha dāḥ loke varāḥ dattāḥ hi anekaśas uvāca he girīndrasutā putraiḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ mayi tuṣṭe jagant tuṣṭam viruddhaḥ kaḥ api no bhavet bāla rūpaḥ api yasmāt tvam mahā vikramaiḥ mad sarva gaṇādhyakṣaḥ saṃpūjyaḥ tvam bhava adhunā evam uktvā śaṃkareṇa pūjāḥ vidhiḥ anekaśas āśiṣaḥ ca api anekāḥ hi kṛtāḥ tasmin tu tad kṣaṇāt tatas deva gaṇāḥ ca eva gītam vādyam ca mudā te kārayāmāsuḥ tathā eva apsarasām gaṇāḥ mudā te kārayāmāsuḥ tathā eva apsarasām gaṇāḥ punar ca eva varaḥ dataḥ su prasannena śambhunā tasmai ca gaṇanāthāya śivena eva mahātmanā mudā vratam kāryam viśeṣeṇa ku0 sukham icchanti ye atulam ca api anekaśas tvām pūjayantu te bhaktyā caturthyām vidhi pūrvakam mārgaśīrṣe tathā māse ramā yām vai caturthikā prātar snānam tadā kṛtvā vratam viprān nyavedayet prātar pūjanam kāryam upavāsaḥ tathāvidhaḥ rātryāḥ ca prahare jāte snātvā saṃpūjayet naraḥ mūrti dhātu mayīm kṛtvā pravāla sambhavām tathā śveta arka sambhavām ca api mārdavām nirmitām tathā mān gandhaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ divyaiḥ candanaiḥ puṣpakaiḥ iha vitasti mātrā dūrvā ca tri aṅgā vai mūla varjitā īdṛśāṇām tad valānām śatenaka uttareṇa tvām tatra pūjayitvā ittham bālacandram ca pūjayet paścāt viprān ca saṃpūjya bhojayet madhuraiḥ mudā svayam ca eva tatas bhujyāt madhuram lavaṇam vinā visarjayet tatas paścāt niyamam sarvam ātmanaḥ gaṇeśa smaraṇam kuryāt sampūrṇaiḥ śubham dvādaśa brāhmaṇāḥ tatra bhojanīyāḥ mad ājñayā kumbham ekam ca saṃsthāpya pūjyā mūrti tvadīyakā pūjayitvā mūrtya vidhi pūrvakam niśi jāgaraṇam kārya punar prātar prapūjayet visarjanam tatas ca eva punar āgamanāya ca ca puṣpa añjali pradadyāt ca vrata saṃpūrṇa hetave puṣpa añjali pradadyāt ca vrata saṃpūrṇa hetave namaskārān tatas kṛtvā nānā kārye prakalpayet evam vratam kṛtam yena tasya īpsita phalam bhavet eva tathā upacāraiḥ anekaiḥ vai pūjayet tvā gaṇeśvaram evam tvā bhaktyā nānā upacārāt teṣām siddhiḥ bhavet nityam vighna nāśaḥ bhavet iha sarva aivarṇaiḥ prakarttavyā strībhiḥ ca eva viśeṣataḥ udaya abhimukhaiḥ ca eva rājbhiḥ ca viśeṣataḥ yam yam kāmayate yaḥ vai tam tam āpnoti niścitam atas kāmayamānena tena sevyaḥ sadā bhavān tathā iti uktvā tu taiḥ sarvaiḥ gaṇaiḥ śambhu priyaiḥ mune pūjitaḥ hi gaṇādhīśaḥ vidhinā parame saḥ pūjā iti śeṣaḥ samānarcuḥ viśeṣeṇa nānā vastuṣu ādarāt girijāyāḥ samutpannaḥ yaḥ ca harṣaḥ muni īśvaraiḥ caturbhiḥ vedanena eva tam avarṇyam ca katham bruve deva dundubhayaḥ neduḥ nṛtuḥ ca apsaras ganāḥ jaguḥ agandharva mukhyāḥ ca puṣpa varṣam papāta ha jagat svāsthyam tadā prāpa gaṇādhīśe pratiṣṭhite mahā utsavaḥ mahān āsīt sarve duḥkham kṣayam gatam śiva aśivau ca modetām viśeṣeṇa ati nāradaiḥ āsīt su ma iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām caturthe kumārakhaṇḍe gaṇeśagaṇādhipapadavīvarṇanam nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sādhu pṛṣṭam muni śreṣṭhaiḥ bhavatā karuṇa ātmanā śrūyatām datta karṇaḥ hi vakṣye aham ṛṣi sattamaiḥ śivā śivaḥ ca vipra indra dvayoḥ ca sutayoḥ param dṛśīdṛśī ca tad līlām mahā premṇa samāvahat pitroḥ lālayatoḥ tatra sukham ca ati vyavardhata sadā prītyā mudā ca atikhela snehaḥ vyavardhata mahān śuka pakṣe yathā śaśī snehaḥ vyavardhata mahān śuka pakṣe yathā śaśī kadācid tau sthitau tatra rahasi prema saṃyutau śivā śivaḥ ca deva ṛṣe su vicāra parāyaṇau śivā śivau ūcatuḥ vivāha yogyau saṃjātau sutau iti ca tau ubhau vivāhaḥ ca katham kāryaḥ putrayoḥ ubhayayoḥ śubham ṣaṇmukhaḥ ca priyatamaḥ ca tathā eva ca iti cintā samudvinaḥ līlā ānandau babhūvatuḥ sva pitroḥ matam ājñāya tau sutau api saṃspṛhī tad icchayā vivāha artham babhūvatu prabhū laukika ācāram āśritya vismayam paramam gatau kim kartavyam katham kāryaḥ om vivāha vidhiḥ etayoḥ iti niścitya tābhyām vai racitā tā kadācid samaye sthitvā samāhūya sva putrakau kathayāmāsatuḥ tatra putrayoḥ pitarau tadā śiva aśivau ūcatuḥ niyamaḥ pūrvam kṛtaḥ ca sukha doṃ hi vām śrūyatām su sutau prītyā kathayāvaḥ yathārthakam samau dvau api sat putrau viśeṣaḥ na atra labhyate tasmāt paṇaḥ kṛtaḥ śam tayoḥ eva putrayoḥ ubhayayoḥ api putrayoḥ ubhayayoḥ api yaḥ ca eva pṛthivīm sarvā krāntvā pūrvam upātrajet tasya eva prathamam kāryaḥ om vivāhaḥ śubha lakṣaṇaḥ uvāca vacaḥ śrutvā śarajanmā mahā balaḥ jagāma mandirāt tūrṇam pṛthivī kramaṇāya vai gaṇanāthaḥ ca tatra eva saṃsthitaḥ buddhi sattamaḥ su buddhayā saṃvicārya iti citte eva punar punar citte eva punar punar kim kartavyam kva gaṃtavyam laṅghitum na eva śakyate krośa mātram gataḥ syāt vai gamyate na mayā punar kim punar pṛthivīm etām krāntvā ca upārjitam sukham vicārya eti gaṇeśaḥ tu yat cakāra śṛṇuṣva tat snānam kṛtvā yathānyāyam samāgatyam svayam gṛham uvāca pitaram tatra tena atha pūjitau tau ca prakrāntau ca punar punar uvāca bho māta bhoṃ pitar tvam ca śṛṇu paramam vacaḥ śīghram ca eva atra kartavyaḥ vivāhaḥ śobhanaḥ mama uvāca iti evam vacanam śrutvā pu0 krāntā sapta vāram punar punar evam katham bruvāte vai punar ca pitarau iha brahmā uvāca tat vacaḥ tu tadā śrutvā laukikām gatim āśritau mahā līlā karau tatra pitarau ūcatuḥ ca tam tatra pitarau ūcatuḥ ca tam ūcatuḥ kadā krāṃtā tvayā putraiḥ pṛthivī su mahattarā sapta dvīpā samudra antā mahadbhiḥ gahanaiḥ yutā bhavatoḥ pūjanam kṛtvā mama vai bhavet iti na saṃśayaḥ śīghram ca bhavitavyaḥ mama vivāhaḥ kriyatām śubhaḥ atha vā veda śāstram ca vyalīkam kathyatām iti mahā vacaḥ tasya vismayam paramam gatau tau tatas śivā putram buddhi vicakṣaṇam su praśasya ūcatuḥ prītyā tau yathārtha prabhāṣiṇam siṃhaḥ mada unmattaḥ śaśakena nipātitaḥ veda śāstra purāṇeṣu bālakasya yathā uditam tvayā kṛtam tu tat sarvam dharmasya paripālanam samyak kṛtam tvayā yat ca tat kena api bhavet iha āvābhyām ānitam tat ca na anyathā kriyate adhunā sāgaram vivāha karaṇe ca asya matim cakratuḥ uttamām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām caturthe kumārakhaṇḍe nāma tābhyām sukham ca eva aticintakam prāptavan ca mune tat tu varṇitum na eva śakyate kiyatā ca eva kālena gaṇeśasya mahātmanaḥ evam sukham acityam vai bhuṃjāne hi gaṇeśvare ājagāma dvitīyaḥ ca krāntvā pṛthvīm sutaḥ tadā tāvat ca nāradena eva prāptaḥ gehe mahātmanā miṣam bravīmi aham satyam bravīmi aham niṣkāsya tvām kukramaṇam miṣam utpādya yatnāt gaṇeśasya vivāhaḥ para śobhanaḥ nirantaram bhavatā pṛthivī krāntā sa samudrā sa kānanā tad chala ājñā vaśāt tātaiḥ tasya jātam phalam tu idam chalam tāta vicāryatām sva svāmibhyām viśeṣeṇa hi anyaḥ kim na karoti vai asamyak ca kṛtam tvad pitṛbhyām hi karma ha vicārya tām tvayā api iha mad citte na śubham matam tām tvayā api iha mad citte na śubham matam dadyāt yadi garam mātā vikrīṇīyāt pitā yadi rājā harati sarva svam kasmai kim ca bravītu vai yena eva idam kṛtam syāt vai karma anartha karam param śānti kāmaḥ sudhīḥ tātaiḥ tad mukham na vilokayet iti nītiḥ śrutau proktā smṛtau śāstreṣu sarvatas skandaḥ api pitaram natvā kopa agni jvalitaḥ tadā jagāma parvatam krauñcam pitṛbhyām vāritaḥ api san pu0 yat kṛtam mayi evam uktvā gataḥ tatra mune saḥ adya api vartate darśanena eva sarveṣām lokānām pāpa hārakaḥ tad dinam hi samārabhya bhārtikyām ca sadā devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca sa tīrthakāḥ darśana artha kumārasya gacchanti ca muni īśvarāḥ kārttikyām kṛttikā saṅge kuryāt yaḥ svā prabho svayam tatas anyatra gantum āsīt hi śivau parvaṇi parvaṇi darśana arthe kumārasya tasya nāradaiḥ gacchataḥ amāvāsyā dine śambhuḥ svayam gacchati tatra ha pūrṇamāsī dine tatra pārvatī gacchati bhavati pāpaiḥ pramucyate śobhanām labhate kāmān īpsitān sakalān sadā yaḥ paṭhet pāṭhayet vā api śṛṇuyāt śrāvayet tathā sarvān kāmān avāpnoti na atra brāhmaṇaḥ brahma varcasvī kṣatriyaḥ vijayī bhavet vaiśyaḥ dhana samṛddhaḥ syāt śūdraḥ sat sama tām iyāt rogī rogāt pramucyeta mahā pautra ādi kārakam pāmaiḥ ca su mukṣibhiḥ śiva advaita pradam ca etat sadāśiva mayam śivam iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām caturthe kumārakhaṇḍe gaṇeśa namaḥ nāma ku0 khaṃ0 mad saṃvarta namaḥ uvāca śrutam asmābhiḥ ānanda pradam caritam uttamam gṛhasthasya eva śambhoḥ ca gaṇaskam trīṇi ekena ca bāṇena yugapad kena vīryavān etat sarvam samācakṣva caritam śaśimaulinaḥ deva ṛṣi sukha dam śaśvat māyā viharataḥ hṛṇu vyāsaiḥ mahā prājñaiḥ caritam śaśimaulinaḥ yathā dadāha tripuram bāṇena ekena viśvahṛt śiva ātmajena skandena nihate tāraka asure tad putrāḥ tu trayaḥ daityāḥ paryatapyan muni īśvaraiḥ trayaḥ daityāḥ paryatapyan muni īśvaraiḥ tāraka ākhyaḥ tu tad jyeṣṭhaḥ vidyunmālī ca madhyamaḥ kamalākṣaḥ kanīyāḥ ca sarve tulya balāḥ sadā jite mad vihāya su manoharān vasante sarva kāmān ca gīta vādi ca nissvanam vihāya sa utsavam te tāraka ātmajāḥ grīṣme sūrya prabhām mahā pratāpa patitāḥ sarve pi āsan su mūrchitāḥ trāsāḥ vṛṣṭi mūrdhani adhārayan śarad kāle prasūtam tu bhojanam tu bubhukṣitāḥ ramyam snigdham sthiram hṛdyam phalam mūlam anuttamam mahātmānaḥ jittvā pānāni uccāvacāni api bubhukṣitebhyaḥ da tvā tu babhūvuḥ upalāḥ iva saṃsthitāḥ te mahātmānaḥ nirādhārāḥ caturdiśam tuṣāra deha saṃchannāḥ dhairyeṇa parameṇa tu tuṣāra deha saṃchannāḥ jala kkinnena vāsasā āsādya deham kṣaumeṇa śiśire toya madhya gāḥ anirviṇṇāḥ tatas sarve varṣāṇām śatakam ca eva padam ekam nidhāya ca bhūmau sthitvā param tatra tepuḥ te balavattarāḥ te sahasram tu varṣāṇām vātabhakṣāḥ tapaḥ tepuḥ durātmānaḥ param tāpam upāgatāḥ tapaḥ tepuḥ durātmānaḥ param tāpam upāgatāḥ varṣāṇām tu sahasram vai mastakena āsthitāḥ tathā varṣāṇām tu śatena eva ūrdhva vāhavaḥ ā hi te sthitāḥ evam duḥkham param prāptāḥ durāgraha pare ime īdṛś te saṃsthitāḥ daityāḥ divārātra mataṃdvitāḥ evam teṣām gataḥ kālaḥ mahān sutapatām mune brahma ātmanām tārakāṇām dharmeṇa iti matiḥ mama prādurāsīt tamaḥ brahmā sura asura guruḥ mahān saṃtuṣṭaḥ tapasā teṣām varam dātum mahā yaśāḥ suni deva asuraiḥ sārdham sāṃtva pūrvam idam vacaḥ tatas tān abravīt sarvān sarva bhūta pitāmahaḥ pu0 pāntu naḥ paripaṃthinaḥ jarā roga ādayaḥ sarve na asmān mṛtyuḥ agāt kacid ajara aśva amarāḥ sarve bhavāmaḥ iti naḥ matam iti śrutvā vacaḥ teṣām daityānām ca tapasvinām pratyuvāca śivam smṛtvā sva prabhum giriśam vidhiḥ mara tvam ca nivartadhvam atas asurāḥ anyam varam vṛṇīdhvam vai yādṛśaḥ vaḥ hi rocate jātaḥ janiṣyate nūnam jantuḥ kaḥ api asurāḥ kvacid na bhaviṣyati bhū tale ṛte tu khaṇḍaparaśoḥ kāla kālāt hareḥ tathā tau dharma adharma paramau avyaktau vyakta rūpiṇaḥ sampīḍanāya dussādhyam mṛtyum vacayata anaghāḥ api adhṛṣyāḥ śātravāṇām tu yatra vatsyāmahe sukham purāṇi trīṇi naḥ dehi nirmāya ati adbhutāni hi tatas tāni na anyathā tāni na anyathā sarva deva mayaḥ devaḥ sarveṣām mama kuhelayā asaṃbhave rathe tiṣṭhan sarva upakaraṇa anvite yu0 bhinattu nagarāṇi naḥ nirvairaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ tu yaḥ naḥ iti nityaśas vaidyaḥ pūjyaḥ abhivādyaḥ ca saḥ naḥ nirdahet katham saṃghāya tādṛśaḥ bhuvi durlabhaḥ uvāca bho prāha sṛṣṭi kartā smaraśivam iti ādiśya mayam brahmā pratyakṣam prāviśat divam teṣām nāraka putrāṇām paśyatām nijadhāma hi bhūmau ca kramāt jñeyāni tāni vai bhūmau ca kramāt jñeyāni tāni vai da tvā surebhyaḥ ca purāṇi trīṇi vai mayaḥ praviveśa svayam tatra hita kāma parāyaṇaḥ bubhujuḥ sakalān bhogān mahā bala parākramāḥ bubhujuḥ sakalān bhogān mahā bala parākramāḥ kalpadrumaiḥ ca saṃkīrṇam gaja vāji samākulam maṇi jāla samāvṛtam sūrya maṇḍala saṃkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ sarvatomukhaiḥ padmarāga mayaiḥ ca eva śobhitam candra saṃnibhaiḥ divyaiḥ kailāsa śikhara upamaiḥ divyaiḥ kailāsa śikhara upamaiḥ divya strī jana saṃkīrṇaiḥ gadharvaiḥ siddha cāraṇaiḥ rudra ālayaiḥ pratigṛham agnihotraiḥ pratiṣṭhitaiḥ dvijottamaiḥ śāstra vijñaiḥ śiva mā bhakti rataiḥ sadā matta mātaṃga yūthaiḥ ca turaṃgaiḥ ca su śobhanam rathaiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ śibikābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam yad yad yad yad yad yad yad yad yad tad tad tad tad tad tad tad adhyayana śālābhiḥ vividhābhiḥ pṛthak pṛthak mahātmabhiḥ śubha ācāraiḥ puṇyavadbhiḥ pravakṣyate pativratābhiḥ sarvatra pāvitaḥ sthalam uttamam pati sevana śīlābhiḥ vimukhābhiḥ kudharmāt vīryaiḥ ravi maruta mahā indra saṃnikāśaiḥ sura marthanaiḥ mu dṛḍhaiḥ su sevitam yat śāstra veda purāṇeṣu ye ye dharmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ mad priyāḥ sadā daivāḥ te dharmāḥ tatra sarvatas evam labdha varāḥ te tu daiteyāḥ tāraka ātmajāḥ śaivam mayam upāśritya nivasanti sma tatra ha sarva trailokyam utsārya praviśya nagarāṇi te sma mahat rājyam śiva mārga ratāḥ sadā tatas mahān gataḥ kālaḥ vasatām puṇya karmaṇām pu0 yathāsukham yathājoṣam sat rājyam kurvatām mune brahmā uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya vyāsasya amita dhīmataḥ sanatkumāraḥ provāca smṛtvā śiva pada ambujam duḥkham vijñāpayāmāsuḥ vilokya avasaram tatas ūcuḥ dhātar tripura nāthena sa tāraka sutena hi sarve pratāpitāḥ nūnam mayena punar ca prārthayadhvam vai sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ karṇya vidheḥ vāṇīm sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ duḥkhitāḥ te yayuḥ tatra yatra āste vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ praṇamya bhaktyā deveśam sarve prāñjalayaḥ tadā taskaṃdhāḥ śaṃkaram loka śaṃkaram ūcuḥ sarva namaḥ hara svarūpāya bhūta saṃhāra kāriṇe nirguṇāya namaḥ te śivāya amita tejase avasthā rahitāya atha nirvikārāya varcase bhūtātma bhūtāya nirliptāya mahātmane namaḥ te bhūtapataye mahā bhāra sahiṣṇave tṛṣṇā harāya nirvaira ākṛtaye bhūri tejase vahnaye vahnaye namaḥ te śūlapāṇaye mahā danuja nāśāya namaḥ te parameśvara ambikāpataye tubhyam namaḥ sarva astra dhāraka namaḥ te pārvatī nāthaiḥ paramātman maheśvaraiḥ nīlakaṇṭhāya rudrāya namaḥ te rudra rūpiṇe namaḥ vedānta vedyāya mārga atītāya te namaḥ saṃkarṣaṇāya namaḥ te kaṃsa nāśine cāṇūra mardine te dāmodara viṣādine hṛṣīkeśa acyuta vibho mṛḍa śaṃkaraiḥ te namaḥ rāte kāmāre viṣa bhakṣaṇaiḥ yu0 hāriṇe pāpa apahāriṇe te namaḥ vṛṣabhavāhanaiḥ kṣaṇa ādi kāla rūpāya sva bhakta bala dāyine nānā rūpāya rūpāya daitya cakra vimardine stutya ācāra priyāya ca caturvidha svarūpāya jala sthala ja rūpiṇe sarve deva ādayaḥ nāthaiḥ śreṣṭha tvena vibhūtayaḥ tvam raviḥ mataḥ satya lokaḥ asi lokānām ghusarit bhavān śveta varṇaḥ asi varṇānām sarasām mānasam saraḥ śailānām tvam ca goṣu ha kṣīrodadhiḥ tu sindhūnām dhātūnām hāṭakaḥ bhavān varṇānām brāhmaṇaḥ asi tvam nṝṇām rājā asi śaṃkaraiḥ mukti kṣetreṣu kāśī tvam tīrthānām tīrtha rāj bhavān upaleṣu samasteṣu sphaṭikaḥ tvam maheśvaraiḥ kamalaḥ tvam prasūneṣu śaileṣu himatrān tathā bhavān vāc vyavasthā hāreṣu bhārgavaḥ tvam kaviṣu api pakṣiṣu eva asi śarabhaḥ siṃhaḥ hiṃsreṣu saṃmataḥ śālagrāma śilā ca tvam śilāsu vṛṣabhadhvaja pūjya rūpeṣu sarveṣu mad liṅgam eva hi nandīśvaraḥ asi paśuṣu vṛṣabhaḥ parameśvaraḥ vedeṣu upaniṣad rūpaḥ yajvanām śīta bhānumān pratāpinām pāvakaḥ tvam bhavān bhāratam tvam purāṇānām makāraḥ asi akṣareṣu ca praṇavaḥ bīja mantrāṇām dāruṇānām viṣam bhavān vyom vyāptimatām tvam vai paramātmā asi yat ca ātmanām indriyāṇām manaḥ ca tvam dānānām abhayam bhavān pāvanānām jalam ca asi jīvanānām tathā amṛtam lābhānām putra lābhaḥ asi mahā vāyuḥ vegavatām asim nityakarmasu sarveṣu saṃdhyā upāstiḥ bhavān matā ṛtūnām aśvamedhaḥ asi yugānām prathamaḥ yugaḥ puṣpaḥ tvam sarva dhiṣṇyānām amā vāsyā tithiṣu asi sarva ṛtuṣu vasantaḥ tvam sarva sarva su saṃkramaḥ kuśaḥ asi tṛṇa jātīnām sthūla vṛkṣeṣu vai vaṭaḥ yogeṣu ca vyatīpātaḥ saḥ ca mataḥ dharmaḥ tvam sarva bandhūnām āśramāṇām paraḥ bhavān mokṣaḥ tvam sarva vargeṣu rudrāṇām nīlalohitaḥ vāsudevaḥ hanumant vānareṣu ca yajñānām japa yajñaḥ asi rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtām bhavān gandharvāṇām citrarathaḥ vasūnām pāvakaḥ dhruvam māsānām adhimāsaḥ tvam vratānām pu0 caturdaśī caturdaśī airāvataḥ gaja indrāṇām kapilaḥ mataḥ anantaḥ tvam hi nāgānām pitṝṇām aryamā bhavān kālaḥ kalayatām ca tvam uvāca iti stutvā surāḥ sarve mahādevam vṛṣadhvajam stotraiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ divyaiḥ śūlinam parameśvaram pratyūcuḥ prastutam dīnāḥ sva artham sva artha vicakṣaṇaḥ trailokyam sva vaśam nītaḥ tathā ca muni sattamāḥ vidhvastāḥ sarva saṃsiddhāḥ sarvam utsāditam jagant gṛhṇāti ca śaṃkaraiḥ yāvat na kṣīyate daitya eva ūroḥ tripura vāsibhiḥ tāvat vidhīyatām nītiḥ yayā saṃrakṣyate jagant yat vacaḥ teṣām indra ādīnām divaukasām śivaḥ saṃbhāṣamāṇānām prativākyam uvāca saḥ kvacid jānāmi deva kaṣṭam ca vibudhāḥ sakalam mahat daityāḥ te prabalāḥ hetum aśakyāḥ tu sura asuraiḥ puṇyavantaḥ tu te sarve samayāḥ tārakā dussādhyaḥ tu vadhaḥ teṣām sarveṣām pura vāsinām dussādhyaḥ tu vadhaḥ teṣām sarveṣām pura vāsinām mitra droham katham jānan karomi raṇa karkaśaḥ suhṛd dohe mahat pāpam pūrvam uktam svayambhunā surāḥ vicāryatām bhavadbhiḥ vai dharma jñaiḥ eva dharmāt tāvat te na eva hantavyāḥ yāvat bhakti kṛtaḥ ca mama tathā api viṣṇave devāḥ niṣkāma veidyam kāraṇam tu idam uvāca iti evam tat vacaḥ śrutvā devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ nyavedayan drutam sarve brahmaṇe prathamam mune tatas vidhi puraskṛtya sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ vaikuṇṭham prayayuḥ śīghram sarve śobhā samanvitam tatra gatvā harim dṛṣṭvā praṇemuḥ jāta sambhramāḥ mahā bhaktyā kṛta añjali puṭāḥ surāḥ sva duḥkha kāraṇam sarve pūrvavat tad anantaram nyavedayan drutam tasmai viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave deva duḥkham tatas śrutvā dattam ca tripurālaye jñātvā vratam ca teṣām tat viṣṇuḥ vacanam abravīt uvāca idam satyam vacaḥ ca eva yatra sanātanaḥ tatra duḥkham na jāyeta sūrye dṛṣṭe yathā tamaḥ sanatkumāraḥ uvāca iti etat vacanam śrutvā devāḥ duḥkham upāgatāḥ punar ūcuḥ tathā viṣṇum parimlāna mukha ambujāḥ ūcuḥ ca eva prakarttavyam katham duḥkham nirasyate katham bhavema sukhinaḥ katham madhyam ca eva vidhīyatām noced akālikā deva saṃhatiḥ kriyatām dhruvam sanatkumāraḥ uvāca iti uktvā te tadā devāḥ duḥkham kṛtvā punar te vai cakruḥ deva varāt iha sthitim na eva gatim te vai cakruḥ deva varāt iha tān vai tathāvidhān dṛṣṭvā hīnān vinaya saṃyutān tayā cetasām tathā kim kāryam deva kāryeṣu mayā deva sahāyinā śiva bhaktāḥ tu te daityāḥ tārakasya sutāḥ iti iti saṃcintya tad kāle tatas viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā tatas yajñāḥ smṛtāḥ tena deva kārya artham akṣayāḥ tatas viṣṇuḥ smṛti mātreṇa yajñāḥ te tad kṣaṇam drutam āgatāḥ tatra yatra āste puruṣottamaḥ tatas viṣṇum yajñapatim purāṇam puruṣam harim praṇamya tuṣṭuvuḥ te vai kṛta añjali puṭāḥ tadā bhagavant api tān dṛṣṭvā yajñān prāha sanātanam yajñān prāha sanātanam sanātanaḥ tadā sa indrān devān ālokya ca acyutaḥ uvāca anena eva sadā devāḥ yajadhvam parameśvaram vināśāya jagatraya vibhūtaye surāḥ evam stutvā tatas devāḥ ayajan yajñapuruṣam yajña uktena vidhānena saṃpūrṇa vidhayaḥ mune tatas tasmāt yajña kuṇḍāt samutpe bhūta saṃghāḥ śūla śakti gadā āyudhāḥ śūla śakti gadā āyudhāḥ dadṛśuḥ te surāḥ tān vai bhūta saṃghān sahasraśas dṛṣṭvā tān abravīt viṣṇuḥ praṇipatya puras sthitān bhūtān yajñapatiḥ śrīmān nudrā ājñā pratipālakaḥ uvāca bhūtāḥ śṛṇuta mad vākyam deva kārya arthaiḥ tejasi bhasmasāt abhavan sadyas śalabhāḥ iva pāvake avaśiṣṭāḥ ca ye kecid palāyana parāyaṇāḥ nismṛtya āram samāyātāḥ hareḥ ni bhagavant kaṭama ākulāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā saḥ hariḥ śrutvā tat ca vṛttam aśeṣatas ciṃtayāmāsa bhagavant manasā puruṣottamaḥ kim kṛtyam adhunā kāryam iti ārṣam pu0 mānasaḥ saṃtaptān āmarān sarvān ājñāya ca sa vāsavān katham teṣām ca daityānām balāt hatvā puratrayam devakāya kariṣyāmi iti āsī citā rumā kulaḥ na asti dharmiṣṭhānām na saṃśayaḥ iti prāha svayam ca īśaḥ śruti ācāra pramāṇa kṛt ca hi sarve vāsinaḥ tasmāt avadhya tām prāptāḥ na anyathā asura puṃgavāḥ kṛtvā tu su mahat pāpam rudram abhyarcayanti te mucyaṃte pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ padma pattram iva aṃga tatas anekāvidha sampattyāḥ mokṣasya api paratra ca tatas kṛtvā dharma vighnam teṣām eva ātma māyayā daityānām deva kārya arthe hariṣye tripuram kṣaṇāt puruṣottamaḥ vicārya ittham tatas teṣām bhagavant puruṣottamaḥ kartum vyavasthitaḥ paścāt dharma vighnam sura arīṇām yāvat ca veda dharmāḥ tu yāvat vai śaṃkara arcanam ca niścitya vai viṣṇuḥ vighna artham akarot tadā teṣām dharmasya daityānām upāyam śruti khaṇḍanam tadā eva uvāca devān saḥ viṣṇuḥ deva sahāya kṛt mad ājñayā trailokya rakṣaṇe rakṣaṇe uvāca tān rudrāt vimukhān nūnam kariṣyāmi su yatnāt sva bhakti rahitā jñātvā tān kariṣyati bhasmasāt tad ājñām śirasā avāya śvāsitāḥ te amarā śvāsitāḥ te amarā viśvastāḥ yayuḥ brahma api moditāḥ bhūta tripura dharma varṇanam nāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca asṛjat ca mahā tejāḥ puruṣam sva ātma sambhavam ekam māyā mayam teṣām mlāna vastram ca gumphi pātra samanvitam dadhānam puñjikām haste pade pade munim prasanna mānasaḥ bhūtvā ca idam abravīt uvāca asi nibodha kathayāmi mahā na saṃśayaḥ māyin māyā mayam śāstram tat ṣoḍaśa sahasrakam śrauta smārta viruddham ca varṇa āśrama vivarjitam apabhraṃśa mayam śāstram karma vāda mayam tathā racaya iti prayatnena tad vistāraḥ bhaviṣyati dadāmi te nirmāṇe sāmarthyam tat bhaviṣyati ca bhaviṣyati yat kartavyam mayā devaiḥ drutam ādiśa tat prabho tvad ājñayā akhilam karma saphalam ca ca bhaviṣyati māyā mayam tathā śāstram māyā mayam tathā iha iva svarga naraka pratyayaḥ om na anyathā punar tam uvāca punar viṣṇuḥ smṛtvā śiva pada ambujam mohanīyāḥ ime daityāḥ sarve vāsinaḥ mad mad as na saṃśayaḥ anayā vidyayā sarve sphoṭanīyāḥ dhruvam yate gam arhasi nāśa artham suṇḍin tripura vāsinām mad ājñayā bhavat dhama vistāram yāsyati dhruvam prāpsyasi paripālayan hareḥ ājñām tathā nirmitavan ca śiṣyān yathā svarūpam caturaḥ tadānīm māyā mayam śāstram apāṭhayat svayam yathā svayam tathā muṇḍi mama te atha dharmam pāṣaṇḍam āśritāḥ haste pātram dadhānāḥ ca tuṇḍa vastrasya dhārakāḥ malināni eva vāsāṃsi dhārayantaḥ hi abhāṣiṇaḥ dharmaḥ oṃ lābhaḥ param tattvam vadataḥ tu ati harṣāt tattvam vadataḥ tu ati harṣāt mārjanīm vastra khaṇḍā vinirmitām śanais śanais calantaḥ hi jīva hiṃsā bhayāt dhruvam te sarve ca su prītyā tad nām api viśeṣataḥ yathā tvam ca tathā eva ete madīyāḥ vai na saṃśayaḥ ādi rūpam ca tad nām pūjya tvāt pūjyaḥ ucyate yatiḥ tathā ākīryaḥ upādhyāyaḥ iti svayam imāni api tu nāmāni prasiddhāni bhavantu vaḥ mama api ca grāhyam pu0 punar ari hā iti tat nām dhyeyam pāpa praṇāśanam bhavadbhiḥ ca eva kartavyam kāryam loka sukha āvaham loka anukūlam caratām bhaviṣyati uttamā gatiḥ mudā praviśya tat puram tūrṇa viṣṇunā noditaḥ vaśī mahā māyāvinā tena ṛṣiḥ māyām tadā akarot nagara upavane kṛtvā māyām śiṣyaiḥ yuktaḥ sthitim tadā māyām pravartayāmāsa māyinām api mohinīm śiva arcana prabhāvena tad māyā sahasā mune na cacāla āśu nirviṇṇaḥ bhūt tadā yatiḥ atha viṣṇum sa sasmāra tuṣṭāva ca hṛdām bahu naṣṭa utsāhaḥ vicetaskaḥ hṛdayena vidūyatā tad smṛtaḥ tvaritam viṣṇuḥ sasmāra śaṃkaram hṛdi prāpya ājñām manasā tasya smṛtavan nāradam drutam hi śiva ājñayā ucyate tātaiḥ gaccha tvam tripuram drutam ṛṣiḥ tatra gataḥ śiṣyaiḥ mahā artham tad su vāsinām uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya nāradaḥ muni sattamaḥ gataḥ tatra drutam yatra saḥ ṛṣiḥ māyinām varaḥ nāradaḥ api tathā māyī niyogāt māyinaḥ prabhoḥ praviśya tat puram tena māyi nā saha dīkṣitaḥ tatas ca nāradaḥ gatvā tripurādhīśa saṃnidhau kṣemapraśna ādikam kṛtvā rājñe sarvam nyavedayat yatiḥ dharma parāyaṇaḥ sarva vidyā prakṛṣṭaḥ hi veda vidyā para anvitaḥ dṛṣṭā ca bahavaḥ na etena sadṛśāḥ punar tvam atra dṛṣṭvā dharma sanātanam dṛṣṭvā dharma sanātanam te icchā yadi varteta daitya sattamaiḥ tad dharmasya mahā rājaiḥ grāhyā dīkṣā tvayā punar uvāca tadīyam saḥ vacaḥ śrutvā mahat artha sugarbhitam vismitaḥ hṛdi daitya īśaḥ jagau tatra vimohitaḥ prumaḥ iti evam ca viditvā vai jagāma svayam eva ha tad rūpam ca tadā dṛṣṭvā mohitaḥ māyayā tathā uvāca vacanam tasmai namaskṛtya mahātmane uvāca dīkṣā deyā tvayā me nirmala āśaya bho ṛṣe aham śiṣyaḥ bhaviṣyāmi satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ vacaḥ śrutvā daitya rājasya nirmalam pratyuvāca su yatnena ṛṣiḥ saḥ ca sanātanaḥ madīyā karaṇīyā syāt yadi ājñā daitya sattamaiḥ tadā deyā mayā dīkṣā na anyathā koṭi yatnāt iti evam tu vacaḥ śrutvā rājā māyā mayaḥ abhavat uvāca vacanam śīghram yati tam hi kṛtāñjaliḥ śatṛ pratyaya ārṣa yu0 yathā ājñām dāsyati tvam ca tat tathā eva na ca anyathā tvad ājñām na ucuṃghayiṣye satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ tripura adhīśituḥ tadā tripura adhīśituḥ tadā dūrīkṛtya mukhāt vastram uvāca ṛṣi sattamaḥ dīkṣām gṛhṇīṣva daitya indraiḥ sarva dharma uttamottamām yena dīkṣā vidhānena prāpsya tvam kṛtārtha tām tu śiṣyaiḥ praśiṣyaiḥ ca tadā tripuram sakalam mune tripuram sakalam mune pañcame yuddhakhaṇḍe sanatkumāra pārāśarya saṃvāde tripuradīkṣāvidhānam nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ mohite kim uvāca tadā māyī kim cakāra saḥ daityapaḥ uvāca dīkṣām da tvā yatiḥ tasmai ari hā nārada ādibhiḥ hi keśvaraḥ tatra na dvitīyaḥ tad īśitā yat brahma viṣṇu rudra ākhyā tad ākhyāḥ dehinām imāḥ ākhyā yathā mad ādīnām ari han ādiḥ ucyate yathā asmadā dīnām sva kālena vilīyate brahma ādi maśaka antānām sva kāla ālīyate tathā maithunam nidrā bhayam sarvatra yat samam nirāhāra parīmāṇam prāpya sarvaḥ hi dehabhṛt sadṛśām eva saṃvṛtim prāpnuyāt na adhika itarām vayam tṛṣitāḥ tu tathā anye api na viśeṣaḥ alpakaḥ adhikaḥ saṃtu nāryaḥ sahasrāṇi rūpa lāvaṇya bhūmayaḥ param nidhuvane kāle svāpe sukham yat upajāyate tat eva saukhyam nidrā abhibhūta bhū śāyinām api yathā eva maraṇāt bhītiḥ asmat ādi vapuṣmatām brahma ādi kīṭa kāntānām tathā tulyaḥ na kvāpi jagatī tale tasmāt sarva prayatnena kāryā jīva dayā nṛbhiḥ ekasmin rakṣite jīve trailokyam rakṣitam pu0 mad pūrva sūribhiḥ iti uktam sat pramāṇa tayā dhruvam tasmāt na hiṃsā karttavyā naraiḥ naraka bhīrubhiḥ na hiṃsā sadṛśam pāpam trailokya bhītebhyaḥ ca abhayam deyam yādhitebhyaḥ tathā auṣadham deyā vidyā arthinām vidyā deyam annam kṣudhā āture yāni yāni iha ca na arhati ṣoḍaśīm a vicitya prabhāvam hi maṇi mantra auṣadham balam tat abhyasyam prayatnena nāma artha upārjanāya vai artha anupāye bahuśas hi dvādaśa āyatanāni vai paritas paripūjyāni kim anyaiḥ iha pūjitaiḥ dvādaśa āyatanam śubham iha eva svarga narakau prāṇinām na anyatas kvacid sukham svargaḥ samākhyātaḥ duḥkham narakam eva hi sukheṣu paramaḥ mokṣaḥ vijñeyaḥ tattva cintakaiḥ paramaḥ mokṣaḥ vijñeyaḥ tattva cintakaiḥ prāmāṇikā śrutiḥ iyam procyate veda vādibhiḥ na hiṃsyāt sarva bhūtāni na anyā hiṃsā pravartakā agnīṣṭomīyam iti yā bhrāmikā sā asatām iha na sā pramāṇam jñātṝṇām paśu ālambhana kārakā vṛkṣān chitvā paśūn hatvā tathā khilān paurān uvāca punar ādarāt yācamāna manas vṛtti prīṇane yasya naḥ janiḥ tena bhū bhīravatī eṣā samudra āga drumaiḥ na hi sa tvaram gatvā araḥ dehaḥ saṃcayāḥ saṃparityayāḥ iti prasādhayet ca prātar bhojyam idam vapuḥ ca prātar bhojyam idam vapuḥ prapaṭhyate sudhā jāti vikalpaḥ yam lokeṣu parikalpyate mānuṣye sati sāmānye kaḥ adharmaḥ kaḥ atha ca uttamaḥ brahma ādi sṛṣṭiḥ eṣā iti bṛddha puruṣaiḥ procyate vṛddha puruṣaiḥ tasya jātau sutau dakṣa marīcī ca iti viśrutau mārīcena kaśyapena dakṣa kanyāḥ su locanāḥ dharmeṇa kila mārgeṇa trayodaśa nairmatyaiḥ alpabuddhi parākramaiḥ api gamyaḥ tu agamyaḥ ayam vicāraḥ kriyate sudhā cāturvarṇyam saha uditam kalpanā iyam kṛtā pūrvaiḥ na ghaṭeta vicārāt ekasyām ca tanau jātāḥ ekāt yadi vā kvacid catvāraḥ tanayāḥ tat kim uvāca ittham ābhāṣya daitya īśam paurān ca saḥ yatiḥ yune sa śiṣyaḥ veda dharmān ca nāśayāmāsa ca ādarāt strī dharmam khaṇḍayāmāsa pātivratya param mahat jita indriya tvam sarveṣām puruṣāṇām tathā eva saḥ deva dharmān viśeṣeṇa śrāddha dharmāḥ tathā eva ca tīrtha śrāddham viśeṣataḥ śiva pūjām viśeṣeṇa liṅga ārādhana pūrvakām viṣṇu sūrya gaṇeśa ādi pūjanam vidhi pūrvakam taḥ yatiḥ māyī māyāvinām varaḥ khaṇḍayāmāsa saḥ yatiḥ māyī māyāvinām varaḥ kim bahu uktena vipra indraiḥ tripure tena māyinā veda dharmāḥ ca ye kecid te sarve dūratas kṛtāḥ pati dharma āśrayāḥ sarvāḥ mohitāḥ tripura aṅganāḥ bhṛrtṛ śuśrūṣaṇavatīm vijahuḥ matim uttamām abhyasya ākaṃrṣaṇām vidyām vaśīkṛtya mayīm api phalīcakruḥ para dāreṣu mohitāḥ antar pura carāḥ nāryaḥ tathā rāja kumārakāḥ paurāḥ pura aṅganāḥ ca api sarve vimohitāḥ sarveṣu nija dharmeṣu sarvathā parāṅmukheṣu jāteṣu prolalāsa vṛṣetaraḥ māyā ca devadevasya viṣṇoḥ tasya ājñayā prabho buddhi moham tathābhūtam yathā māyā vinirmitam teṣām da tvā kṣaṇāt eva kṛtārthaḥ abhūt saḥ nāradaḥ nāradaḥ api tathārūpaḥ yathā māyī tathā eva saḥ tathā api vikṛtaḥ na abhūt param pa rama īśāt anugrahāt daitya rājaḥ api bho mune bhrātṛbhyām sahitaḥ tatra ca śiva icchayā mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddhakhaṇḍe tripuramohanam nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sthitvā asau devaiḥ saha ramāpatiḥ tatas bhūri saṃ ca brahmā parameṇa samādhinā manasā prāpya sarvajñam brahmanā saḥ hariḥ tadā maheśvaram devāya namaḥ te puruṣottamaḥ pu0 mahādevam daṇḍa vat praṇipatya haṃ jajāpa rudra mantram ca dakṣiṇāmūrti sambhavam jajāpa rudra mantram ca dakṣiṇāmūrti sambhavam jale sthitvā sārdha koṭi pramitam tad manāḥ prabhuḥ manasā mama aham aham svaprabhum parameśvaram tāvat devāḥ tadā sarve tad manaskāḥ maheśvaram ūcuḥ namaḥ sarvātmane te śaṃkarāya ārti hāriṇe nīla tvam eva jagantām kartā bhartā hartā tvam eva hi hṛd puṇḍarīka vibare yoginām tvam hi saṃsthitaḥ vadanti vedāḥ tvām santaḥ para brahma svarūpiṇam tvam eva śarvaiḥ sarva ātmānam iti āhuḥ asmin jaganti yat vibho tvam eva śarvaiḥ sarva ātman triloka adhipate bhavam dṛṣṭam śrutam stutam sarvam jñāyamānam tvā namāmi ca sarvatas sarvajñam sarvatas vyāpin sarveśvaram anāvṛtam viśvarūpam virūpākṣam tvā namāmi ca sarvatas bhāskara saṃkāśam tvām namāmi ca sarvatas viśvadevam anādyantam ṣaṭtriṃśatkam anīśvaram pravartakam ca sarveṣām tvām namāmi ca sarva ca pravartakam ca prakṛtyāḥ sarvasya prapitāmaham sarva vigraham īśam hi tvām namāmi ca sarvatas evam vadanti vara dam sarva āvāsam svayam tvām eva deva asura surāḥ ca anye ca vai sthāvara jaṃgamāḥ ca pāhi ananyagatī śambho surān naḥ deva vallabhaiḥ naṣṭa prāya tripurāt vinihatya asurān kṣaṇāt kuru uvāca iti stutvā maheśānam devāḥ tu puratas sthitāḥ kṛta añjali puṭāḥ dīnāḥ āsan saṃnata mūrtayaḥ stutaḥ ca evam sura indra ādyaiḥ viṣṇoḥ jāpi enam ca īśvaraḥ agacchat tatra sarva īśaḥ vṛṣam āruhya harṣitaḥ viṣṇum āliṃgya nandīśāt avāruhya prasanna dhīḥ dadarśa tatra nandī datta karaḥ akhilān tatra nandī datta karaḥ akhilān atha devān samālokya kṛpā dṛṣṭyā harim haraḥ prāha gambhīrayā vācā prasannaḥ pārvatīpatiḥ adharmaiḥ teṣām daityānām deva sattamaḥ puratraya vināśam ca kariṣye aham na saṃśayaḥ parantu te mahā daityāḥ madbhakāḥ dṛḍha mānasāḥ vadhyā mayā eva syuḥ vyāja tyakta vṛṣa uttamāḥ iti śambhoḥ tu vacanam śrutvā sarve divaukasaḥ vimanaskāḥ babhruvuḥ te hariḥ ca api muni īśvaraiḥ devān viṣṇum udāsīnān dṛṣṭvā ca bhava kṛt vidhiḥ brahmā vacanam abravīt uvāca na kiṃcid vidyate pāpam yasmāt tvam yoga vittamaḥ parameśaḥ para brahma sadā sura ṛṣi prāṇa rakṣaka sādhūnām rakṣaṇa arthāya iṃtavyāḥ mleccha jātayaḥ rājñaḥ tasya na tat pāpam vidyate dharmāt te tasmāt rakṣet dijān sādhūn kaṃ yat iṭakāt vai viśodhayet evam icchet iha anyatra rājā ced rājyam ātmanaḥ prabhu tvam sarva lokānām tasmāt rakṣasva māciram muni indra īśāḥ tathā yajñāḥ vedāḥ śāstra ādayaḥ ukhilāḥ prajāḥ te devadeveśaiḥ hi aham viṣṇuḥ api dhruvam devatā sārvabhaumaḥ tvam samrāj sarva īśvaraḥ prabho parivāraḥ te eva eṣa hari ādi sakalam jagant yuvarājaḥ hariḥ tejaiḥ brahmā aham te purohitaḥ rāja kārya karaḥ śukaḥ tvad ājñā paripālakaḥ yam iha prabhuḥ kaścid vahṇīyām yam iha prabhuḥ rathaḥ na asti mahā divyaḥ tāharū sārathinā saha dhanuḥ bāṇa ādikam ca api saṃgrāme jaya kārakam āsthāya gṛhītvā yojya vai manaḥ nihaniṣyāmi aham daityān prabalān api saṃgare nihaniṣyāmi aham daityān prabalān api saṃgare uvāca praharṣitāḥ śrutvā prabhoḥ tadā vākyam natvā procuḥ maheśvaram ūcuḥ vayam bhavāma deveśaiḥ tad prakārāḥ maheśvaraiḥ ratha ādikā te svāmin saṃgrāma yad naddhāḥ saṃgarāya hi iti uktvā saṃhatāḥ sarve śiva icchām adhigamya ha pṛthak ūcuḥ prasannāḥ te kṛtāñjali puṭāḥ surāḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śivastutivarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ pu0 haraḥ aṃgīcakāra su prītyā śaraṇyaḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ etasmin antare devī putrābhyām saṃyutā śivā ājagāma tatra yatra deva anvitaḥ haraḥ āsa na jānataḥ tad āgamana kāraṇam atha sarvaiḥ stutā devaiḥ devī adbhuta kutūhalā uvāca svāminam prītyā nānā līlā viśāradam bho paśya ṣaṇmukham ravi saṃnibham putram putravatām śreṣṭham bhūṣitam bhūṣaṇa evaraiḥ iti evam lokamātrā ca vāgbhiḥ saṃbodhitaḥ śivaḥ maśānaḥ piban skanda ānana amṛtam na sasmāra āgatān daityān nija tejas nipīḍitān skandam āliṃgya ca atrāya sumodā ati maheśvaraḥ jagadambā atha tatra eva saṃmantrya prabhuṇā ca sā sthitvā kiṃcid samuttasthau nānā līlā viśāradā tatas sa nandī saha ṣaṇmukhena tayā ca sārdham girirājaputryā śambhu kim kartavyam kva kaḥ syāt mad sukha pradaḥ kim tu kim tu iti saṃjātam hā hatāḥ sma iti vādinam surāḥ tasmin eva antare teṣām śrutvā śabdān anekaśas kumbhodaraḥ mahā tejāḥ daṃḍena atāḍayat surān dudruvuḥ te bhaya āviṣṭāḥ devāḥ hāhā iti tāḥ iti evam vacanam śrutvā kaśyapa ādi uditam mune āśvāsayan munīn devān hariḥ vākyam upādade viṣṇuḥ uvāca he devāḥ munayaḥ sarve mad vacaḥ mahat ārādhanam devāḥ na susādhyam vicāryatām śrutam vijñāya dṛḍha tām devāḥ prasannaḥ bhavati dhruvam śivaḥ sarva gaṇādhyakṣaḥ sahasā parameśvaraḥ vicāryatām hṛdā sarvaiḥ katham vaśyaḥ bhave praṇavam pūrvam uccāryam namaḥ paścāt udāharet śivāya iti tatas paścāt śubhadrayam atas param tatas proktam śivāya ca tatas maṃtram evam sadā budhāḥ namaḥ ca praṇavaḥ ca eva mantram evam sadā budhāḥ āvartadhvam punar yūyam yadi śambhu kṛte tadā koṭimakam tathā jatvā śivaḥ kāryam kari tathā iti ukte ca tadā tena hariṇā prabhaviṣṇunā tathā devāḥ punar cakruḥ harasya ārādhanam saṃjajāpa hariśvā api sa vidhiḥ śiva mānasaḥ devānām kārya siddhi artham munīnām ca viśeṣataḥ he hare he vidhe devāḥ munayaḥ ca śubhavatāḥ ca rakṣa asmān parameśānaiḥ dīna bandho kṛpā karaiḥ svayā eva rakṣitāḥ devāḥ sadā āpadbhyaḥ muhur muhur vacanam teṣām śrutvā saṃhari vedhasām vihasya antar tadā brahman maheśaḥ punar abravīt he hare he vidhe devāḥ munayaḥ ca akhilā madīyam śṛṇuta ādṛtya naṣṭam matvā puratrayam ratham ca sārathim divyam kārmukam śaram uttamam pūrvam aṅgīkṛtam sarvam upapādayata aciram āyuṣyaḥ svarga kāma arthinām nṛṇām hi akāmānām muktānām bhukti mukti daḥ yaḥ imam kīrtayet mantram śuciḥ bhūtvā sadā naraḥ sarva deva mayam divyam ratham parama śobhanam racayāmāsa viśvakarmā tad ājñayā tāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe devastutivarṇanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ īśituḥ brū īśvaraḥ sanatkumāraḥ provāca smṛtvā śiva pada ambujam śaitra ka sukha āvah iti artha pu0 sādaram sarva bhūta mayaḥ ca eva sauvarṇaḥ sarva saṃmataḥ ratha gam dakṣiṇam sūryaḥ tad vāmam somaḥ eva ca dakṣiṇam dvādaśa aram hi ṣoḍaśa aram tathā uttara teṣu vipra indra ādityāḥ dvādaśa eva tu tu eva xcṣaṇam ṛtavaḥ nemayaḥ ṣaṭ ca tayoḥ vai vipra puṃgavaiḥ puṣkaram ca antarikṣam vai rathanīḍaḥ ca mandaraḥ asta ādviḥ udaya ādiḥ tu tau ubhau kūbarau smṛtau adhiṣṭhānam mahā meruḥ āśrayāḥ kesara acalāḥ vega saṃvatsarāḥ tasya ayane cakra saṃgamau muhūrtāḥ baṃdhurāḥ tasya mahyaḥ ca eva kalāḥ smṛtāḥ tasya kāṣṭhāḥ smṛtāḥ ghoṇā śvāsadaṃḍāḥ kṣaṇāḥ ca vai nimeṣā ca anukarṣaḥ ca īṣā śva anulavāḥ smṛtāḥ prakoṇāḥ tasya api ahaṃkāraḥ bhūtāni ca balam smṛtam indriyāṇi ca tasya eva bhūṣaṇāni samaṃtataḥ śraddhā ca gatiḥ asya eva rathasya muni sattamaiḥ tadānīm bhūṣaṇāni eva ṣaḍaṅgāni upabhūṣaṇam purāṇa nyāya mīmāṃsā dharma śāstrāṇi suvratāḥ balāśayāḥ varāḥ ca eva sarva lakṣaṇaiḥ mantrāḥ ghaṇṭāḥ smṛtāḥ teṣām varṇa pādāḥ tad āśramāḥ ayaḥ vandhaḥ hi anantaḥ tu sahasra phaṇa bhūṣitaḥ diśaḥ pādāḥ rathasya asya tathā ca upa mahā ādyāḥ sauvarṇāḥ diśaḥ ca ha puṣkara ādyāḥ sauvarṇāḥ ratna bhūṣitāḥ samudrāḥ tasya catvāraḥ rathakaṃbalinaḥ smṛtāḥ gaṅgā ādyāḥ saritaḥ mad sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ cāmara āsakta hasta agrāḥ sarva astrī rūpa śobhitāḥ tatra tatra kṛta sthānāḥ śobhayāṃcakrire ratham mānasa ādiḥ tu śobhanaḥ pāśāḥ samantataḥ tasya sarve varṣācalāḥ smṛtāḥ talāḥ tasya rathasya atha sarve tala nivāsinaḥ sārathiḥ bhagavān brahmā devāḥ raśmidharāḥ mṛtāḥ pratodaḥ brahmanaḥ tasya praṇavaḥ brahma daivatam akāraḥ ca mahat chattram mandaraḥ pārśva daṇḍa bhāj śaila indraḥ kārmukam tasya jyā bhujaṃgāḥ tasya tathā proktāḥ catvāraḥ nigamāḥ mune jyotīṃṣi bhūṣaṇam teṣām avaśiṣṭāni atas param yu0 ārṣam ṛṣayaḥ vyāsa mukhyāḥ ca vāha vāhāḥ tathā abhavan su alpa akṣaraiḥ tat travīmi kim sunīśvaraiḥ brahmāṇḍe ca eva yat kiṃcid vastu tat vai rathe evam samyak kṛtaḥ tena dhīmatā viśvakarmaṇā saḥ ratha ādi prakāraḥ hi brahma viṣṇu ājñayā śubhaḥ dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe rathādiyuddhaprakāravarṇanam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nānā āścarya mayam ratham saṃnahya nigamān aśvān tam brahmā prārpayat śitram śambhave asau nivedya adhiropayāmāsa śūlinam viṣṇunā brahmaṇā ca api lokapālaiḥ babhūva ha hati ratham kalpitam loka saṃbhṛtam śirobhiḥ patitāḥ bhūmau turaṃgāḥ veda sambhavāḥ cacāla vasudhā celuḥ sakalāḥ ca mahīdharāḥ sahasā heṣaḥ asoḍhā tad bhāram āturaḥ atha adhas saḥ rathasya asya bhagavān dharaṇīdharaḥ vṛṣa indra rūpī ca utthāya sthāpayāmāsa vai kṣaṇam varam nāt vai ratham varam tatas asau nodayāmāsa manaḥ māruta raṃhasaḥ brahmā hayān veda mayān naddhān ratha vara etaḥ purāṇi udiśya vai trīṇi teṣām kha hi adhiṣṭhite maheśe tu dānavānām tarasviṇām adhiṣṭhite maheśe tu dānavānām tarasviṇām atha āha bhagavant nudraḥ devān ālokya śaṃkaraḥ paśūnām ādhipatyam mama hanmi asurān asurān pṛthak paśu tvam devānām tathā anyeṣām sura uttamāḥ kalpayitvā eva vadhyāḥ te na anyathā daitya sattamāḥ uvāca iti śrutvā vacaḥ tasya devadevasya dhīmataḥ viṣādam agaman sa vai paśu tvam pratiśaṃkitāḥ teṣām bhāvam atha jñātvā devadevaḥ ambikāpatiḥ bhaviṣyatām ca saḥ vai pāśupatam divyam cariṣyati saḥ mokṣyati paśu tvāt iti satyam vaḥ pratijñātam samāhitāḥ ca api anye kariṣyanti mama vratam pāśupatam mama mokṣyanti te na saṃdehaḥ paśu tvāt sura sattamāḥ naiṣṭhikam dvādaśa abdam vā tad ardha varṣaka trayam śuśrūṣām kārayet yaḥ tu saḥ paśu tasmāt param idam divyam vimucyate cariṣyatha sura uttamāḥ paśu tvāt mokṣyatha tadā yūyam atra na saṃśayaḥ uvāca pu0 sarve devarṣayaḥ tadā amudan ca ati deveśaḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ pare api ca hi varṣa śataiḥ api evaṃvidhaḥ maheśānaḥ maheśāni akhila īśvaraḥ jagāma tripuram hetum sarveṣām sukha dāyakaḥ tam devadevam tripuram nirhatum tadā nu sarve tu ravi prakāśāḥ gajaiḥ hayaiḥ siṃha varaiḥ rathaiḥ ca vṛṣaiḥ yayuḥ te amara rāja mukhyāḥ halaiḥ ca śāḻemu śalabhu śuḍagarī indra kalpaiḥ giri saṃnibhāḥ ca saṃyuta bāhavaḥ te tatas nu hṛṣṭāḥ prayayuḥ sura īśāḥ nānā āyudha āḍhyāḥ parama prakāśāḥ mahā utsavāḥ śambhu jayam vadataḥ tadā indra padmodbhava viṣṇu mukhyāḥ jahaṣuḥ munayaḥ sarve daṇḍa hastāḥ jaṭā dharāḥ vavṛtuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddha cāraṇāḥ vacmi gaṇa īśvaraiḥ deva gaṇaiḥ ca bhṛṅgī samāvṛtaḥ sarva gaṇa indra varyaḥ jagāma yogān tripuram nihantum vimānam āruhya yathā mahā indraḥ keśaḥ vigatavāsaḥ ca mahākeśaḥ mahājvaraḥ somavallīsavarṇaḥ ca somapassanakaḥ tathā sūryavarcāḥ ca sūryapreṣaṇakaḥ tathā sūryākṣaḥ sūri nāmā ca surasundaraḥ eva ca mahā indra jayaḥ ca eva yantā himakaraḥ tathā śatākṣaḥ ca eva pañcākṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ mahodaraḥ karpūrapūtanaḥ lakṣya mahādevam tadā āpuḥ te pinākinam samāvṛtya mahādevam tadā āpuḥ te pinākinam dagdhum samarthāḥ manasā kṣaṇena sacarācaram dagdhum jagant sarvam idam samarthāḥ tvam ca dagdhum tripuram pinākī rathena kim ca atra śareṇa tasya gaṇaiḥ ca kim deva gaṇaiḥ ca śambhoḥ saḥ eva dagdhum tripurāṇi tāni deva dviṣām vyāsaiḥ svayam gataḥ tatra gaṇaiḥ ca sārdham nijaiḥ surāṇām api saḥ adbhuta ūtiḥ kim tatra kāraṇam ca anyat vacmi te ṛṣi sattama khyāpa na arthe vai yaśaḥ para mala apaham anyat ca kāraṇam hi etat duṣṭānām pratyayāya vai sarveṣu api ca deveṣu yasmāt na anyaḥ viśiṣyate mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śivayātrāvarṇanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ratha sthaḥ sarva saṃyutaḥ tripuram sakalam dagdhum udyataḥ abhūt suradviṣām śīrṣa sthānakam āsthāya saṃdhāya ca śara uttamam sannam tat kārmukam kṛtvā pratyālīḍham niveśya dṛḍhamuṣṭau ca dṛṣṭim dṛṣṭau niveśya ca atiṣṭa niścalaḥ tatra śatam varṣa sahasrakam tatas uḍuṣṭhe gaṇādhyakṣaḥ sa tudati aniśam sthitaḥ na lakṣyam viviśuḥ tāni purāṇi asya triśūliṇaḥ tatas uṃtarikṣādaiḥ śṛṇot dhanus bāṇa dharaḥ haraḥ muñjakeśaḥ virūpākṣaḥ vācam parama śobhanām bho na yāvat bhagavant na arcitaḥ asau vināyakaḥ purāṇi jagadīśa īśaiḥ sāṃpratam na haniṣyati etat śrutvā tu vacanam gaja vakram apūjayat bhadrakālīm samāhūya tatas udhaka niṣūdanaḥ tasmin saṃpūjite harṣāt parituṣṭe puraḥsare vināyake tatas vyomi dadarśa bhagavant haraḥ trīṇi daityānām tārakāṇām mahātmanām yathātatham hi yuktāni kecid ittham vadanti ha para brahmani deveśaiḥ sarva upāsye maheśvare anya prasādāt kārya devasya vara dātuḥ maheśituḥ mumucuḥ stuvantaḥ ca aṣṭamūrtinam atha āha iti tadā brahmā jagantām patiḥ samayaḥ api samāyātaḥ daityānām vadha karmaṇaḥ teṣām tāraka putrāṇām tripurāṇām maheśvaraiḥ deva kāryam kuru vibho ekatvam api ca āgatam yāvat na yānti deveśaiḥ viprayogam tāvat vāṇam vimuṃcaḥ ca tripuram bhasmasātkuru atha sajyam dhanuḥ kṛtvā śarvaḥ saṃdhāya tam śaram pūjya pāśupata astram saḥ tripuram samacitayat atha devaḥ mahādevaḥ vara līlā viśāradaḥ kena api kāraṇena atra sa avajñam tat avaikṣata puratrayam virūpākṣaḥ kartum tat bhasmasāt kṣaṇāt dussaham ātmanaḥ nām viśrāvya samābhāṣya mahā asurān mārtaṃḍa koṭi vapuṣam kāṇḍam ugraḥ sumoca ha tyān trī vimala apahaḥ saḥ āśu gaḥ viṣṇu mayaḥ vahni tena satyena bhūyas api kadā tvam pradahiṣyasi śra drutam dagdhāḥ bhasmasāt abhavat mune anye api vālāḥ vṛddhāḥ ca dānavāḥ tena vahninā śiva ājñayā drutam vyāsaiḥ nirdagdhāḥ bhasmasātkṛtāḥ striyaḥ vā puruṣāḥ vā api vāhanāni ca tatra ye sarve tena agninā dagdhāḥ kalpa ante tu jagant yathā bhartṝn kaṇṭha gatān hitvā kān vidagdhāḥ vara striyaḥ babhramu maham ūcchitāḥ tena na āsīt su sūkṣmaḥ api ghora tripura vahninā tasmāt yatnaiḥ sat bhaktaiḥ maheśa śaraṇa āgatam sarveṣām daivāt yadi yatas bhavet brahmapurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe tripuradāhavarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca brahma putra mahā prājña dhanyaḥ tvam śaivaiḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vyāsa vākyam bhagavant bhava kṛt sutaḥ sanatkumāraḥ provāca śiva pāda yugam smaran uvāca haritam śṛṇu vyāsaiḥ mahābuddhe pārāśaryaiḥ mahā uśituḥ caritam loka līlā anusāriṇaḥ maheśvareṇa sarvasmin tripure daitya saṃkule dagdhe viśeṣataḥ tatra tam diśaḥ daśa koṭi sūrya pratīkāśam pralaya anala saṃnibham bhayāt devam nirīkṣya eva devīm ca himavat sutām biyire nikhilāḥ deva pramukhāḥ tasthuḥ dṛṣṭvā anīkam tadā bhītam devānām ṛṣi puṃgavāḥ na kiṃcid ūcuḥ saṃtasthuḥ praṇemuḥ te samaṃtataḥ tuṣṭāva tuṣṭa hṛdayaḥ devaiḥ saha samāhitaḥ viṣṇunā ca sa bhītena devadevam bhavam haram tripurārim sa girijam bhakta adhīnam maheśvaram namaḥ te svargeśāya namaḥ astu te sadāśivāya śāntāya maheśāya pinākine sarvajñāya śaraṇyāya sadyojātāya te namaḥ rudrāya tadā api apuruṣāya ca tripura kalā amarān dagdhvā ca tripuram sarve kṛtārthāḥ amarāḥ kṛtāḥ stutvā evam devatāḥ sarvāḥ namaskāram pṛthak pṛthak cakuḥ te parama prītāḥ brahma ādyāḥ tu tuṣṭāva praṇataḥ bhūtvā nata skandhaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ śaṃkaraiḥ tvayi bhaktiḥ parā mama astu mahādeva anapāyinī bhava vibho sadā tvam parameśvaraiḥ janārdanaḥ api bhagavant namaskṛtya maheśvaram kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā tuṣṭāva ca maheśvaram uvāca bhairava īśaiḥ maheśānaiḥ dīna bandho kṛpā karaiḥ prasīda parameśānaiḥ kṛpām kuru nata priyaiḥ nirguṇāya namaḥ punar ca saguṇāya ca prakṛti rūpāya punar ca puruṣāya ca ca paśvāt guṇa svarūpāya nataḥ viśvātmane namaḥ bhakti priyāya śāntāya śivāya paramātmane tvāya bhaktiḥ dṛḍhā mama adya bardhamānā bhavatu iti mahā bhaktiḥ dṛḍhā naḥ nityam anapāyinī uvāca iti stutaḥ ca deveśaḥ brahmanā hariṇā amaraiḥ pratyuvāca prasanna ātmā śaṃkaraḥ loka śaṃkaraḥ uvāca he vidhe he hare devāḥ prasannaḥ asmi viśeṣataḥ manas abhilaṣitam brūta varam sarve vicārāt tvayā devadeveśaiḥ ca naḥ jñātvā dāsān hi naḥ surān yadā duḥkham tu devānām saṃbhavet deva sattamaiḥ tadā tvam prakaṭaḥ bhūtvā duḥkham pu0 sarvadā uvāca iti uktaḥ bhagavant rudraḥ brahmanā hariṇā amaraiḥ yugapad prāha tuṣṭa ātmā tathā iti astu niraṃtaram stavaiḥ etaiḥ ca tuṣṭaḥ asmi dāsyāmi sarvadā dhruvam yat abhīṣṭatamam loke paṭhatām śṛṇvatām surāḥ iti uktā śaṃkaraḥ prītaḥ deva duḥkha tat sarvam haraḥ sadā sarva deva priyam yat vai tat sarvam ca pradattavan nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca etasmin antare śambhum prasannam vīkṣya dānavaḥ praṇanāma haram prītyā surān anyān api dhruvam kṛtāñjaliḥ nata skandhaḥ praṇanāma punar śivam atha utthāya śivam tuṣṭāva bhakti pūrṇa ātmā saḥ dānava varaḥ mayaḥ rāja bhakti pūrṇa ātmā saḥ dānava varaḥ mayaḥ uvāca devadevaiḥ mahādevaiḥ akasmāt sarva lokapaiḥ jātakarma ādi saṃskārān kuruṣva asya jagadguro taruṇaḥ sarva śāstra artha pāragaḥ mahā parākramaḥ dhīraḥ yoddhā ca raṇa durmadaḥ bhaviṣyati ca gambhīraḥ tvam yathā samare guhaḥ sarva jetā ca saṃgrāme sarva saṃpad virājitaḥ daityānām adhipaḥ vālaḥ sarveṣām ca bhaviṣyati viṣṇoḥ api bhavet jetā na kutaśvid parābhavaḥ mad śīla sāgarā tānām pravaraḥ sudhīḥ sādhu sva karma nipuṇaḥ ākarṇya maheśasya vacaḥ saṃnibham te sarve pramudā hi āsan naṣṭam matvā ca dānavam hariḥ jagāma vaikuṇṭhaiḥ satya loke vidhiḥ tadā praṇipatya maheśam ca sura ādyāḥ sva yayuḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śaṃkhacūḍavadhe śivopadeśaḥ nāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atha īśānaḥ mahā rudraḥ duṣṭa kālaḥ satām gatiḥ śaṃkhacūḍa vadham citte niścikāya sura icchayā dūtam kṛtvā citraratham gandharva aiśvara mīpsitam śīghram prasthāpayāmāsa śaṃkhacūḍa antike mudām sarveśvara ājñayā dūtaḥ yayau tat nagaram ca saḥ mahendra nagara utkṛṣṭam kubera bhavana adhikam gatvā dadarśa tad madhye śaṃkhacūḍa ālayam varam rājitam dvādaśa airi dvārapāla samanvitam saḥ dṛṣṭvā puṣpadantaḥ tu varam dvāram dadarśa saḥ kathayāmāsa tad dvārapālāya nirbhayaḥ atikramya ca tad dāram jagāma abhyantare mudā atīva sundaram ramyam vistīrṇa samalaṃkṛtam tam dadarśa danuja adhipam vīra maṇḍala madhya stham ratna siṃhāsana sthitam dānava indraḥ parivṛtam sevitam ca tri koṭibhiḥ ha anyaiḥ ca bhramadbhiḥ śastra pāṇibhiḥ evaṃbhūtam ca tam dṛṣṭvā puṣpadantaḥ sa vismayaḥ uvāca raṇa vṛttāntaiḥ yat uktam śaṃkareṇa ca uvāca rāja indraiḥ śiva dūtaḥ aham puṣpadanta abhidhaḥ prabho uktam śaṃkareṇa eva tat śṛṇu tvam bravīmi te uvāca dehi ca devānām adhikāram hi sāṃpratam no ced kuru raṇam sārdham pareṇa ca mayā satām devāḥ mām śaraṇa āpannāḥ deveśam śaṃkaram satām rājyam dāsyasi kim vā tvam kariṣyasi raṇam ca kim tat tvam brūhi dvayoḥ ekam dānava indraiḥ vicāryam vai iti uktam yat mahe tubhyam tat mama niveditam vitatham śambhra vākyam na kadāpi danuja adhipa aham sva svāminam gantum icchāmi tvaritam haram gatvā vakṣyāmi kim hanta tathā tvam vada mām iha saḥ pari prayāyī syāt sa vīraḥ bhuvane adhamaḥ atas pūrvam aham rudra tvām gamiṣyāmi asaṃśayam prabhāte āgamiṣyāmi vīra yātrā vicārāt gacchā cakṣva rudrāya hi īdṛśam vacanam mama iti śrutvā śaṃkhacūḍa vacanam su prahasya saḥ uvāca dānava indram saḥ śambhoḥ tu garvitam na sthātum sammukhe yogyaḥ kim punar tasya sammukham saḥ tvam dehi ca devānām adhikārāṇi sarvaśas hareḥ vidhaiḥ ca sa svāmī nirguṇaḥ sa guṇaḥ sa hi yasya bhrū bhaṅga mātreṇa sarveṣām pralayaḥ bhavet śivasya pūrṇa rūpaḥ ca loka saṃhāra kārakaḥ satām gatiḥ duṣṭa hantā nirvikāraḥ parātparaḥ mad śānam param brahma cit ātmakam dehi rājyam hi devānām adhikārān ca sarvaśas evam te kuśalam tātaiḥ bhaviṣyati anyathā bhayam uvāca iti saṃchinna dhvaja bāṇa asi tanutra vara bhūṣaṇāḥ mahā bhujaiḥ sā ābharaṇaiḥ saṃchinnaiḥ sa āyudhaiḥ tathā sahasā paṭalaiḥ vā sa sāraṅghaiḥ mṛdhe bhaṭāḥ pradhāvantaḥ kabandhān sva śira ukṣibhiḥ paśyantaḥ tatra ca utpetuḥ udyata āyudha sa gujaiḥ ati pu0 sa toyāḥ iva toyadāḥ sarvatas śara kūṭena vīraḥ sa ratha sārathim vīram saṃchādayāmāsa prāvṛṣ sūryam iva ambudaḥ cuyudhuḥ dvaṃdva yodhinaḥ āhvayantaḥ viśantaḥ aye kṣipataḥ marmabhiḥ mithas sarvatas vīra saṃghāḥ ca nānā bāhu dhvaja āyudhāḥ vyadṛśyaṃta mahā saṃkhye mahā ravān siṃha saṃravam sva śakhān ca vidadhmuḥ vai pṛthak pṛthak balganam cakrire tatra mahā vīrāḥ praharṣitāḥ evam cirataram kālam babhūva yuddham vikaṭam karālam vīraṃharṣa dam babhūva yuddham vikaṭam karālam vīraṃharṣa dam līlā iyam śaṃkarasya parātmanaḥ yayā saṃmohitam sarvam sa deva asura mānuṣam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śaṃkhacūḍa vadhe parasparayuddhavarṇanam nāma paṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tadā deva gaṇāḥ sarve dānavaiḥ aiśvaiḥ parājitāḥ dudruvuḥ bhaya bhītāḥ ca śastra astra kṣata vigrahāḥ te parāvṛtya viśveśam śaṃkaram śaraṇam yayuḥ trāhi iti sarva īśaiḥ iti ūcuḥ vihvalayā girā dṛṣṭvā parājayam teṣām deva ādīnām saḥ śaṃkaraḥ sa bhayam vacanam śrutvā kopam uccais cakāra ha nirakṣyi sa kṛpā dṛṣṭayā sa kṛpā dṛṣṭayā devebhyaḥ śva abhayam dadau balam ca sva gaṇānām vai vardhayāmāsa tejasā śiva ājñaptaḥ tadā skandaḥ dānavānām gaṇaiḥ saha yuyudhe nirbhayaḥ saṃkhye mahā vīraḥ hara ātmajaḥ kṛtvā krodham vīra śabdam devaḥ yaḥ tārakāntakaḥ śatakam samare sa jaghāna ha rudhiram pātayāmāsa kālī kamala locanā teṣām śirāṃsi saṃchidya babhakṣa sahasā ca sā teṣām ca dānavānām samantataḥ yuddham cakāra vividham sura dānava bhīṣaṇam śata lakṣam gaja indrāṇām śata lakṣam nṝṇām tathā samādāya eka hastena mukhe mahān kolāhalaḥ jātaḥ kkībānām ca bhayaṃkaraḥ punar skandaḥ prakupya uccais ha śara varṣī cakāra ha pātayāmāsa kṣayāt koṭiśas asura nāyakān dānavāḥ śara jālena skandasya kṣata vigrahāḥ bhītāḥ praduvuḥ sarve śeṣāḥ maraiḥ tadā vṛṣaparvā vipracitti daiśva api vikampanaḥ skaṃdena yuyudhuḥ sārdham tena sarve krameṇa ca mahā mārī ca yuyudhe na babhūva parāṅmukhā babhūvuḥ te kṣata aṅga aśvaiḥ skanda śakti prapīḍitāḥ mahā mārī skandayoḥ ca vijayaḥ bhūt tadā neduḥ dudubhayaḥ svarge puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ papāta ha samaram dṛṣṭvā mahā raudram tam adbhutam dānavānām kṣaya karam yathā prakṛti kalpakam dānavānām kṣaya karam yathā prakṛti kalpakam mahā mārīkṛtam tat ca upadravam kṣaya hetukam cukopa atīva sahasā saṃnaddhaḥ bhūt svayam tadā varam vimānam āruhya nānā śastra astra saṃyutam abhayam sarva vīrāṇām nānā ratna paricchadam mahā vīraiḥ śaṅkhacūḍaḥ jagāma cakāra ha devāḥ pradudruvuḥ sarve ye anye nandīśvara ādayaḥ ekaḥ eva kārttikeyaḥ tasthau samara mūrdhani parvatānām ca sarpāṇām nāgānām śākhinām tathā rājā cakāra vṛṣṭim ca durnivāryā bhayaṃkarām tad dṛṣṭayā prahataḥ skandaḥ babhūva śiva nandanaḥ nīhāreṇa ca sāṃdreṇa saṃvṛtau bhāskarau yathā cakāra avidan mahā māyī mahā balaḥ śaraṇa ekena divyena dhanuḥ ciccheda tasya vaiṃ divya astreṇa cakāra saḥ divya astreṇa cakāra saḥ cikṣepa sūrya ābhām tasya vakṣāse ghātinīm mūrchām avāpa sahasā tad prahāreṇa saḥ kṣaṇaiḥ punar ca cetanām prāpya kārttikaḥ para vīra hā ratna indra sāra nirmāṇam āruroha sva vāhanam smṛtvā pādau maheśasya sā ambe ṣaṇmukhaḥ śastra astrāṇi gṛhītvā eva cakāra raṇam ulbaṇam sappaḥ ca parvatān ca eva vṛkṣān ca prastarān tathā sarvāḥ ciccheda kopena divya astre mad śiva ātmajaḥ nivārayāmāsa pārjanyena śareṇa ha ratham dhanuḥ ca ciccheda śaṃkhacūḍasya līlayā ājvalam vīra śabdam cakāra asau jagarja ca punar punar cikṣepa śakti sūrya ābhām dānava indrasya vakṣāse ca muhūrta mātram tad kleśam vinīya saḥ mahā balaḥ cetanām prāpya ca uttasthau jagarja hari vacaṃsaḥ śaktyā jaghāna tam ca api kārti balam sa papāta mahī pṛṣṭhe moghām kurvan vidhi pradām kālī gṛhītvā tam kroḍe nināya śiva saṃnidhau jñānena tam śivaḥ ca api jīva bhadraḥ mahā balaḥ śaṅkhacūḍena yuyudhe samare bala śālinā vavarṣa samare astrāṇi yāni yāni ca dānavaḥ ciccheda līlayā vīraḥ tāni tāni śaraiḥ śaraiḥ divyāni astrāṇi śataśas mumuce dānava īśvaraḥ tāni ciccheda taṃ bāṇaiḥ vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān pratāpavān śaktyā jaghāna urasi tam sa cakampe patāta kau kṣaṇena cetanām prāpya samuttasthau gaṇeśvaraḥ jagrāha ca dhanuḥ bhūyas vīrabhadro vāhakāḥ punar samudyatāḥ ca āsan pu0 iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śaṃkhacūḍa vadhe sa sainya śaṃkhacūḍayuddhavarṇanam nāma adhyāyaḥ ca punar punar aṭṭaṭṭahāsam aśivam cakāra ca punar punar tadā papau ca mādhvīkam nanarta raṇa mūrdhani ugradaṃṣṭrā ca ugradaṇḍā koṭavī ca papau sura gaṇa ādayaḥ dṛṣṭvā kālīm śaṅkhacūḍaḥ śīghram ājau samāyayau dānavāḥ ca bhayam prāptāḥ rājā tebhyaḥ abhayam dadau kālī cikṣepa vahni ca pralaya agni śikhā upamam rājā jaghāna tam śīghram vaiṣṇava aṃkita līlayā rājā jaghāna tam śīghram vaiṣṇava aṃkita līlayā nārāyaṇa astram sāṃ devī cikṣepa tad upari aram vṛddhim jagāma tat chattram dṛṣṭvā mam ca dānavam tam dṛṣṭvā śaṅkhacūḍaḥ ca pralaya agni śikhā upamam papāta daṇḍa vat bhūmau praṇanāma punar punar nivṛttim prāpa tat chattram dṛṣṭvā namram dānavam brahmāstram atha sā devī cikṣepa mantra pūrvakam tam dṛṣṭvā prajjvalantam ca praṇamya bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ brahmāstreṇa dānava indraḥ vinirvāram cakāra jagarja sa aṭṭahāsam ca dānavāḥ bhayam āyayuḥ jagarja sa aṭṭahāsam ca dānavāḥ bhayam āyayuḥ kālyai cikṣepa śaktim sa śata yojanam āyatām devī divya astra jālena śata khaṇḍam cakāra sā ca ca cikṣepa caṇḍikā upari cakāra sarve devāḥ ca dānavāḥ api sarve devāḥ ca dānavāḥ api atha kruddhā mahā devī kālī kāla samā raṇe jagrāha mantra pūtam ca śaram pāśupatam ruṣā bhū pūrvam tat niṣeddhum vāc babhūva aśarīriṇī kṣepāt pūrvam tat niṣeddhum vāc babhūva aśarīriṇī na kṣipa astram imam devi śaṃkhacūḍāya vai ruṣā mṛtyuḥ pāśupatāt moghāt api ca caṇḍike maṅkhacūḍasya vīrasya upāyam anyam vicāraya iti ākarṇya bhadrakālī na cikṣepa tat astrakam śata lakṣam dānavānām jaghāsa līlayā kṣudhā attum jagāma vegena śaṅkhacūḍam bhayaṃkarā divya astreṇa ca raudreṇa vārayāmāsa dānavaḥ atha kruddhaḥ dānava indraḥ khaṅgam cikṣepa sa tvaram sūrya upamam tīkṣṇa dhāram atyanta bhīkaram sā kālī tam samālokya āyatim prajjvalitam ruṣā prasārya mukham āhāram cakre tasya ca paśyataḥ divyāni astrāṇi ca anyāni ciccheda dānava īśvaraḥ prāptāni pūrvatas cakre śata khaṇḍāni tāni ca punar atam mahādevī vegatas tam ma gāma ha sarva siddha īśvaraḥ śrīmān antardhānam cakāra saḥ vegena muṣṭinā kālī tam a dṛṣṭvā ca dānavam babhañja ca ratham tasya jaghāna kila sārathim devī tam tadā cakram vāma hastena līlayā jagrāha sva mukhena eva āhāram vīrabhadra ādi saṃyutaḥ bhairavaiḥ kṣetrapālaiḥ ca sva samāna prāptaḥ maheśaḥ ca vīra rūpam vidhāya ca raṇam prāptaḥ maheśaḥ ca vīra rūpam vidhāya ca virarāja adhikam tatra rudraḥ mūrtaḥ iva antakaḥ
