paṭhet vā api pāṭhayet vā sudhīḥ naraḥ dhanam dhānyam sutam saukhyam labheta atra na saṃśayaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnoti śiva bhakti bhavet dhana āḍhyaḥ vaiśya jaḥ śūdra śṛṇvan sattama tām iyāt iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śaṃkhacūḍa vadhaḥ mahākhyānam nāma catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavān vīrya ādhānam cakāra ha tulasyāḥ kena yatnena yonau tat vai arhasi uvāca nārāyaṇaḥ hi devānām kārya kartā satām gatiḥ śaṃkhacūḍasya rūpeṇa reme tat ramayā saha tat eva śṛṇu viṣṇoḥ śva caritam pramudā āvaham śiva śāsana kartuḥ ca mātuḥ ca jagantām hareḥ raṇa madhye vyoma vacaḥ śrutvā devena śambhunā tvaritam preritaḥ śaṃkhacūḍasya gṛhītvā kavacam param vipra rūpeṇa tvaritam māyayā nijayā hariḥ jagāma śaṃkhacūḍasya rūpeṇa tulasī gṛham dadarśa parama ādarāt yayau yayau tāmbūlam ca dadau tasmai karpūra ādi su vāsitam mama saphalam janma jīvanam saṃbabhūva ha raṇe gatam ca prāṇeśam paśyatyāḥ ca punar gṛhe iti uktvā sa kaṭākṣam sā nirīkṣya sa smitam mudā papraccha raṇaiḥ raṇaiḥ vṛttatim kāntam madhurayā girā uvāca prabho kartum sārdham ca tena eva samaram tvam gataḥ prabho katham babhūva saṃgrāmaḥ tena deva sahāyinā katham babhūva saṃgrāmaḥ tena deva sahāyinā kuśalī tvam iha āyātaḥ tam jitvā parameśvaram vijayaḥ te brūhi tat eva me śrutvā ittham tulasī vākyam saḥ vihasya ramāpatiḥ śaṅkhacūḍa rūpa dharaḥ tām uvāca amṛtam vacaḥ uvāca yadā aham raṇa bhūmau ca jagāma samara priyaḥ kolāhalaḥ mahān yātaḥ pravṛttaḥ abhūt mahā raṇaḥ deva dānavayoḥ yuddham saṃbabhūva jaya eṣiṇoḥ jitāḥ tantra nirjaraiḥ bala garvitaiḥ tadā aham samaram tatra akāryam devaiḥ bala utkaṭaiḥ parājitāḥ ca te devāḥ śaṃkaram śaraṇam yayuḥ rudraḥ api tad sahāyā mama artham ājagāma raṇam prati tena aham vai ciram kālam ayaut sa bala darpitaḥ tena aham vai ciram kālam ayaut sa bala darpitaḥ āvayoḥ samaraḥ kānte pūrṇam abdam babhūva nāśaḥ babhūva sarveṣām asurāṇām prītim ca kārayāmāsa brahmā ca svayam āvayoḥ prītim ca kārayāmāsa brahmā ca svayam āvayoḥ devānām adhikārāḥ ca pradattāḥ a brahma śāsanāt mayā āgatam sva bhavanam śiva lokam śivo sarva svāsthyam atīva āpa hi upadravaḥ sarva svāsthyam atīva āpa hi upadravaḥ sanatkumāraḥ uvāca iti uktvā jagantām nāthaḥ śayanam ca cakāra ha reme ramāpatiḥ tatra ramayā saḥ tayā mudā ramayā saḥ tayā mudā sā sādhvī vyatikramāt vitarkayāmāsa kaḥ tvam eva iti uvāca sā uvāca kaḥ vā tvam vada pu0 mām āśu bhuktā aham māyayā tvayā dūrīkṛtam yat satī tvam atha tvā vai śapāmi aham uvāca tulasī vacanam śrutvā hariḥ śāpa bhayena ca hāra līlayā brahman sva mūrti su manoharām tat dṛṣṭvā tulasī rūpam jñātvā viṣṇum tu cihnāt pātitratya parityāgāt kruddhā sā tam uvāca ha uvāca he viṣṇo te dayā na asti pāṣāṇa saṃdṛśam manaḥ pati dharmasya bhaṅgena mama svāmī hataḥ khalu pāṣāṇa sadṛśaḥ tvam ca dayā hīnaḥ yatas khalaḥ tasmāt pāṣāṇa rūpaḥ tvam mad śāpena bhava adhunā ye vadanti dayā sindhum tvā bhrāṃtāḥ te na saṃśayaḥ bhaktyā vinā aparā para arthe ca katham hataḥ uvāca iti uktā tulasī sā vai śaṃkhacūḍa priyā satī bhṛśam ruroda śoka ārtā vilalāpa bhṛśam muhur tatas tām rudatīm dṛṣṭvā saḥ viṣṇuḥ parameśvaraḥ sasmāra śaṃkaram devam yena saṃmohitam jagant tatas prādurbabhūva atha śaṃkaraḥ bhakta hariṇā praṇataḥ ca āsīt saṃnutaḥ vinayena saḥ hariṇā praṇataḥ ca āsīt saṃnutaḥ vinayena saḥ śoka ākulam harim dṛṣṭvā vilapatīm ca tad priyām nayena bodhayāmāsa tam tām tat anyathā katham syāt vai jātam tvayi tathā ca tat idam śarīram tyaktā ca divya deham vidhāya ca bhava bhava te iyam tanuḥ utsṛṣṭā nadī rūpā bhavet iha bhārate puṇya rūpā sā gaṇḍakī iti ca viśrutā kiyatkālam mahādevi deva pūjanam sādhane tulasī bhaviṣyati vareṇa mama ca vṛkṣa adhiṣṭhātṛ devī tvam vaikuṇṭhe divya rūpiṇī sārdham rahasi hariṇā nityam krīḍām kariṣyasi nadī adhiṣṭātṛ devī yā bhārate bahu puṇya dā upala patnī sā haryeśasya bhaviṣyasi hariḥ vai śaila rūpī ca gaṇḍakī tīra saṃnidhau saṃkariṣyati adhiṣṭhānam bhārate te śāpāt tatra koṭyāḥ ca tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭrāḥ bhayaṃkarāḥ tat chittvā kuhare cakram kariṣyanti tadīyakam śālagrāma śilā sā hi tad bhedāt ati puṇya dā bhaviṣyati bhāryā hīnaḥ bhavet saḥ api rogī syāt sapta janmasu bhāryā hīnaḥ bhavet saḥ api rogī syāt sapta janmasu śālagrāmaḥ ca tulasī śaṅkham ca ekatra eva hi yaḥ rakṣati mahā jñānī saḥ bhavet śrī hari priyaḥ uvāca iti uktvā śaṃkaraḥ tatra māhātmyam ūcivāḥ tadā śālagrāma śilāyāḥ ca tulasyāḥ bahu puṇya dam tatas ca antarhitaḥ bhūtvā modayitvā harim ca tām jagāma sva ālayam śambhuḥ śarma daḥ hi sadā satām iti śrutvā vacaḥ śambhoḥ prasannā tu tulasyaiḥ ca parityajya babhūva ca parityajya babhūva mune bhūt acyutaḥ saḥ api tad tīre puṇya daḥ nṛṇām tatra chidram bahuvidham mune jale patanti yāḥ tatra śilāḥ tāḥ tu ati puṇya dāḥ sthala sthā piṅgalā jñeyāḥ ca upatāpāya ca eva hi iti evam kathitam sarvam te praśna anusārāt caritam puṇya dam śambhoḥ sarva kāma pradam nṛṇām miśritam bhukti mukti pradam puṇyam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi tulasīśāpavarṇanam nāma ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca mama ayam tṛptaḥ asmi no tvattaḥ amṛtam pītvā yathā janaḥ brahman yat caritam tasya maheśasya mahātmanaḥ māyām āśritya saṅghīlām kurvataḥ bhakta moda dām uvāca jalaṃdhara vadham śrutvā vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ aprākṣīt imam eva artham brahma putram sunīśvaram sanatkumāraḥ provāca vyāsam satyavatī sutam su praśaṃsya maheśasya caritam maṅgalāyanam uvāca śṛṇu vyāsaiḥ maheśasya caritam maṅgalāyanam yathā andhakaḥ gāṇapatyam prāpa śambhoḥ parātmanaḥ kṛtvā parama saṃgrāmam tena pūrvam sunīśvaraiḥ prasādya tam maheśānam sattva bhāvāt punar punar māhātmyam adbhutam śambho māhātmyam etat vṛṣabhadhvajasya śrutvā muniḥ gandhavatī sutaḥ hi bhaktyā hi uvāca tam brahma sutam muni indram uvāca kaḥ hi andhakaḥ vai bhagavan muni īśaiḥ kasya anvaye vīryavataḥ pṛthivyām jātaḥ mahātmā balavān katham prāpa śambhoḥ parama tejasaḥ ca etat vacanam niśamya provāca saḥ brahma sutaḥ tadānīm maheśvara ūtiḥ parama āpta lakṣmīḥ saṃśrotu kāmam janakam śukasya bhakta kṛpā ākaraḥ asau kailāsāt śailam sutā gaṇa āḍhyaḥ vihartu kāmaḥ kila kāśikām vai sva śailāt nirjara cakravartī pu0 hi vidhāya tasyām cakre para ūtīḥ sukha dāḥ janānām tad rakṣakam bhairava nāma vīram kṛtvā samam śailajayā hi bahūḥ saḥ ekadā mandara nāmadheyam gataḥ nagam tad vara su prabhāvāt tatra api nānā gaṇa vīra mukhyaiḥ śivā sametaḥ vijahāra bhūri pūrve diśaḥ mandara śaila saṃsthā parākramasya tatas netra nimīlanam tu sā pārvatī narma yutam sa līlam pravāla hema abja dhṛta prabhābhyām kara ambujābhyām nimimīla netre harasya netreṣu nimīliteṣu bhoḥ lalāṭe kṣaṇa vahni taptaḥ vinirgataḥ bhūri jalasya binduḥ babhūva atha bhayaṃkaraḥ krodha paraḥ kṛtaghnaḥ virūpī jaṭilaḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ naretaraḥ vaikṛtikaḥ suromā nimīlya netrāṇi kṛtam ca karma bibheṣi sā asmāt dayite katham tvam gaurīharāt tat vacanam niśamya vihasyamānā pramumoca netre tasmin ghora rūpaḥ jātaḥ udhakārāt api netra hīnaḥ tādṛgvidham tam ca nirīkṣya bhūtam papraccha gaurī puruṣam maheśam haraḥ tat vacanam priyāyāḥ līlākaraḥ sṛṣṭi kṛtaḥ adharūpām līlākarāya atri jagat jananyā vihasya kiṃcid bhagavant uvāca bike hi adbhuta vṛtta kāre utpannaḥ eṣaḥ adbhuta caṇḍa vīryaḥ nimīlite cakṣuṣi mama bhavatyā sa sveda jaḥ meṃ dhaka nāmadheyaḥ tvam ca asya kartāsi ayathānurūpam tvayā āsa sakhyā dayayā gaṇebhyaḥ tvayā āsa sakhyā dayayā gaṇebhyaḥ sa rakṣitavyaḥ tvayi tam hi vā ekam vicārya buddha akaraṇīya māyeṃ bacaḥ niśamya kāruṇya bhāvāt sahitā sakhībhiḥ nānā prakāraiḥ bahubhiḥ cakāra rakṣām sva sutasya yadvat hiraṇyanetraḥ tu atha putra kāmaḥ sva jyeṣṭhaiḥ bandhoḥ tanaya pratānam saṃvīkṣya ca āsīt priyayā niyuktaḥ araṇyam āśritya tapaḥ cakāra asuraḥ tadā kaśyapa ja artham kāṣṭha upamaḥ asau jita roṣa doṣaḥ saṃdarśana artham tu maheśvarasya tuṣṭaḥ pinākī tapasā asya samyak vara pradānāya yayau dvijendraḥ namra śirāḥ uvāca stutyā ca natvā vividham girīśam tad artham etad vratam āsthitaḥ aham tam dehi deveśa suvīryaṃvatam yasmāt ca mad dhātuḥ ananta vīryāḥ prahlāda pūrve api pañca putrāḥ mama iha na asti iti gata anvayaḥ asya ham kaḥ māmakam rājyam idam bubhūṣet rājyam parasya sva balena hṛtvā bhuṃkte athavā svam pituḥ eva dṛṣṭam sa procyate putraḥ iha tu amutra putrī sa tena api bhavet pitā asau mama ātmajam tu andhaka nāmadheyam tvad tulya vīryam tu aparājitam ca vṛṇīṣva putram sakalam vihāya duḥkham pratīcchasva sutam tvam eva uvāca yathākrameṇa stotraiḥ anekaiḥ abhipūjya rudram tuṣṭaḥ sva rājyam gatavan mahātmā tatas tu putram giriśāt avāpya rasātalam caṇḍa parā tu imām dharitrīm anayat sva deśam daityaḥ vijitvā tridaśān aśeṣān tatas tu devaiḥ munibhiḥ ca siddhaiḥ sarva ātmakam yajña mayam karālam āśritya bapuḥ pradhānam ārādhitaḥ viṣṇuḥ ananta vīryaḥ ghoṇā prahāraiḥ vividhaiḥ dharitrīm pātāla talam praviśya tuṇḍena daityān śataśas vicūrṇya daṃṣṭrābhiḥ agryā mārtaṃḍa koṭi pratimena paścāt sudarśanena adbhuta caṇḍa tejāḥ hiraṇyanetrasya śiraḥ jvalantam ciccheda daityān ca dadāha duṣṭān tatas prahṛṣṭaḥ ditija indra rājaḥ tvam andhakam tatra sa ca abhyaṣiṃcat tatas dharitrīm dṛṣṭvā aṅkureṇa uddharataḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ bhūmim ca pātāla talāt mahātmā pupoṣa bhāgam tu antha pūrvakam tu devaiḥ samastaiḥ munibhiḥ prahṛṣṭaiḥ abhiṣṭutaḥ padmaiḥ munayaḥ ca sarve pare ca jīvāḥ sukhinaḥ babhūvuḥ sanatkumāraiḥ sarva jñaiḥ hate tasmin sura nuhi kim akārṣīt tatas tasya jyeṣṭha bhrātā mahā asuraḥ miti śrotum mama asti iha muni īśvaraḥ tat śrāvaya kṛpām kṛtvā brahma putra namaḥ astu te iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya vyāsasya sa munī manatkumāraḥ provāca smṛtvā śivaṃpada ambujam uvāca pu0 tapya anuṣā śucā tatas prajānām kadanam vidhātum kadana priyān nirdiḥ daśa asurān vīrān hari vaira priyaḥ hi saḥ atha te bhartṛ saṃdeśam ādāya asurāḥ deva prajānām kadanam vidadhuḥ kadana priyāḥ tatas viprakṛte loke asuraiḥ taiḥ duṣṭa mānasaiḥ divam devāḥ parityajya bhuvi ceruḥ alam hiraṇyakaśipuḥ bhrātuḥ saṃparetasya duḥkhitaḥ kṛtvā kara udaka ādīni tad kalatra ādi asāṃtvayat tatas saḥ daitya rāja indraḥ hi ajeyam ajarāma mum pāda aṅguṣṭha āśrita avaniḥ tiryañcam ūrdhvam adhas lokān atapat viṣvañc īritaḥ tena taptāḥ divam tyaktvā brahma lokam yayuḥ surāḥ dhātre vijñāpayāmāsuḥ tad tapas vikṛta ānanāḥ atha vijñāpitaḥ devaiḥ vyāsaiḥ taiḥ ātmabhūḥ vidhiḥ parītaḥ bhṛgu dakṣa ādyaiḥ yayau daitya īśvara āśramam pratāpya lokān akhilān tatas asau samāgatam padmabhavam dadarśa varam hi dātum tam uvāca dhātā varam vṛṇīṣva iti pitāmahaḥ upi niśamya vācam madhurām vidhātuḥ vacaḥ abravīt evam amūḍha buddhiḥ mama bhagavant prajā īśa pitāmahaiḥ abhūt na kadāpi deva śastra astra pāśa aśani śuṣka vṛkṣa giri indra toya agni ripu prahāraiḥ kim svarge dharaṇyām divase niśāyām na eva ūrdhvataḥ na api adhataḥ prajā īśaiḥ praṇamya viṣṇum manasā tam āha dayā anvitaḥ asau iti padmayoniḥ alam tapaḥ te paripūrṇa kāmaḥ samāḥ sahasrāṇi ca uttiṣṭha rājyam kuru dānavānām śrutvā giram tad su mukhaḥ babhūva tatas bhayāt indra mukhāḥ ca devāḥ pitāmaha ājñām samavāpya sarve upadrutāḥ daitya vareṇa jātāḥ kṣīrodadhim yatra hariḥ tu śete ārādhayāmāsuḥ atīva viṣṇum stutvā vacobhiḥ sukha dam hi matvā prasannam duḥkham svakīyam sakalam hi te te śrutvā tadīyam sakalam hi duḥkham tuṣṭaḥ rameśaḥ pradadau varān tu utthāya tasmāt śayanāt upendraḥ nija anu rūpaiḥ vividhaiḥ vacobhiḥ śrutvā rameśasya vacaḥ tura īśāḥ śakra ādikāḥ te nikhilā api tuṣṭāḥ yayuḥ sva dhāmāni hiraṇyanetra anujam ca matvā nihatam sunīśaiḥ loḍa yai luṅ ārṣaḥ ārṣī rūpam jaṭilam karālam daṃṣṭra āyudham tīkṣṇa nakham su nāsam saiṃham ca nāram su vidārita āsyam mārtaṃḍa koṭi pratimam su ghoram yugānta kālāgni sama prabhāvam jagat mayam kim vacobhiḥ astam khau asau api hi gacchati īśaḥ gataḥ asurāṇām nagarīm mahātmā tatra adbhuta vikramaḥ ca vabhañja tān tān asurān nṛsiṃhaḥ tatra adbhuta vikramaḥ ca vabhañja tān tān asurān nṛsiṃhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa daityaiḥ atula prabhāvaḥ te rebhire te hi tathā eva sarve siṃham ca tam sarva mayam nirīkṣya prahlāda nāmā uvāca rājānam ayam mṛgendrī jagat mayaḥ kim samupāgataḥ ca bhavantaḥ vīrāḥ virūpa bhrukuṭi īkṣaṇam tu tasya ājñayā daitya varāḥ tatas te grahītu kāmāḥ viviśuḥ mṛgendram kṣaṇena dagdhāḥ śalabhāḥ iva agnim rūpa abhi malāṣāt pravivikṣavaḥ vai daityeṣu dagdheṣu api yuddham saḥ mṛgādhipena śastraiḥ samayaiḥ ā akhilaiḥ tathā astraiḥ śakti aṣṭi pāśa aṅkuśa pāvaka āndyaiḥ bahūn ca kṛtvā bhujān śastra yutān nirīkṣya nṛ siṃha rūpam prayayau mṛgendram saṃyudhyamānam sahasā samantāt tathā akhila atraiḥ kṛtvā mahā daitya varaḥ nṛsiṃham kṣayam gataiḥ śūla dharaḥ abhyupāyāt tatas gṛhītaḥ sa mṛga adhipena bhujaiḥ anekaiḥ giri sāravadbhiḥ nidhāya jānau saḥ bhujāṃtareṣu nakha aṃkuraiḥ dānava marma bhidbhiḥ nakha aṅkuraiḥ dānava marma bhidbhiḥ nakha astra hṛd padmam asṛj vimiśram utpādya jīvāt vigataḥ kṣaṇena tyaktaḥ tadānīm sa tu kāṣṭhaiḥ bhūtaḥ punar punar varṇita sarva gātraḥ tasmin hate deva ripau prasannaḥ prahādam āmaṃtrya kṛta praṇāmam rājye abhiṣicya adbhuta vīrya viṣṇuḥ tatas prayātaḥ tatas ati hṛṣṭāḥ sakalāḥ sura īśāḥ praṇamya viṣṇum diśi vipraiḥ tasyām yayuḥ svadhā mānim pitāmaha ādyāḥ kṛta sva kāryam bhagaiḥ īḍyam pravarṇay tu andhaka janma rudrāt hiraṇyanetrasya mṛtiḥ varāhāt nṛsiṃhāt tad sahajasya nāśaḥ prahāda rājya āptiḥ iti prasaṅgāt bhava kṛt pralabdham śṛṇu tu idānīm dvija varyaiḥ mattaḥ ūdhaka prabhāvam bhava kṛt pralabdham hareṇa yuddham khalu tasya paścāt gaṇa ādhipatyam giriśaṃsya tasya iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe nāma tri ca pu0 adhyāyaḥ uvāca tatas hiraṇyākṣa sutaḥ kadācid saṃśrāvitaḥ narma yutaiḥ mada andhaiḥ taiḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ saṃprayutaḥ vihāre kim andhaiḥ rājyena te adya kāryam hiraṇyanetraḥ tu mūḍhaḥ kali priyam netra vihīnam eva yaḥ labdhavan tvām vikṛtam virūpam coraiḥ tapobhiḥ giriśam prasādya sa tvam na bhāgī khalu tāni vicārya budhyā svayam eva dīnaḥ tān śāṃtayitvā vividhaiḥ vacobhiḥ gataḥ tu araṇyam niśi nirjanam tu pādaḥ āhāra hīnaḥ niyama ūrdhva bāhuḥ karttum na śakyam hi sura asuraiḥ yat śastreṇa nikṛtya dehāt sa mantrakam pratyaham eva hutvā snāyu asthi śeṣam kuṇapam tadā asau kṣayam gatam śoṇitam eva sarvam yadā asya māṃsāni na santi de prakṣetu kāmaḥ tu hutāśanāya tatas saḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tridaśālayaiḥ janaiḥ su vismitaiḥ bhīti yutaiḥ samastaiḥ atha amaraiḥ śīghrataram prasāditaḥ vabhūva dhātā nutibhiḥ hi hi padmayoḥ tu vacaḥ niśamya provāca dīnaḥ praṇataḥ tu daityaḥ mama prahṛtam tu rājyam prahlāda mukhyāḥ mama santu bhṛtyāḥ mayāt ca śarvāt śrutvā vacaḥ tasya su dāruṇam tat su śaṃkitaḥ padmabhavaḥ tam āha uvāca daitya indraiḥ sarvam bhavitā tat etad vināśa hetum ca gṛhāṇa yasmāt na jātaḥ janiṣyate vā yaḥ na praviṣṭaḥ mukham antakasya atyanta dīrghaiḥ khalu jīvitam tu bhavādṛśāḥ sat puruṣāḥ tyajantu niśamya pitāmahāt prāha daityaḥ madhye khalu ratna bhūtā mama api nityam jananī iva kācid kāyena vācā manasā api agamyā nārī nṛ lokasya ca durlabhāya kāma yānasya mama astu na aṃśaḥ daitya indra bhāvāt bhagavant svayambhuḥ vākyam tat ākarṇya saḥ padmayoniḥ su vismitaḥ śaṃkara pāda padmam sasmāra saṃprāpya nideśa saṃpūjyamānaḥ muni siddha saṃghaiḥ saṃspṛṣṭa mātraḥ sa ca daitya rājaḥ sampūrṇa dehaḥ balavān babhūva saṃjāta netraḥ subhagaḥ babhūva hṛṣṭaḥ svam evam nagaram viveśa nāgān suparṇān vara rākṣasān ca gandharva yakṣān anugān anugān anugān anugān anugān anugān anugān anugān tu giri indra vṛkṣān samareṣu sarvān catuṣpadaḥ siṃha mukhān vijigye trailokyam a tat hi carācaram vai vaśam cakāra ātmani saṃniyojya su darśanāni nārī sahasrāṇi bahūni gatvā rasātale ca eva tathā dharāyām triviṣṭape yāḥ pramadāḥ surūpāḥ tābhiḥ yutaḥ anyeṣu sa parva teṣu rarāma ramyeṣu nadī taṭeṣu teṣu rarāma ramyeṣu nadī taṭeṣu krīḍāyamānaḥ sa tu madhya vartī tāsām praharṣāt atha dānava indraḥ tad pīta śiṣṭāni piban pravṛttaye divyāni ca anyāni divyāni tu phalāni mūlāni su gandhavanti saṃprāpya yānāni su vāhanāni mayena sṛṣṭāni gṛha uttamāni puṣpa ardha dhūpa anna vilepanaiḥ ca su śobhitāni adbhuta darśanaiḥ ca saṃkrīḍamānasya gatāni tasya varṣa ayutāni iha jānāti kiṃcid na śubham paratra yadā tu tatra nirīkṣya babhrāma saha sa vāsāya cakāra mohāt sa vāsāya cakāra mohāt śubham dṛḍham tatra puram saḥ kṛtvā mudā āsthitaḥ daityapatiḥ prabhāvāt niveśayāmāsa punar krameṇa atyadbhutam mandara harṣāt dutam mahā daitya patim sametya ūcuḥ yathādṛṣṭam atīva prītyā tathā andhakam vīra varam hi sarve yāna nimīlita akṣaḥ daitya indraiḥ kaścid muniḥ atra dṛṣṭaḥ rūpa anvitaḥ candra kalā ardha cūḍaḥ kaṭi sthale baddha gaja indra kṛttiḥ pu0 mahā gātraḥ kapāla mālā ābharaṇaḥ jaṭālaḥ sa śūla hastaḥ śara tūṇa dhārī mahā dhanuṣmān vivṛta akṣa sūtraḥ sarva āyudhaḥ rūkṣa karaḥ ca rakṣan sthiraḥ jarat go vṛṣabhaḥ ca śuklaḥ tasya upaviṣṭasya tapasvinaḥ api su cāru rūpā taruṇī manojñā nārī śubhā pārśva gatā mālya śubha upagūḍhā yena dṛṣṭena ca anyena kim atra kāryam mānyā maheśasya ca divya nārī bhāryām muneḥ puṇyavataḥ priyā sā yogyā hi draṣṭum bhavataḥ ca samyak ānā daitya indra su ratna bhoktaḥ uvāca śrutvā iti teṣām vacanāni tāni kāma āturaḥ ghūrṇita sarva gātraḥ muneḥ sakāśam duryodhana ādīn sahasā saḥ daityaḥ āsādya te tam munim aprameyam vṛhat ratam mantri varāḥ hi tasya muni īśaiḥ praṇamya tam daitya nideśam āduḥ ūcuḥ hiraṇyanetrasya sutaḥ mahātmā daitya adhirājaḥ andhaka nāmadheyaḥ nāthaḥ bhava kṛt nideśāt iha upaviṣṭaḥ adya vihāra śālī tad mantriṇaḥ vai vayam aṅga vīrāḥ te upakaṇṭham ca samāgatāḥ sma tad preṣitāḥ tvām yat uvāca śubhā daitya pateḥ muni indra kva idam śarīram tava bhasma digdham kapāla mālā ābharaṇam virūpam yat jāhnavī puṇyatamā kva ayam śaśī vā kuṇapa asthi khaṇḍam dīrgha mukhaḥ kva sarpaḥ kva saṃgamaḥ pīna payodharāyāḥ striyā tapaḥ kim kuruṣe vimūḍha ayuktam etat tvayi na anurūpam yasmāt aham ratna patiḥ triloke vimuca śastrāṇi mayā adya ca uktaḥ kuruṣva paścā tapaḥ eva śuddham ullaṅghya mad śāsanam apradhṛṣyam vimokṣyase sarvam idam śarīram satu adhikam duṣṭamatim pradhānaḥ maheśvaraḥ laukika bhāva śīlaḥ śṛṇu prabhāvam mama daitya nāthaiḥ nyāyyam na vaktum vacanam tvayā evam carāmi na mātaram tu ajñatamaḥ virūpaḥ amūlam etat mayi tu prasiddham su dustyajam sarvam idam mama asti bhāryā mama iyam taruṇā surūpā trailokya nāśāya kṛta pratijñam babhāṣire daitya patim pramattam praṇamya rājānam adīna sattvāḥ te tatra sarve jaya śabda pūrvam rudreṇa yat tat smita pūrvam uktam ūcuḥ ha mama ca śastrāṇi ca dāruṇāni yuddham kka vīrakaḥ vānara vakra tulyaḥ niśācaraḥ jarasā jarjara aṅgaḥ kāyam sva rūpaḥ kva ca mandabhāgyaḥ balam tvadīyam kva ca vīrudhaḥ vā śaktaḥ api ca tvam prayatasva yuddham kartum tadā hi ehi kuruṣva kiṃcid bhavādṛśām nāśa karam ca ghoram kva te śarīram mṛdu padma tulyam vicārya ca evam kuru rocate yat āha rājñ smayamānaḥ eva vivastu śūnyaiḥ bahubhiḥ pralāpaiḥ vacanam niśamya jajvāla roṣeṇa saḥ manda buddhiḥ ājya avasiktaḥ tu iva kṛṣṇavarmā satyam hitam tat kuṭilam su tīkṣṇam pracaṇḍa vāta anukṛtim ca kurvan gaṃtum ca tatra smara vāṇa viddhaḥ samudyataḥ abhūt viparīta daivaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddhakher̤e andhakagāṇatatyalābhopākhyāne dūtasaṃvādaḥ nāma catuścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca gataḥ tatas matta gaja indraiḥ ca snigdham yathā vīkṣya pataṃgu saṃjñaḥ ca kṛmiḥ div upetya babhūva kāma agni dagdha deha oṃdhakaḥ mahā daitya patiḥ saḥ mūḍhaḥ prapīḍyaḥ kaḥ tvam samupāgatā asi niśamya tadām sva matam sa tasmai cakāra yuddham saḥ tu vīrakeṇa muhūrtam āśvarya vat aprameyam saṃkhye jitaḥ vīratareṇa daityaḥ saṃkhye jitaḥ vīratareṇa daityaḥ tatas tu saṃgrāma śiraḥ vihāya kṣudh kṣāma kaṇṭhaḥ tṛṣitaḥ gataḥ abhūt cūrṇīkṛte khaḍga vare ca khinne palāyamānaḥ gata vidhiḥ saḥ cakruḥ tadā ājim saha vīrakeṇa prahlāda mukhyāḥ ditija pradhānāḥ lajjā aṃkuśa ākṛṣṭa dhiyaḥ babhruvuḥ su dāruṇāḥ śastra śataiḥ anekaiḥ śi tatra cakāra yuddham bālaḥ ca bāṇaḥ ca sahasrabāhuḥ bālaḥ ca bāṇaḥ ca sahasrabāhuḥ bhajiḥ kujambhaḥ tu atha śambaraḥ ca vṛtra ādayaḥ ca api atha vīryavantaḥ medaḥ vasā māṃsa supūya madhye tu bhayaṃkare śoṇita kardame tu bhagna tu daityaiḥ bhagavant pinākī vratam mahā pāśupatam su ghoram priye mayā yat kṛta pūrvam āsīt dākṣā tasmāt valam yat mama tat praṇaṣṭam matyaiḥ amartyasya yatas prapātaḥ sundari vai viśokāḥ mahat vanam puṇyatamam su ghoram hi śakyam tu sura asuraiḥ yat na tādṛśam varṣa sahasra mātram sā pārvatī mandara parvata sthā pratīkṣyamāṇā āgamanam bhavasya bhū pativratā śīla guṇa upapannā ekākinī nityam atho guhā antare duḥkha parā vabhūva saṃrakṣitā sā muta vīrakeṇa tatas saḥ daityaḥ vara dānam atta nidrāḥ rātriṃdivam pañca śatāni pañca kruddhaḥ sa sainyaḥ saha vīrakeṇa khadvaiḥ sa kutaiḥ saha bhidipāle gadā bhuśuṇḍibhiḥ atho prakāṇḍaiḥ ardha devī sakhībhiḥ sahitā ca viṣṇum sainyam ca mad vīra varasya sarve sa smārayāmāsa guhā antara sthā brahmā tathā saṃsmṛta mātraḥ eva strī rūpa dhārī bhagavant ca sarvaiḥ saha sainyakaiḥ ca strī rūpam āsthāya samāgatāḥ te bhūtvā striyaḥ te viviśuḥ tadānīm muni indra saṃghāḥ ca mahā anubhāvāḥ siddhāḥ ca nāgāḥ tu atha guhyakāḥ ca guhā antaram parvatarāja putryāḥ yasmāt su rājya āsana saṃsthitānām ataḥpure saṃgamanam viruddham sahasrāṇi saṃkhyāni api darśayatyaḥ darśayatyaḥ rūpāṇi divyāni mahā adbhutāni gauryai guhāyām tu sa vīrakāyai striyaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ girirāja kanyām bherī ca saṃgrāma jaya pradāḥ tu ghmātāḥ su śaṅkhāḥ mūrchā vihāya adbhutaiḥ caṇḍa vīryaḥ sa vīrakaḥ vai puratas sthitaḥ tu pragṛhya śastrāṇi mahā rathānām tebhiḥ eva śastraiḥ ditijam jaghāna brāhmī tatas daṇḍa karā viruddhā gaurī tadā krodha parīta cetāḥ nārāyaṇī śaṅkha gadā cakra dhanus dharā pūrita bāhu daṇḍā viniryayaḥ lāṅgala daṇḍa hastā vaiśvānarā śaktiḥ asaumya vakrā yāmyā ca su tīkṣṇa khaṅga udyata pāṇi ruyā vāraṇa pāśa hastā vinirgatā yuddham abhīpsamānā pracaṇḍa vāta prabhavā ca devīm kṣudhā vapuḥ tvam kuśa pāṇiḥ eva kalpānta vahni pratimām gadā ca pāṇau gṛhī tvā dhanada udbhavā ca yājñeśvarī tīkṣṇa mukhā virūpā nakha āyudhām nāga bhayaṃkarā ca etāḥ tathā anyāḥ śataśas hi devyaḥ su nirgatāḥ saṃkula yuddha bhūmim dṛṣṭvā ca tat sainyam ananta pāram vivarṇa varṇāḥ ca su vismitāḥ ca samākulāḥ saṃcakitāḥ bhayāt vai devyaḥ babhūvuḥ hṛd adīna sattvāḥ samādhāya mṛtyum atha ātmanaḥ ca nārībhiḥ anye vara dāna sattvāḥ ati adbhutam tatra cakāra yuddham gaurī tadānīm sahitā sakhībhiḥ senāpatim vīraka ghora vīryam hiraṇyanetra ātmajaḥ eva bhūpaḥ ca mahā vyūham aram sukarmā saṃbhāvya viṣṇum ca nirīkṣya yāmyām su dāruṇam tat vidhi mukha karāla vidhi sevayā asya tad kṛta bhagavant āgam kalpa anta ghora arka sahasra kānti kīrṇa ca vai kup kṛttivāsas praṇamya gaurī giriśam ca mūṃdarbhā saṃdarśayan bhartuḥ atīva śauryam gaurī prayuddham ca cakāra hṛṣṭā haraḥ tatas parvatarāja putrīm kaṇṭhe gṛhītvā tu guhām praviṣṭaḥ ramā sahasrāṇi visarjitāni gaurī ca sat māna śataiḥ prapūjya guhā mukhe vīrakam eva sthāpayan naḥ tatas na gaurīm giriśam ca dṛṣṭvā asura īśvaraḥ nīti vicakṣaṇaḥ hi ha tam tam dūtam vidha sāṃkhyam eva saḥ preṣayāmāsa śiva upakaṇṭham taiḥ taiḥ prahāraiḥ api jarjara aṅgaḥ tasmin raṇe deva gaṇa īritaiḥ yaḥ jagāda vākyam tu sa garvaiḥ praviśya śambhum praṇipatya mūrdhanā te kiṃcid asti vimuṃca nārīm taruṇām surūpām prāyas bhavān tāpasaḥ tat juṣasva kṣātam mayā yat kamanīyam antar muniḥ virodhavyaḥ iti tvām dhūrta hi tvām sanatkumāraḥ uvāca etat vacaḥ dūta mukhāt niśamya kapālamālī tam uvāca kopāt jvalan viṣādena mahān trinetraḥ satām gatiḥ duṣṭaiḥ uvāca harīra yātrā api kutas tu aśaktyāḥ kurvantu yat yat hitam tu teṣām mama api yat yat karaṇīyam asti tat tat kariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ atra etat vacaḥ tat vigaśaḥ api tasmāt śrutvā harāt vinirgatam eva hṛṣṭaḥ prāgāt tatas garjita huṃkṛtāni kurvan tatas daitya pateḥ sakāśam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe yuddhaprārambhabhūtasaṃvādavarṇanam nāma pañcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tasya uṅgita jñaḥ ca sa daitya rājaḥ gadām gṛhītvā tvaritaḥ sa sainyaḥ kṛtvā atha sa aṅge gila nāmadheyam su dāruṇam deva vairaiḥ abhedyam hi muditāḥ ca kecid śṛṅgāṇi śailasya ca bhānumanti tatas haraḥ saṃsmṛtavan sva sainyam samāhvayan kupitaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ bhūtāni ca anyāni su dāruṇāni devān sa sainyān saha viṣṇu mukhyān āhūta mātra anugaṇāḥ sa sainyāḥ rathaiḥ gajaiḥ vāji vṛṣaiḥ ca gobhiḥ uṣṭraiḥ kharaiḥ pakṣi varaiḥ ca siṃhaiḥ te sarve devāḥ saha bhūta saṃghaiḥ vyāghraiḥ mṛgaiḥ sūkara sārasaiḥ ca sa mīna matsyaiḥ śiśumāra mukhyaiḥ anyaiḥ ca nānāvidha jīva saṃghaiḥ viśīrṇa veśāḥ bhujaṃgamaiḥ preta śataiḥ piśācaiḥ divyaiḥ vimānaiḥ kamala ākaraiḥ ca nadīnadaiḥ parvata vāhanaiḥ ca samāgatāḥ prāñjalayaḥ praṇamya kapardinam tasthuḥ adīna sattvāḥ senāpatim vīrakam eva kṛtvā visṛjayāmāsa raṇāya devān viśrānta vāhān atha tān pināki yuddhe sthiram labdha jayam pradhānam saṃpreṣitāḥ te tu maheśvareṇa cakṣus yugānta pratimam ca yuddham maryāda hīnam sāgilena sarvaiḥ daitya indra sainyena sadā eva ghoram krodhāt nigīrṇāḥ tridaśāḥ tu saṃkhyāḥ tasmin kṣaṇe yudhyamānāḥ ca sarve brahma indra viṣṇu arka śaśāṅka mukhyāḥ āsan nigīrṇāḥ vighasena tena sainye nigīrṇaḥ asti tu vīrakaḥ hi vihāya saṃgrāma śiraḥ guhām tām praviśya śarvam praṇipatya mūrdhanā provāca duḥkha abhihataḥ smarārim suvīrakaḥ vāgamiravaḥ atha vṛttam tvā prāptaḥ pratibhaya manāḥ māruta gatiḥ svayam viṣṇuḥ devaḥ kanakakaśipum kaśyapa sutam budhyate bhāma ākhyam dinakara kara ākāra vapuṣā prahāsāt tad nānnām tadanum nihatam tena ca tamaḥ punar api mahā yuddham akarot raṇe daityaiḥ ssārdham pradhānaḥ yodhānām muni vara śatānām api mahān nivāsaḥ vidyānām śama dama mahā dhairya sahitaḥ sthitaḥ sajjam kṛtvā dhanuḥ aśani kalpān api śarān tatas niṣkrāntaḥ asau vighasa vadanāt vīraka muni gṛhītvā tat sarve sva balam atulam viṣṇu sahitaḥ yadā vidyā vīryāt punar api sa jīvān prakurute tadā baddha ānītaḥ paśuḥ iva gaṇaiḥ bhūtapataye nirgīrṇaḥ tena asau tripura ripuṇā ādānava guruḥ vinaṣṭe mad ra śakti uddhṛta karaiḥ pramattā eva etāḥ su dṛḍha kara tuḍaiḥ api khagaiḥ vṛkaiḥ nānā saṃgrāme kanakakaśipoḥ vaṃśa jana kaśviram yuddham kṛtvā hari hara mahā indraiḥ ca vijitaḥ praviṣṭe pātāle giri jaladhi rambhrāṇi api tathā tatas sainye kṣīṇe ditija vṛṣabha śva andhaka varaḥ devāḥ pu0 daiḥ parikṣīṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ tadanu girijā rudram atudat tathā vṛkṣaiḥ sapaiḥ aśani nivahaiḥ śastra paṭṭalaiḥ virūpaiḥ māyābhiḥ kapaṭa racanā śambara śataiḥ gāt pramatha patim āhūya matimān cakāra uyam rūpam vikṛta vadanam straiṇam ajitam karālam saṃśuṣkam bahu bhuja latā ākrāntaiḥ kupitaḥ viniṣkrāntaḥ karṇāt guṇa śirasi ca vidhṛtaḥ sthāṇu sadṛśaḥ adhas kāyaḥ śuṣkaḥ tapana kiraṇaiḥ jīrṇa tanumān alāsāraiḥ medhaiḥ pavana sahitaiḥ kvedita vapūḥ tathābhūtaḥ prāṇān tat api na jahau daitya vṛṣabhaḥ tadā tuṣṭaḥ śambhuḥ parama karuṇā vāriṃdhiḥ asau dadau tasmai prītyā gaṇapati padam tena vinutaḥ maya jaya giram procya sukhitāḥ haraḥ taiḥ taiḥ sārdham giri vara guhāyām pramuditaḥ visṛjya ekān aṃśān vividha balinā krīḍām giri vara sutām prāpya muditām tathā putram ghorāt vighasa vadanāt muktam anagham yuddha khaṇḍe andhakavadhopākhyāne aṃdhakayuddhavarṇanam nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tasmin mahati saṃgrāme dāruṇe loma harṣaṇe hukraḥ daityapatiḥ vidvāḥ bhakṣitaḥ tripurāriṇā iti śrutam samāsāt mama tat punar brūhi vistarāt kim cakāra mahā yogī jaṭhara sthaḥ pinākinaḥ na dadāha katham śambhoḥ śukram tam jaṭhara analaḥ kalpa anta dahanaḥ kālaḥ dīpta tejāḥ ca bhārgavaḥ viniṣkrāṃtaḥ katham dhīmān śambhoḥ jaṭhara tathā ārādhayāmāsa kiyatkālam saḥ bhārgavaḥ katham ārādhayāmāsa kiyatkālam sa bhārgavaḥ atha ca labdhavan vidyām tām mṛtyu śamanām parām kā sā vidyā parā tāta yayā mṛtyuḥ hi vāryate lebha indhakaḥ gāṇapatyam katham śūlāt vinirgataḥ devadevasya vai śambhoḥ muneḥ līlā vihāriṇaḥ etat sarvam aśeṣeṇa mahā dhī tāta kṛpāṃḥ kuru śiva līlā amṛtam tāta śṛṇvataḥ kathayasva mama brahmā uvāca iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā vyāsasya amita tejasaḥ sanatkumāraḥ bhava provāca smṛtvā śiva pada ambujam uvāca śṛṇu vyāsaiḥ mahābuddhe śiva līlā amṛtam param dhanyaḥ tvam śaiva mukhyaḥ asi mama ānanda karaḥ svatas jayaḥ śiva prabhāvāt abhavat pramathānām mune jayaḥ tat śrutvā āsīt viṣaṇṇaḥ hi mahā daitya undhaka asuraḥ katham syāt mama jayaḥ iti vicāraṇa paraḥ abhavat ha aṃjaliḥ nīti vittamaḥ hi tvad anugrahāt vidhūya tvad anugrahāt rakṣa rakṣa abhitas vipraiḥ pratrajya śaraṇa āgatān asurān śatrubhiḥ vīraiḥ arditān ca mṛtān api pramathaiḥ bhīma vikrāntaiḥ krāntān mṛtyu pramāthibhiḥ tān paśya huṃḍāndīn mad guṇān varān paśya huṃḍāndīn mad guṇān varān yaḥ pītvā kaṇadhūmam vai sahasram śaradām purā tvayā prāptā vasa vidyā tasyāḥ kālaḥ yam āgataḥ adya vidyā phalam tat te sarve paśyantu bhārgavaiḥ pramathāḥ asurān sarvān kṛpayā jīvayiṣyataḥ uvāca ittham andhaka vākyam saḥ nārībhiḥ prabalābhiḥ adūrāt śaṃkara anucarān śauriḥ bhūta pramatha guhyakān drāvayāmāsa tīkṣṇa ayaiḥ śaraiḥ śārṅga dhanus cyutaiḥ sva balam dṛṣṭvā sva balam dṛṣṭvā rudraiḥ uti amarṣaṇaḥ krodham cakāra su mahān anāda ca mahā ulbaṇam tat śrutvā śaṃkara gaṇāḥ vineduḥ yuyudhuḥ ca te varddhitāḥ śambhu tejasā pṛthagvidhāni ca ayukta śāstrāṇi pinākine pratyakṣaiḥ śamayāmāsa śūlapāṇiḥ avismitaḥ brahmāstrasya ca brahmāstram pu0 pūrṇa rudra su tejasā vidrāvite sva sainye tu śrī kṛṣṇaḥ ca param tapaḥ svam jvaram śītala ākhyam hi vyasṛjat vāruṇam mune vidrāvite kṛṣṇa sainye kṛṣṇasya māheśvara bala arditaḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ atha samākrandat māheśvara bala arditaḥ a labdhvā bhayam anyatra tuṣṭāva vṛṣabhadhvajam atha prasannaḥ bhagavant viṣṇu jvara nutaḥ haraḥ maheśvaram prāha śaraṇa āgata vatsalaḥ muc gātrebhyaḥ balena apākramat raṇāt kumbhāṇḍa kūpa karṇābhyām nānā astraiḥ ca samāhataḥ dudrāva balabhadraḥ api na tasthe api raṇe balī sahasram kāyānām pītvā toyam mahā arṇavāt garuḍaḥ nāśayati atha āvataiḥ megha arṇava ambuṣu atha kruddhaḥ maheśasya vāhanaḥ nijaghāna hāya ca janārdanam evam jāte caritram tu bhagavant devakī sutaḥ uvāca sārathim śīghram rudra teja ūti vismitaḥ he sūtaiḥ śṛṇumat vākyam ratham mama vāhaya drutama mahādeva samīpa sthaḥ yathā syām gaditum vacaḥ dārukaḥ sva guṇa agraṇī drutam tam vāhayāmāsa ratham rudra samīpatas atha vijñāpayāmāsa nataḥ bhūtvā kṛtāñjaliḥ vatsalam prāṇaḥ ātmā ca vikāraḥ tad samūhakaḥ bīja roha pravāhaḥ tu tvad māyā eṣā jagatprabho tad nibandham prapadya iha tvām aham parameśvaram līlayā eva svīkṛtaiḥ nirjara ādikān lokaśas nūnam vibharṣi haṃsi unmārgān svabhāvāt mala ātmānam ākāśam iva kevalam yu0 yayā saṃcakāsti hi ayam parama dṛś bhavān guṇena apihitaḥ api tvam guṇena eva guṇān vibho sva pradīpaḥ cakāsti tvam bhūmn giriśaiḥ śaṃkaraiḥ tvad pādau saḥ śocyaḥ hi ātma vañcakaḥ tvad ājñayā aham bhagavant bāṇa dos chettum āgataḥ tu atha eva śaptaḥ bāṇaḥ ayam garvitaḥ garva hāriṇā nivartasva raṇāt devaiḥ tvad śāpaḥ na vṛthak bhavet ājñām dehi prabho mama tvam bāṇasya bhuja kṛntane īśvaraḥ pratyuvāca prasanna ātmā kṛṣṇa stutyā maheśvaraḥ pratyuvāca prasanna ātmā kṛṣṇa stutyā maheśvaraḥ uvāca satyam uktam tvayā tātaiḥ mayā śaptaḥ hi syāt vāṇa bhuja kṛntanam atas tvam jṛmbhaṇa astreṇa mām jṛṃbhaya mad ājñayā tatas tvam kuru kārya svam yatheṣṭam ca sukhī bhava uvāca iti uktaḥ śaṃkareṇa atha śārṅgapāṇiḥ su vismitaḥ svaraṇa sthānam āgatya mumoda saḥ muni īśvaraḥ mohayitvā tu giriśam jṛmbhaṇa astreṇa jṛmbhitam bāṇasya pṛtanām śauriḥ jaghāna asi gaiḥ daṣṭibhiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe bāṇa amurarudrakṛṣṇādiyuddhavarṇanam nāma catuḥ paṃcāśattamaḥ arthaḥ adhyāyaḥ hariṇā samare hare hate vāṇa bale bāṇaḥ kim akārṣīt ca tat vada sūtaḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya vyāsasya amita tejasaḥ pratyuvāca prasanna ātmā brahma putraḥ muni īśvaraḥ uvāca śṛṇu vyāsaiḥ mahā prājñaiḥ kathām ca parama adbhutām kṛṣṇa śaṃkarayoḥ tātaiḥ loka līlā anusāriṇoḥ śayite līlayā rudre sa putre sa gaṇe sati vāṇaḥ vinirgataḥ yuddham kartum kṛṣṇena daitya rāj kumbhāṇḍa saṃgṛhītā vaḥ tatas cakāra yuddham atulam bali putraḥ mahā balaḥ dṛṣṭvā nija balam naṣṭam saḥ daitya indraḥ ati amarṣitaḥ cakāra yuddham atulam bali putraḥ mahā balaḥ mahā vīraḥ giriśa āpta mahā balaḥ uccais jagarja tatra ājī vāṇam tṛṇa upamam kakud doṣaṇī iti bhāṣya udāharaṇāt dās śabdasya napuṃsaka tvam pu0 yat bāṇa sainyam tat avaśiṣṭam muni īśvaraiḥ tena nādena mahatā dhanuḥ ṭaṅkāra jena hi dyāvābhūmyoḥ antaram vai vyāptam āsīt anantaram tān bāṇān bāṇāya kupitaḥ hariḥ karṇa antam tat vikṛṣya atha tīkṣṇān āśīviṣa upamān āyātaḥ tān nirīkṣya atha saṃ bāṇaḥ bali nandanaḥ tān eva ciccheda sva śaraiḥ sva dhanu cyutaiḥ punar jagarja saḥ vibhuḥ bāṇaḥ vairi gaṇa ardanaḥ tatra sum vṛṣṇayaḥ sarvam kṛṣṇa ātmānaḥ vicetasaḥ mahā śiva pada ambhojam cikṣepa nija sāyakān sa kṛṣṇāya ati śūrāya baleḥ sutaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ api tān asaṃprāptān acchinat sva śaraiḥ drutam śiva pada ambhojam amarāriḥ mahā balaḥ rāma ādayaḥ vṛṣṇayaḥ ca sva svam yoddhāram āhave nijaghnuḥ balinaḥ sarve kṛtvā krodham samākulāḥ cirataram tatra balinoḥ ca dvayoḥ api babhūva tumulam yuddham śṛṇvatām vismaya āvaham tasmin avasare tatra krodham kṛtvā ati pakṣirāj sarva pakṣa āghātaiḥ amardayat ca cukopa ati baleḥ putraḥ śaiva rāj ditija īśvaraḥ smṛtvā śiva īśvara cakra ambhoja sahasra bhujavān drutam mahat parākramam cakre vairiṇām dussaham saḥ vai cikṣepa yugapad vāṇān amitān tatra vīra hā pṛthak jaghāna ekena garuḍam kṛṣṇam ekena pattriṇā balam ekena ca mune parān api tathā balī kṛṣṇaḥ mahā vīra om viṣṇu rūpaḥ surāri hā cukopa ati raṇe tasmin jagarja ca maheśvaraḥ jaghāna bāṇam tarasā śārṅga nissṛta sat śaraiḥ ati tad valam atyu yugapad smṛta śaṃkaraḥ yugapad smṛta śaṃkaraḥ ciccheda tat dhanuḥ śīghram chattra ādi kamanā ākulaḥ hayāḥ ca pātayāmāsa hatvā tān sva śaraiḥ hariḥ bāṇaḥ api ca mahā vīraḥ jagarja ati prakupya ha kṛṣṇam jaghāna gadayā saḥ apatat dharaṇī tale utthāya āram tatas kṛṣṇaḥ yuyudhe tena śatruṇā babhūva su mahān raṇaḥ evam dvayoḥ ciram kālam babhūva su mahān raṇaḥ śiva rūpaḥ hariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ saḥ ca śaiva uttamaḥ balī kṛṣṇaḥ atha kṛtvā samaram ciram bāṇena vīryavān ciram bāṇena vīryavān śiva ājñayā muni īśvaraḥ hā mama chettam samudyataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vīra tvam āpannaḥ tadā rudraḥ samutthitaḥ uvāca bhagavant devakīputraiḥ yat ājñaptam mayā purā tat kṛtam ca tvayā māḥ bāṇasya mad ājñā kāriṇā sadā bāṇasya śiraḥ chidhi saṃhara sva sudarśanam mad ājñayā cakram idam amogham majjane sadā dattam mayā purā tubhyam a nivārya raṇe te cakram jayam ca govindaiḥ nivarta svaraṇāt tatas dadhīce rāvaṇe vīre tārakā ādi pureṣu api vinā mad ājñām lakṣmīśa rathāṅgam na amucaḥ tvam tu yogi īśvaraḥ sākṣāt paramātmā janārdanaiḥ vicāryatām sva manasā sarva bhūta hite rataḥ varam asya mayā dattam na mṛtyuḥ bhayam asti vai tad anujñāpyaḥ sa gaṇaḥ sva putram sva ālayam yayau uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ śambhoḥ saṃhṛtya ca sudarśanam akṣata aṅgaḥ tu vijayī tad kṛṣṇā antaḥpuram yayau aniruddham samāśvāsya sahitam punar jagrāha ratna saṃghātam bāṇadattam anekaśas tad sakhīm citralekhām ca gṛhītvā para yoginīm prasannaḥ abhūt tatas kṛṣṇaḥ kṛta kāryaḥ śiva ājñayā hṛdā praṇamya giriśam āmantrya ca baleḥ sutam parivāra sametaḥ tu jagāma sva purīm hariḥ pathini jitvā ca varu raṇam viruddham tam anekadhā ca purīm prāptaḥ samutsavam amanvitaḥ visarjayitvā garuḍam sakhīn vīkṣya upahasya ca dvārakāyām tatas dṛṣṭvā kāma cārī cacāra ha iti hi śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe bāṇabhujakṛta nagarvāpahāravarṇanam nāma pañcapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nārada uvāca kṛṣṇe gate dvārakāyām aniruddhena bhāryayā tatas bāṇaḥ tattvam vada mahā mune tatas maniruddhena bhāryayā duḥkhitaḥ abhūt tatas bāṇaḥ sva ajñānam saṃsmaran hṛdā tatas nandī bāṇam provāca duḥkhitam samanvitam uvāca bāṇaiḥ śaṃkara sat bhaktaiḥ mā anutāpam kuruṣva bhoḥ bhakta anukampī śambhuvai bhakta vatsala nāmadhṛk ca yat jātam tat jātam iti cetasā manyasva bhakta śārdūlaiḥ śivam smara punar punar punar tāṇḍavam mukhyam pratyālīḍha ādi śobhitam sthānakaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ ālīḍha pramukhaiḥ api mukhavāda sahasrāṇi bhrū kṣepa sahitāni api śiraḥ kampa sahasrāṇi prāpta anīkaḥ sahasraśas vārīḥ ca vividha ākārāḥ darśayitvā śanais śanais tathā śoṇita dhārābhiḥ siñcayitvā mahī talam prasādayāmāsa mahā bhaktaḥ śūlinam candra śekharam bāṇa asuraḥ mahā bhaktaḥ vismṛta ātma gatiḥ mamaḥ tatas nṛtyam mahat kṛtvā bhagavant bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca bāgam saṃhṛṣṭaḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ śambho daitya indreṇa tadā mune bāṇena saṃvṛṇītaḥ abhūiṃraiḥ tu vraṇa ropaṇe yuddhasya tat patyam atha akṣayam uṣā putrasya rājyam tu tasmin śoṇitaka āhvaye nirvaira tā ca vibudhaiḥ viṣṇunā ca viśeṣataḥ na punar aidaitya tā duṣṭā rajasā tamasā mune sadā suraḥ premṇā anayanaḥ rudram tuṣṭāva su kṛta añjaliḥ mahā akhila īśvaraḥ brahmāṇḍa tanuḥ ugra īśaḥ virāj sarva anvitaḥ paraḥ nābhiḥ nabhaḥ agniḥ vadanam ambu retaḥ diśaḥ śrutiḥ dyauḥ śīrṣa te manaśū andraḥ te prabho jaṭharam vidhiḥ prajāpatiḥ visargaḥ ca hi hṛdayam te auṣadhayaḥ nāthaiḥ keśāḥ jala mucaḥ tava guṇāḥ trayaḥ tri netrāṇi sarva ātmā puruṣaḥ bhavān brāhmaṇam te mukham prāhuḥ bāhum kṣatriyam eva ca yaḥ tvā visṛjate martyaḥ ātmānam priyam īśvaram viparyaya indriya artha arthaiḥ viṣam atti amṛtam tyajan vibudhāḥ munayaḥ vā amala āśayāḥ sarva ātmanā prapannāḥ tvā śaṃkaram priyam īśvaram sanatkumāraḥ uvāca iti uktvā bali putraḥ tu virarāma śara asuraḥ prema praphullita aṅgaḥ ca praṇamya saḥ maheśvaram iti śrutvā sva bhaktasya bāṇasya bhagavant bhavaḥ labhiṣyasi iti uktvā tatra eva antaradhīyata śambhoḥ prasādena mahākāla tvam āgataḥ rudrasya anucaraḥ bāṇaḥ mahā pramuditaḥ abhavat iti kila śara nāmnā śaṃkarasya api vṛttam sakala guru janānām saṃ mahā bhāga śūlapāṇeḥ kathitam iha variṣṭam śrotra ramyaiḥ vacobhiḥ sakala bhuvana madhye krīḍamānasya nityam ma0 yuddha khaṇḍe bāṇāsuragaṇapatvaprāptivarṇanam nāma ṣaṭpaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanatkumāraḥ uvāca śṛṇu vyāsaiḥ mahā premṇā caritam śaśimau yathā avadhī triśūleṇa dānava indram gaja asuram dānava nihate devyā samare mahiṣa asure devānām ca hita arthāya purā devā sukham yayuḥ tatāpa paramam tapaḥ avadhyaḥ aham bhaviṣyāmi strīpuṃsaiḥ kāma nirjitaiḥ saṃvicārya eti manasā abhūt tapas rata mānasaḥ tepe himavat roṇyām tapaḥ parama dāruṇam ūrdhvabāhuḥ nabhas dṛṣṭiḥ pāda aṅguṣṭha āśrita avaniḥ jaṭā bhāraiḥ saḥ vai reje pralaya arkaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ samudbhavāt nipetuḥ sa grahāḥ tārāḥ jajjvaluḥ ca diśaḥ daśa tena taptāḥ surāḥ sarve divam tyaktvā sa vāsavāḥ brahma lokam yayuḥ vijñāpayāmā bhūḥ mam tasya ca anyān jīvayitum kṛpā lokāḥ naṃkṣyati anyathā hi satyam satyam bruvāmahe iti vijñāpitaḥ devaiḥ vāsava ādyaiḥ saḥ ātmabhūḥ brahmā yayau daitya vara āśramam brahmā yayau daitya vara āśramam tapantam tapasā lokān yathā abhra apihitam divi vilakṣya vismitaḥ prāha vihasan sṛṣṭi kārakaḥ uvāca māhiṣe tapas siddhaḥ asi māhiṣe prāptaḥ aham vara daḥ tāta varam vṛṇu yathepsitam uvāca utthāya utthāya daitya indra īkṣamāṇaḥ dṛśā vibhum rāḥ gadgadayā prītaḥ agṛṇāt devam sa māhiṣiḥ uvāca namaḥ te devadeveśa yadi dāsyasi mama varam avadhyaḥ aham bhaveyam vai strīpuṃsaiḥ kāmani ajeyaḥ deva ādibhiḥ sadā mahā balaḥ mahā vīryaḥ ajeyaḥ deva ādibhiḥ sadā sarveṣām lokapālānām nikhila ddhi subhuj vibho uvāca evam vṛtaḥ śa tat vijitya diśaḥ savām lokān ca trīn mahā asuraḥ deva asura manuṣya indrān gandharva garuḍa uragān ityādīn nikhilān jitvā vaśa mānī mahā indra bhavanam sākṣāt nirmitam viśva reme abhivaṃdya antri yugaḥ sura ādibhiḥ pratāpitaiḥ ūrjita caṇḍa śāsanaḥ tatas kāle vyatīte pāpa buddhiḥ abhūt tatas mahiṣa asura putraḥ asau saṃcikkeśa dvijān varān tāpasān nitarām pṛthvyām dānavaḥ sura mardanaḥ surān narān ca pramathān sarvān cikkeśa durmatiḥ dharma anvitān viśeṣeṇa pūrva vairam anusmaran ekasmin samaye tāta dānavaḥ asau mahā balaḥ agaccha hi vai śaṃkarasya gajāmuraḥ hi putraḥ asau yadā puryām samāgataḥ pramathan pramathān sarvān nija vīrya mada uddhataḥ tasmin avasare devāḥ śaka ādyāḥ tad parājitāḥ śivasya śaraṇam jagmu ādarāt nyavedayan dānavasya tasya kāśau samāgamam keśa ādhikyam tatratyānām tad nāthānām viśeṣataḥ ūcuḥ devadevaiḥ mahādevaiḥ te gataḥ asuraḥ kaṣṭam datte tvad janānām tam jahi tvam kṛpā nidhe yatra yatra dharāyām ca caraṇam pramiṇoti hi yasya dos daṇḍa ghātena cūrṇīsyuḥ ca śiloccayāḥ yasya mauli ja saṃgharṣāt vanāḥ vyom tyajanti api nīlimānam na ca adya api jaghuḥ tad keśa saṅga jam satvaram satvaram samabhyeti saḥ yam dussaha dānavaḥ tatra ājagāma soram tad badha kāmanayā haraḥ āgatam tam samālokya śaṃkaṭaiḥ bhakta vatsalam triśūla hastam garjatam jagarja saḥ gaja asuraḥ tatas tayoḥ mahān āsīt samaraḥ dāruṇaḥ adbhutaḥ nānā astra śastra sampātaiḥ vīra ārāvam prakurvatoḥ bāṇaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ dānava ghātinam atha rudraḥ raudra tanuḥ sva śaraiḥ ati dāruṇaiḥ tad śarān cicchide pūrṇam aprāptaḥ tilaśas mune tatas gaja asuraḥ maheśāna tripurāṃtaka sarvagaiḥ kiṃcid vijñaptum icchāmi tat śṛṇuṣva kṛpā karaiḥ satyam bravīmi na asatyam mṛtyuṃjayaiḥ vicāraya yu0 vikatthate iti śeṣaḥ yaḥ vandyaḥ viśvasya upari saṃsthitaḥ kālena sarvaiḥ martavyam śreyase mṛtyuḥ īdṛśaḥ sanatkumāraḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya śaṃkaraḥ karuṇā tva indraḥ gaja asuraḥ asuraḥ gaja asuraḥ uvāca yadi prasannaḥ digvāsaḥ tadā nityam vasāna mama imām kṛttim maheśāna tu atriśūla anipāvitām pramāṇām sukha sparśā raṇa aṅgaṇa paṇīkṛtām darśanīyām mahā divyām sarvadā eva sukha āvahām iṣṭa gandhiḥ sadā eva astu sadā eva astu ati komalā eva nirmalā ca astu sadā eva astu ati maṇḍanām mahā tapas nala jvālām prāpya api su ciram vibho na dagdhā kṛttiḥ eṣā mama puṇya gandha nidheḥ tatas yadi puṇyavatī na eṣā mama kṛtti diś ambaraiḥ tadā tvad aṅga saṅgaḥ usyāḥ katham jātaḥ raṇa aṅgaṇe anyam ca me varam dehi yadi tuṣṭaḥ asim śaṃkaraiḥ astu vatsalaḥ tathā iti uvācam su prītaḥ maṃhiṣa asura jam punar provāca prīta ātmā dānavam tam gaja asuram punar provāca prīta ātmā dānavam tam gaja asuram bhakta priyaḥ maheśānaḥ bhakti nirmala mānasam uvāca mama liṅgam te kṣetre asmin mukti sādhane mama liṅgam bhavatu atra sarveṣām mukti dāyakam kṛttivāseśvaram nāma mahāpātaka nāśanam sunīśvaraiḥ harṣam āpuḥ janāḥ sarve kāśi sthāḥ pramathāḥ tathā hari brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ harṣa nirbhara mānasāḥ yaśasyam āyuṣyam dhana dhānya pravardhanam yaśasyam āyuṣyam dhana dhānya pravardhanam yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt prītyā śrāvayet vā śuci vrataḥ saḥ bhuktvā ca mahā saukhyam labhetām bhūyas te param sukham iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām
